### [1] [Escaping Mode Collapse in LLM Generation via Geometric Regulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00435)
*Xin Du,Kumiko Tanaka-Ishii*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文从动力系统视角将生成模型中的模式坍塌（mode collapse）重新解释为由几何坍塌（geometric collapse）导致的表示空间低维受限，并据此提出强化模式调控（Reinforced Mode Regulation, RMR），一种在线低秩阻尼干预Transformer值缓存（value cache）的轻量方法。实验表明，RMR能在极低熵率下维持稳定高质量生成，显著优于标准解码方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本生成中的模式坍塌长期存在且难以消除，现有方法多依赖符号约束或概率解码启发式。作者试图从动力系统（dynamical systems）视角揭示模式坍塌的本质机制，证明其并非纯词元级现象，从而提出更根本的解决方案。

Method: 将模式坍塌重新解释为几何坍塌，即生成过程中模型内部轨迹（internal trajectory）被限制在表示空间（representation space）的低维区域。据此提出强化模式调控（RMR），通过对Transformer值缓存进行在线低秩阻尼（low-rank damping）干预，抑制占主导的自强化方向（self-reinforcing directions）。

Result: 在多个大型语言模型上，RMR显著减少了模式坍塌，能够在极低熵率（0.8 nats/step）下实现稳定高质量生成，而标准解码方法通常在接近2.0 nats/step时发生坍塌。

Conclusion: 模式坍塌本质上是表示空间的几何受限问题，非词元级现象，因此无法被符号约束或纯概率解码启发式可靠解决。RMR作为一种轻量在线干预手段，能有效克服该问题。

Abstract: Mode collapse is a persistent challenge in generative modeling and appears in autoregressive text generation as behaviors ranging from explicit looping to gradual loss of diversity and premature trajectory convergence. We take a dynamical-systems view and reinterpret mode collapse as reduced state-space accessibility caused by *geometric collapse*: during generation, the model's internal trajectory becomes confined to a low-dimensional region of its representation space. This implies mode collapse is not purely a token-level phenomenon and cannot be reliably solved by symbolic constraints or probability-only decoding heuristics. Guided by this perspective, we propose *Reinforced Mode Regulation* (RMR), a lightweight, online state-space intervention that regulates dominant self-reinforcing directions in the Transformer value cache (implemented as low-rank damping). Across multiple large language models, RMR substantially reduces mode collapse and enables stable, high-quality generation at extremely low entropy rates (down to 0.8 nats/step), whereas standard decoding typically collapses near 2.0 nats/step.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Demonstration of a fermion Quadrupling Condensate via Quantum Monte Carlo Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00137)
*Alexandru Golic,Egor Babaev,Johan Carlström*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过设计一个具有关联跳跃（correlated hopping）的微观费米子模型，显著缓解了费米子符号问题（fermionic sign problem），并利用大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）模拟首次提供了费米子四重态凝聚（fermion-quadrupling condensate）的直接数值证据，表明该类超越BCS平均场描述的非传统有序态在超冷原子气体中具有实验可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索费米子体系中是否存在配对外的新型有序态，特别是费米子四重态凝聚（如电荷4e超导体和电荷0反向流凝聚态），这类超越标准BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer）框架的奇异态由于强关联效应和费米子符号问题，在微观层面极难进行数值研究。

Method: 提出一个包含关联跳跃项的微观费米子模型，该模型能显著缓解费米子符号问题，从而支持严格的基于蒙特卡洛方法的数值分析。随后在大规模模拟框架下进行系统性计算。

Result: 大规模模拟结果表明，该模型存在费米子四重态凝聚（fermion-quadrupling condensate），且其转变温度（transition temperature）与跳跃能标（hopping energy scale）相当，直接提供了微观体系中四次费米子有序（quartic fermionic order）的数值证据。

Conclusion: 研究结论指出，费米子四重态凝聚态不仅是微观模型中可证实的理论相，而且在超冷原子气体（ultracold atomic gases）中具有实验可及性，为未来实验探索此类奇异量子态提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Fermionic condensation typically occurs via pairing. In recent decades, however, a fundamental question has emerged: whether alternative forms of order exist, such as condensates of fermion quadruplets. These states--including ``charge-4e" superconductors and ``charge-0" counterflow condensates--lie beyond the standard Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer framework, and require strong fluctuations and correlation effects that invalidate the BCS mean-field description. This makes the problem notoriously difficult to study numerically at a microscopic level, as it involves both strong interactions and the fermionic sign problem. Here, we present a microscopic fermionic model featuring correlated hopping that significantly mitigates the sign problem, enabling rigorous Monte-Carlo-based analysis. Using large-scale simulations, we demonstrate the existence of a fermion-quadrupling condensate with a transition temperature comparable to the hopping energy scale. These results provide direct numerical evidence for quartic fermionic order in a microscopic system and suggest that these exotic states are also experimentally accessible in ultracold atomic gases.

</details>


### [3] [Signatures of time-reversal-symmetry breaking in multiband 2H-TaS2 revealed by zero-field Josephson nonreciprocity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00477)
*Daniel Margineda,David Caldevilla-Asenjo,Yuriy Yerin,Covadonga Álvarez-García,Andrei Mazanik,Maxim Ilyn,Celia Rogero,Luis E. Hueso,F. Sebastian Bergeret,Marco Gobbi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在非中心对称的2H-TaS2/2H-NbSe2范德华结中观察到零场约瑟夫森二极管效应，并通过多能带超导相结构的建模，证明该效应源于内禀的时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal-symmetry breaking），为各向同性自旋单态超导体中的非常规超导性提供了互补证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自发破缺时间反演对称性的超导体具有复杂序参量，被视为非常规超导性的标志。然而，在标称各向同性的自旋单态配对（spin-singlet pairing）超导体中是否也能出现这种对称性破缺，仍然是一个未解决的问题。

Method: 实验上制备了非中心对称的2H-TaS2/2H-NbSe2范德华结，测量了零场约瑟夫森二极管效应；利用对称性控制和分子插层控制器件进行对比检验；通过正常态霍尔输运测量和基于约瑟夫森框架的建模，引入能带间散射（interband scattering）作为锁相机制来解释非互易响应。

Result: 零场约瑟夫森二极管效率与超流振幅、TaS2厚度或正常态电阻无系统相关性，排除了简单的外在或界面机制；对称性控制和分子插层器件中非互易响应消失或显著减弱；正常态霍尔输运呈现与多能带关联电子态一致的非线性响应；建模表明能带间散射产生内禀反常相位差和非正弦不对称电流-相位关系（current-phase relation），导致零场整流。

Conclusion: 零场约瑟夫森非互易性与非线性霍尔输运共同为2H-TaS2中的多能带超导相结构提供了互补证据，与内禀的时间反演对称性破缺一致。

Abstract: Superconductors that spontaneously break time-reversal symmetry host complex order parameters and are widely regarded as a hallmark of unconventional superconductivity. Whether such symmetry breaking can also arise in superconductors with nominally isotropic spin-singlet pairing remains an open question. Here we report a zero-field Josephson diode effect in noncentrosymmetric 2H-TaS2/2H-NbSe2 van der Waals junctions. The diode efficiency shows no systematic correlation with supercurrent amplitude, TaS2 thickness, or normal-state resistance, arguing against simple extrinsic, purely interfacial, or transparency-driven mechanisms. Time-reversal-symmetric scenarios are further tested using symmetry-controlled and molecule-intercalated control devices, in which the nonreciprocal response is absent or strongly reduced. Normal-state Hall transport in TaS2 exhibits a nonlinear response consistent with multiband correlated electronic states. Within a Josephson framework, our modelling shows that interband scattering acts as a phase-locking mechanism generating an intrinsic anomalous phase difference and a nonsinusoidal asymmetric current-phase relation, leading to finite zero-field rectification. Together, zero-field Josephson nonreciprocity and nonlinear Hall transport provide complementary evidence for a multiband superconducting phase structure in 2H-TaS2, consistent with intrinsic time-reversal-symmetry breaking.

</details>


### [4] [Long range proximity effects in planar structures involving the halfmetal ferromagnet La0.7Sr0.3MnO3 and Pt interlayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00577)
*Junxiang Yao,Julian van Doorn,Mariona Cabero,Jan Aarts*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文实验性研究了具有铁磁弱连接的超导结中三线态超流的输运行为，重点关注La0.7Sr0.3MnO3（LSMO）纳米条约瑟夫森结的临界电流与条长、条宽的关系，并探索Pt中间层对三线态产生机制的影响。研究发现所有结均表现出强超流，但缺乏简单系统规律；引入Pt中间层后，在2 μm电极间距下实现了清晰的超导转变和零电阻态，表明更大距离的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解半金属铁磁体（halfmetallic ferromagnet）中完全自旋极化超流（fully spin-polarized supercurrent）的输运机制，探究三线态（triplet）配对在铁磁弱连接超导结中的产生条件与传输距离限制。

Method: 采用平面La0.7Sr0.3MnO3（LSMO）纳米条约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction），以NbTi为超导接触电极，系统测量临界电流（critical current, Ic）随纳米条长度和宽度的变化。为探究三线态产生机制，在LSMO/NbTi界面引入Pt中间层，制备NbTi/Pt电极结构，测试不同电极间距下的输运特性。

Result: 所有结均表现出强超流，但未观察到临界电流随结几何参数变化的简单系统性规律。引入Pt中间层后，电极间距达2 μm时仍出现尖锐的超导转变和零电阻态，且存在实现更大间距的迹象。

Conclusion: 现有制备工艺对某些关键参数的控制尚不充分，导致超流行为缺乏简单规律；Pt中间层可有效促进LSMO/NbTi界面处的三线态产生，显著提升超流传输距离。

Abstract: Over the last decade, there has been steady research on superconducting junctions with a ferromagnet as the weak link, and where triplet correlations can transport supercurrents over a substantial distances. Of particular interest are halfmetallic ferromagnets, in which only one spin band is present, so that, presumably, the induced supercurrent is fully spin-polarized. We have earlier reported on a study of triplet transport in planar La0.7Sr0.3MnO3(LSMO) nanostrip Josephson junctions with NbTi superconducting contacts, where we found high values for the supercurrents, and large junction lengths (up to 1.3 μm). Here, we extend that work by studying the dependence of the critical current Ic on the length of the nanostrip between the contacts and the width of the strip. All junctions show strong supercurrents, but we do not observe simple systematics. Apparently, the fabrication process does not allow sufficient control over some of its parameters. To gain more insight in the mechanism for triplet generation at the LSMO/NbTi interface, we also studied the effect of Pt as an interlayer between the LSMO and the NbTi. For this, we etched a NbTi/Pt electrode structure on a full film of LSMO. The results are highly promising, showing sharp superconducting transitions and zero-resistance states being reached at an electrode distance of 2 μm, with indications that larger distances should be feasible.

</details>


### [5] [Superconducting diode effect in correlated electron systems by nonreciprocal magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00601)
*Kyohei Nakamura,Youichi Yanase*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过Rashba-Zeeman-Hubbard模型结合Dyson-Gor'kov方程和涨落交换近似，发现电子关联会抑制传统超导二极管效应（SDE），并揭示了一种新的关联驱动机制：超电流非互易地诱导反铁磁序，从而实现完美二极管效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应（SDE）已在强关联电子体系和量子临界点附近被观察到，暗示存在超越弱耦合理论的新机制，但该机制的物理起源尚不明确，亟需理论阐明。

Method: 采用Rashba-Zeeman-Hubbard模型描述反铁磁量子临界区域中的d波超导，利用Dyson-Gor'kov方程结合涨落交换近似（fluctuation exchange approximation）进行理论计算。

Result: 电子关联抑制了由退配对电流（depairing currents）引起的传统本征SDE；超电流非互易地诱导反铁磁序，该反铁磁序从根本上决定了临界电流（critical current）并实现完美二极管效率。

Conclusion: 揭示了一种先前未被认识的关联驱动超导二极管效应机制，将强关联超导体确立为研究超导二极管物理的平台。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE), characterized by a nonreciprocal critical current in superconductors, has recently been observed in strongly correlated electron systems and near quantum criticality, pointing to unconventional mechanisms beyond weak-coupling theories. Here we investigate the SDE in the Rashba-Zeeman-Hubbard model, which captures $d$-wave superconductivity in an antiferromagnetic quantum critical regime, using the Dyson-Gor'kov equation with the fluctuation exchange approximation. We show that electron correlations suppress the conventional intrinsic SDE arising from depairing currents. More importantly, a supercurrent nonreciprocally induces antiferromagnetic order, which fundamentally governs the critical current and enables perfect diode efficiency. Our results reveal a previously unrecognized correlation-driven mechanism of the SDE and establish strongly correlated superconductors as a platform for superconducting diode physics.

</details>

### [6] [Insights into the electrorheological and electrohydrodynamic regimes in electrically driven emulsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00188)
*Majid Bahraminasr,Anand Yethiraj*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种唯象模型，将油包油乳液的电流变（ER）响应拟合为经典屈服应力流体，在重标度后坍塌为一条主曲线，屈服应力近似随 $E^2$ 增长。宏观小振幅振荡剪切（SAOS）流变学与基于差分动态显微镜（DDM）的被动微流变学结果高度一致，表明ER行为的尺度无关性。在电流体动力学（EHD） regime 中，乳液在稳态剪切与电场共同作用下形成交替的富液滴与贫液滴带状结构，并利用 Jensen–Shannon 散度分析了这些带的结构记忆衰退与统计独立性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作发现油包油乳液在频率依赖电场下存在高频电流变（ER） regime 与低频电流体动力学（EHD） regime，本研究旨在进一步刻画ER regime 的本构行为，验证其是否服从经典屈服应力流体模型，并探究ER行为在宏观与微观尺度下的一致性，同时揭示EHD regime中电场与剪切共同诱导的带状结构动力学。

Method: 采用唯象模型将ER regime下的流变数据拟合为经典屈服应力流体，并通过重标度（rescaling）得到主曲线（master curve）。宏观方面使用小振幅振荡剪切（SAOS）流变学测量，微观方面采用差分动态显微镜（DDM）进行被动微流变学（passive microrheology）测量。在EHD regime中，通过施加稳态剪切和电场，观测带状结构的形成，并使用 Jensen–Shannon 散度（Jensen–Shannon divergence）分析径向强度剖面（radial intensity profiles），以量化结构记忆与统计独立性。

Result: ER regime的流变数据在重标度后坍塌为一条主曲线，屈服应力近似随电场强度的平方（$E^2$）增长。SAOS流变学与DDM微流变学结果高度吻合，表明ER行为在宏观与微观尺度上一致，且SAOS测量不会导致样品重构。在EHD regime中，乳液在电场与稳态剪切共同作用下形成由富液滴区和贫液滴区交替排列的带状结构（banded structures），这些结构在施加电场后数秒内出现，关断电场后迅速衰减。Jensen–Shannon 散度分析显示，驱动结构在约1秒的时间尺度上失去记忆，与EHD对流卷（convection roll）的特征时间相当；在更长的场关断间隔后，先后发生的带状事件统计独立。

Conclusion: 油包油乳液在电流变 regime 服从屈服应力流体行为，且屈服应力呈 $E^2$ 标度；ER行为具有尺度无关性，SAOS可以无损探测材料本征性质。在EHD regime中，电场与稳态剪切协同作用使乳液形成可逆的带状结构，其记忆时间与EHD对流时间尺度匹配，长时间的场关断可实现各次带状事件的统计去相关。

Abstract: Recently, we reported the electrorheoimaging (ERI) technique (Bahraminasr et al, 2026), and found that frequency-dependent electric field of an oil-in-oil emulsion yields two distinct regimes: a high-frequency dipolar, electrorheological (ER) regime and a low-frequency electrohydrodynamic (EHD) regime. In this work, we identify a phenomenological model to fit the results in the ER regime to a classic yield-stress fluid, and find collapse onto a master curve upon rescaling, consistent with a yield stress that grows approximately as $E^2$. Macroscopic small-amplitude oscillatory shear (SAOS) rheology is compared with passive microrheology employing differential dynamic microscopy (DDM), with the close agreement implying scale independence of the ER behaviour, and indicating that, unlike steady shear, SAOS measurements do not restructure these samples and probe underlying material properties. Finally, under the presence of both steady shear and electric fields in the EHD regime, the emulsion forms banded structures composed of alternating droplet-rich and droplet-depleted regions. We explore recurrence and divergence in the location of these bands: they emerge within seconds of field application and decay rapidly after the field is switched off. Using the Jensen--Shannon divergence between radial intensity profiles, we show that the driven structure loses memory on timescales of order $1~s$ commensurate with the timescale of the EHD convection roll. For much longer field-off intervals successive banding events become statistically independent.

</details>


### [7] [Surface-Adsorbed Nanodroplets of Symmetric Diblock Copolymers Form Versatile and Stimuli-Responsive Nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00293)
*Artem Petrov,Guillermo A. Hernández-Mendoza,Alfredo Alexander-Katz*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）计算，发现衬底上吸附的对称双嵌段共聚物（symmetric diblock copolymers）纳米液滴（10–100 nm）能够形成多种可外部切换的纳米结构，并建立了近平衡态的四维形态相图。研究表明，通过改变组分间相互作用强度（如在实验中添加表面活性剂或控制温度），可实现不同液滴形态之间的直接可逆转变，从而证明了这类材料具有刺激响应性（stimuli-responsiveness）。这一发现为制备具有外部可切换层级微纳结构的智能涂层提供了可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 嵌段共聚物在基底上可形成纳米结构液滴，并进一步排列成规则微结构阵列，用于微电子学、等离子体学、传感、光子学、超材料乃至加密等领域。然而，这些材料是否能在施加外部刺激时，在单个液滴层面改变其纳米结构，尚不清楚。本文旨在探索对称双嵌段共聚物纳米液滴能否实现刺激响应性结构转变。

Method: 研究采用大规模自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory, SCFT）计算，在多种润湿（wetting）和相分离（phase separation）条件下，获得液滴形态的近平衡态四维相图。SCFT建模辅以一套计算算法，该算法可在不预先假定可能平衡结构的情况下，确定给定体系中液滴的平衡形态。此外，通过模拟添加表面活性剂（surfactant）来验证刺激响应性的实验可行性。

Result: 研究发现，对称双嵌段共聚物在基底上的纳米液滴（10–100 nm）可形成多种可外部切换的纳米结构。所发现的液滴纳米结构与先前发表的实验数据高度吻合。关键在于，改变组分间相互作用强度可实现不同液滴形态之间的直接可逆转变，而在实验中这种相互作用可通过添加表面活性剂或控制温度来外部调控。模拟添加表面活性剂导致了液滴纳米结构之间的切换，证实了这种刺激响应性的实验可实现性。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，即使是最简单的对称双嵌段共聚物，在限制于纳米液滴中时，也能在表面产生多功能且刺激响应性的结构。这为制备具有外部可切换层级微结构和纳米结构的智能涂层（smart coatings）开辟了可能性。

Abstract: Block copolymers often create droplets when placed on a substrate. Such nanostructured droplets can be arranged into regular microstructured arrays, thereby forming hierarchically organized materials that can be used in microelectronics, plasmonics, sensing, photonics, metamaterials production, and even cryptography. However, it is unclear if such materials can be stimuli-responsive, i.e., be able to change their nanostructure on a single droplet level upon applying external stimuli. In this work, we discovered that small (10-100 nm) surface-adsorbed droplets of symmetric diblock copolymers can form a multitude of different externally switchable nanostructures. We obtained a near-equilibrium, comprehensive 4D diagram of droplet morphologies by performing large-scale self-consistent field theory (SCFT) calculations under various wetting and phase separation conditions. The SCFT modeling was augmented with a computational algorithm that established an equilibrium droplet morphology in a given system without assuming potentially equilibrium structures prior to simulation. The discovered droplet nanostructures agreed excellently with previously published experimental data. Crucially, we showed that direct and reversible transitions between different droplet morphologies are possible upon changing the interaction strength between components, which can be tuned externally in experiments by adding surfactants or controlling temperature. We confirmed experimental realizability of such stimuli-responsiveness by modeling surfactant addition that led to a switch between droplet nanostructures. This work demonstrates that even the simplest symmetric diblock copolymers are able to produce versatile and stimuli-responsive structures on a surface when confined to a small nanodroplet. This opens the possibility to produce smart coatings with externally switchable hierarchical micro- and nanostructures.

</details>


### [8] [Machine learning evaluation of structural descriptors for supercooled water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00415)
*Kohei Yoshikawa,Kokoro Shikata,Kang Kim,Nobuyuki Matubayasi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用神经网络温度分类框架，系统评估了16种用于描述过冷水局部结构的结构描述符（structural descriptors）的性能，并通过可解释人工智能（explainable AI）方法揭示了这些描述符如何编码局部结构信息，建立了一个数据驱动的描述符基准测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液态水的反常行为被广泛认为与过冷水（supercooled water）中高密度态和低密度态之间的液-液转变（liquid-liquid phase transition）相关，而四面体氢键网络（tetrahedral hydrogen-bond networks）在微观层面主导了这些性质。尽管已有多种结构描述符被提出以刻画局部分子环境，但它们大多是独立提出的，缺乏系统的比较。

Method: 研究采用基于神经网络（neural network）的温度分类框架，对16种先前提出的结构描述符进行性能评估；并结合可解释人工智能（explainable artificial intelligence）方法，识别模型预测所依赖的结构特征。

Result: 该框架客观评估了各描述符区分过冷水中温度依赖结构变化的能力，并通过可解释AI方法揭示了不同描述符如何编码局部结构信息。

Conclusion: 研究工作建立了一个数据驱动的基准测试框架，用于系统评估液态水中的结构描述符。

Abstract: The anomalous behavior of liquid water is widely associated with a liquid-liquid phase transition between high- and low-density states in the supercooled regime. At the microscopic level, tetrahedral hydrogen-bond networks govern these properties, motivating structural descriptors that characterize local molecular environments. These structural descriptors quantify features such as tetrahedral order, local density, and the separation between the first and second coordination shells; however, they have largely been proposed independently, with limited systematic comparison. Here we evaluate 16 previously proposed descriptors using a neural-network-based temperature classification framework, enabling an objective assessment of their ability to distinguish temperature-dependent structural changes in supercooled water. We further apply an explainable artificial intelligence method that identifies the structural features responsible for the model predictions. This approach reveals how different descriptors encode local structural information and establishes a data-driven framework for benchmarking structural descriptors in liquid water.

### [9] [Pre-charging polymer surfaces enhances droplet mobility and electrification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00481)
*Shuaijia Chen,Kenta Morita,Dumindu Dassanayaka,Hans-Jürgen Butt,Peter C. Sherrell,Amanda V. Ellis,Joseph D. Berry*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过系统控制聚合物表面电荷（包括聚四氟乙烯和尼龙-66），研究发现液滴在首次润湿时会拾取预沉积的表面离子，转移电荷量与润湿区域遇到的沉积电荷直接相关（中低密度下与材料性质无关）；沉积电荷通过增加有效固体表面能来降低接触角并提高接触线移动性，高密度时则引发液滴分裂或脱离等不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物材料表面束缚电荷（surface-bound electric charge）会强烈影响液滴行为和固-液电荷转移，但其机制和控制手段尚不清楚，因此本研究旨在系统阐明这一过程并实现可控的固液带电（solid-liquid electrification）。

Method: 首先使用抗静电离子风机（anti-static ion blower）中和聚合物表面（聚四氟乙烯 PTFE 和尼龙-66 Nylon-66），再通过离子枪（ion gun）施加可控电荷，从而系统调控表面电荷密度并进行液滴润湿实验。

Result: 液滴在首次润湿时拾取预沉积的表面离子；在中低沉积密度（|σ_d|<40 μC/m²）下转移电荷量与润湿面积所遇到的沉积电荷直接相关，且与材料性质无关；沉积电荷降低接触角（contact angle）并增加接触线移动性（contact-line mobility），其规律符合有效固体表面能（effective solid surface energy）增加的机制；高表面电荷密度时出现液滴分裂或脱离等不稳定性。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一种有效控制固液带电的方法，可实现表面电荷的放大或抑制，并定向操纵表面上的流体运动。

Abstract: Surface-bound electric charge on polymer materials can strongly influence droplet behaviour and solid-liquid charge transfer, but the mechanisms and the means to control these effects remain unclear. In this work, we systematically controlled the surface charge on polymer surfaces, including polytetrafluoroethylene (PTFE) and Nylon-66, by first neutralising the surfaces with an anti-static ion blower and then applying charge using an ion gun. We find that droplets pick up pre-deposited surface ions during the first wetting of the surface, and that the transferred charge directly correlates with the deposited charge encountered by the wetted area for moderate deposited densities (|σ_d |<40 μC/m2) independent of material properties. We also demonstrate that the deposited charge reduces contact angle and increases contact-line mobility in a manner consistent with an increase in effective solid surface energy. For higher surface charge densities, we observe instabilities such as droplet splitting or detachment. This work demonstrates an effective approach to control solid-liquid electrification, enabling amplification or suppression of surface charge and the directed manipulation of fluid motion on surfaces.

### [10] [Dispersion of multiple charged species in an axially symmetric slowly varying channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00653)
*Thakurdas Mahata,Anirban Chatterjee,Ameeya Kumar Nayak*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过结合润滑近似（lubrication approximation）与均匀化理论（homogenization theory），在电中性（electroneutrality）和零电流（zero-current）约束下，推导出多物种带电离子在通道中输运与弥散的有效传输方程，并研究了通道几何形状对离子分离性能的影响，发现了几何诱导的电-扩散耦合效应会导致理论塔板数（NTP）出现非单调行为，从而有利于分离过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多物种带电离子的输运与弥散是电动力学离子分离等生物与物理过程的核心，但现有理论大多聚焦于中性溶质在通道中的弥散行为，对多电荷物种的输运研究相对不足。

Method: 将润滑近似与均匀化理论相结合，在电中性和零电流约束下推导出关于横截面平均浓度的有效传输方程，并针对多种通道几何构型计算有效弥散系数（effective dispersion coefficient）。

Result: 发现通道几何形状可诱导电-扩散耦合（electro-diffusive coupling），该效应在某些通道中抑制了溶质弥散，导致理论塔板数出现非单调变化。

Conclusion: 几何诱导的电-扩散耦合效应使特定通道构型在离子分离过程中具有优越性能，为优化设计分离通道提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The transport and dispersion of multiple species of charged ions are central to many biological and physical processes, including electrokinetic ion separation. However, most theoretical studies of dispersion in channels have focused on neutral solutes, leaving the transport of multiple charged species comparatively unexplored. Differences in ionic diffusivities in a multispecies electrolyte solution generate an self-induced electric fields that drive electromigration. To capture these effects at the macroscopic scale, we combine the lubrication approximation with homogenization theory, under electroneutrality and zero-current constraints, to derive an effective transport equation governing the cross-sectionally averaged concentrations. We apply our model framework to a range of channel geometries and compute the resulting effective dispersion coefficients. Finally, we investigate how channel geometry can be tuned to enhance ionic separation. We observe a geometry-induced electro-diffusive coupling that inhibits solute dispersion in certain channels, leading to a non-monotonic Number of Theoretical Plates (NTP) and making such channels ideal for separation processes.

</details>


### [11] [Architecting mechanosensitive nanofluidic transport in graphite nanoslits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00661)
*Mathieu Lizée,Zhijia Zhang,Baptiste Coquinot,Qian Yang,Lydéric Bocquet*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究展示二维石墨烯纳米狭缝（nanoslit）中的离子传输可在无结构变形的情况下实现双向压力敏感响应，其机制源于通道入口的选择性充电作为可逆移动载流子源，并通过压力驱动水流调控离子电导。理论模型与实验数据定量吻合，揭示了纳米尺度非线性耦合在设计自适应仿生纳流系统（nanofluidic systems）中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 力学敏感离子传输（mechanosensitive ion transport）是生物系统通过软离子通道变形感知和适应环境的核心机制。本研究旨在探索是否能在无结构变形条件下，通过理性工程设计实现纳流通道的双向压力敏感响应，从而简化仿生力学传感系统。

Method: 研究采用实验与理论相结合的方法：在二维石墨烯纳米狭缝中构建选择性充电的通道入口作为可逆载流子源，并通过压力驱动水流调控离子载流子的平流（advection）；同时建立了一个全面的电流体动力学模型（electrohydrodynamic model），解析地耦合了扩散、对流、表面输运、扩散渗流（diffusio-osmosis）及界面滑移等效应，覆盖纳米狭缝内外区域。

Result: 实验结果显示，该纳米狭缝结构实现了双向压力敏感的电导响应。理论模型定量复现了实验数据，表明简单的表面电荷模式即可产生复杂且依赖于压力的电导行为。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了纳米尺度丰富非线性耦合（nonlinear couplings）的可设计性，可被用于构建自适应仿生纳流系统，并为离子压力传感器（ionic pressure sensors）提供了新范例。

Abstract: Mechanosensitive ion transport plays a central role in enabling living systems to perceive and adapt to their environment through the deformation of soft, embedded ion channels. In this work, we demonstrate that ion transport within a two-dimensional graphite nanoslit can be rationally engineered to achieve a bipolar, pressure-sensitive response without any structural deformation. The mechanosensitivity arises from the selective charging of one channel inlet, which acts as a reversible source of mobile charge carriers. These excess-ions can then be advected in or out of the channel by the pressure-driven water flow, thereby modulating the ionic conductance. This mechanism is captured through a comprehensive electrohydrodynamic model that analytically accounts for coupled diffusion, convection, surface transport, diffusio-osmosis, and interfacial slippage, both inside and outside the nanoslit. The theoretical framework quantitatively reproduces the experimental data, showing that a simple surface charge pattern can give rise to complex, pressure-dependent conductance. These findings reveal how rich nonlinear couplings at the nanoscale can be harnessed to design adaptive, bioinspired nanofluidic systems, exemplified here by ionic pressure sensors.

### [12] [Statistical mechanics for Scrabble predicts strategy, entropy and language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00813)
*Olivier Witteveen,Marianne Bauer*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于最大熵方法（maximum entropy approach）构建了一个配对模型（pairwise model），用于分析 Scrabble 棋盘上连通的字母格子图（connected graphs of occupied sites）。该模型能够准确复现真实游戏中的均值和协方差，预测单词长度统计与几何特征，并揭示不同语言间 Scrabble 图的可区分性及熵差异，其预测能力更依赖于策略性玩法（如棋盘上单词长度）而非词汇表大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望找到一种尽可能无结构的（structureless）描述方式，能够再现真实 Scrabble 游戏中观察到的均值和协方差，并进一步理解 Scrabble 棋盘图的统计特性及其在不同语言之间的差异。

Method: 研究采用最大熵方法（maximum entropy approach），将其适配到连通图（connected graphs）上，构建了一个仅利用均值和协方差信息的配对模型（pairwise model），以拟合真实 Scrabble 游戏数据。

Result: 该配对模型能够准确捕捉数据特征，正确预测单词长度统计和棋盘图的几何特征；其参数具有可解释性，可用于理解 Scrabble 策略。模型计算的熵差异表明，战略玩法（strategy gameplay）比词汇表大小（lexicon size）更能预测熵值。此外，该模型能以较低计算代价将 Scrabble 图正确归入对应语言。

Conclusion: 基于最大熵的配对模型为分析 Scrabble 图的统计特性提供了一种有效且可解释的工具；不同语言间的 Scrabble 图具有可区分性，且游戏策略比语言本身的词汇规模对熵的影响更大。

Abstract: The crossword-like patterns of tiles in Scrabble form connected graphs of occupied sites on a square lattice. We find the most structureless description that reproduces means and covariances observed in real Scrabble games by adapting a maximum entropy approach to connected graphs. This pairwise model captures the data well, and predicts word-length statistics and geometric features of the Scrabble graphs correctly; in addition, the parameters of this model are interpretable and allow us to understand Scrabble playing strategies. Using this pairwise model, we calculate entropy differences and distinguishability of Scrabble graphs across languages, without having access to the letters on the tiles. Notably, we find that the entropy is predicted better by strategic gameplay -- such as word length on the board -- than lexicon size. Finally, we find that we can use the pairwise model to correctly assign Scrabble graphs to languages, avoiding explicit feature selection and at relatively low computational cost.

</details>

### [13] [Observation of single antiferromagnetic magnon modes in the tunnelling transistors of spin-1/2 Kitaev system a-RuCl3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00202)
*Servet Ozdemir,Mikhail Kashchenko,Kostya S. Novoselov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文对少层α-RuCl₃薄膜的平面和隧穿电子特性进行了系统研究，发现其在室温下呈n型半导体性质，并在120K以下表现出莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）行为；在7–14.5K的尼尔温度（Néel temperature）以下观测到非弹性散射特征，其中部分归因于单磁子模式（single magnon modes），证实了原子级薄层极限下保留了体材料的锯齿形反铁磁序（zigzag antiferromagnetic order）及其单磁子模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: α-RuCl₃是实现量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）态最有前景的候选材料之一，但此前对该体系的电子学研究主要局限于石墨烯近邻效应，缺乏对少层薄膜电子性质的系统表征。

Method: 本文采用平面和隧穿电子输运方法，系统研究了三层及以下厚度的α-RuCl₃薄膜的电子特性，包括室温下的半导体性质、低温下的莫特绝缘体转变以及低于尼尔温度的非弹性散射特征。

Result: 室温下α-RuCl₃薄膜表现为n型半导体；120K以下呈现莫特绝缘体性质；在7–14.5K的尼尔温度以下观测到非弹性散射特征，部分特征可归因于单磁子模式。实验证实了原子级薄层中保留了体材料的锯齿形反铁磁序及其单磁子模式。

Conclusion: 该研究为在锯齿形反铁磁序附近实现量子自旋液体态的电学表征以及α-RuCl₃中马约拉纳激发（Majorana excitations）的隧穿晶体管研究提供了实验进展。

Abstract: The small gap room temperature semiconductor a-RuCl3 which is known to undergo a Mott-Hubbard transition at low temperatures, is one of the most promising candidates for realisation of an exotic matter form, the quantum spin liquid state, which may have applications in quantum computing. Although being extensively investigated by neutron scattering techniques, electronic study of this system in form of van der Waals heterostructures has been limited to mainly graphene proximity. Here we report a systematic study of planar and tunnelling electronic properties of a -RuCl3 films, where we observe an n-type semiconducting property of a -RuCl3 films at room temperature, with a Mott insulator nature onset below 120K. In constant some of the previous studies, we focus on films of three-layer thickness and below and we find inelastic scattering features, below the Neel temperature of 7-14.5 K, some of which we attribute to single magnon modes. We believe our study electrically confirms preserved low temperature signatures of the bulk zigzag antiferromagnetic order and its single magnon modes within the previously observed continuum in atomically thin film limit. The experimental progress could be a step for future electronic characterisation of quantum spin liquid state in the vicinity of the zigzag antiferromagnetic order as well as the Majorona excitations in a-RuCl3 in tunnelling transistors.

</details>


### [14] [Polarization-controlled effective Rabi dynamics in driven Graphene: A Floquet-Magnus approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00325)
*V. G. Ibarra-Sierra,J. L. Cardoso,C. Flores-Valente,A. Kunold,J. C. Sandoval-Santana*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Floquet-Magnus展开分析了狄拉克电子在椭圆偏振辐射下的共振动力学，发现偏振椭率β和电子动量与驱动场的相对夹角Δ可作为独立的控制参数，通过贝塞尔谐波J₀(ζ)和J₂(ζ)的干涉调控准能量分裂，并识别出偏振诱导的相位作为等效的初始Floquet敲击，从而为二维狄拉克材料中的量子控制提供可调谐手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索周期性驱动狄拉克系统中偏振椭率（polarization ellipticity）β与相对夹角Δ作为独立控制参数对相干动力学的影响，揭示偏振态如何调控共振响应和量子相干演化。

Method: 采用Floquet-Magnus展开（Floquet-Magnus expansion），在相互作用绘景（interaction picture）中应用旋转波变换，推导出共振条件（ω = Ω/2）下的有效两能级哈密顿量，并通过时间演化算符的显式傅里叶分解分离宏运动（macromotion）与微运动（micromotion）贡献。

Result: 准能量分裂依赖于β和Δ通过贝塞尔谐波J₀(ζ)与J₂(ζ)的干涉；圆偏振（β = ±1）恢复旋转对称性产生与Δ无关的有效拉比频率，而椭圆和线偏振产生π周期角调制的各向异性响应；偏振诱导的相位作为有效初始Floquet敲击改变初始条件，导致占据振荡的时间偏移，其符号依赖于手性和相对取向；数值模拟验证了零阶Magnus近似在弱场下百个驱动周期内均方根误差约为1%。

Conclusion: 偏振椭率和相对取向可作为二维狄拉克材料中可调谐且实验可行的量子控制旋钮，对时间分辨光谱学具有直接意义。

Abstract: Polarization ellipticity $β$ and the relative angle $Δ$ between electron momentum and driving field act as independent control parameters for coherent dynamics in periodically driven Dirac systems. In this work, we analyze the dynamics of resonantly driven Dirac electrons in graphene under elliptically polarized electromagnetic radiation using the Floquet-Magnus expansion. Working in the interaction picture and applying a rotating-wave-type transformation, we derive an effective two-level Hamiltonian that governs the macromotion at resonance ($ω= Ω/2$). The resulting quasienergy splitting depends nontrivially on $β$ and $Δ$ through interference between the Bessel harmonics $J_0(ζ)$ and $J_2(ζ)$. Circular polarization ($β= \pm 1$) restores rotational symmetry and yields a $Δ$-independent effective Rabi frequency, whereas elliptical and linear polarizations produce anisotropic responses with a $π$-periodic angular modulation. Beyond spectral properties, we identify a polarization-induced phase that acts as an effective initial Floquet kick, shifting the effective initial conditions and producing measurable shifts in the timing of occupation oscillations, whose sign depends on both helicity and relative orientation. Through an explicit Fourier decomposition of the time-evolution operator, we separate macromotion from micromotion contributions and validate the zeroth-order Magnus approximation via numerical simulations, achieving root-mean-square errors of $\sim 1\%$ over 100 driving periods in the weak-field regime. These results establish polarization ellipticity and relative orientation as tunable and experimentally accessible knobs for quantum control in two-dimensional Dirac materials, with direct implications for time-resolved spectroscopy.

</details>


### [15] [Investigation of nonlocal transport associated with the orbital Hall effect in Ti](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00359)
*Keitaro Takashina,Naoki Yano,Asahi Oe,Mari Taniguchi,Shuto Kimura,Kazuya Ando*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过在单层Ti霍尔棒（Hall bar）中观测非局域电阻（nonlocal resistance），探索由轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）驱动的轨道输运（orbital transport）特征。实验发现Ti的轨道霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）可忽略，但非局域电阻信号仍然存在。有限元模拟表明信号包含显著的欧姆旁路（Ohmic bypass）贡献，但在小通道宽度下该贡献被强烈抑制，无法完全解释观测到的非局域电阻，提示存在与轨道霍尔效应相关的额外非局域输运成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索单层Ti中由轨道霍尔效应驱动的轨道电流输运（orbital-current transport）特征，以验证轨道霍尔效应是否能在自旋霍尔效应可忽略的材料中产生可观测的非局域输运信号。

Method: 在单层Ti霍尔棒器件上测量非局域电阻，研究其对中心通道宽度（central channel width）的依赖性，并结合有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）分离欧姆旁路贡献。

Result: 实验观测到有限非局域电阻；有限元模拟表明信号包含可观的欧姆旁路贡献，但在小通道宽度时该贡献被强烈抑制；即使考虑Ti电阻率变化，欧姆旁路贡献仍无法完全解释观测到的非局域电阻。

Conclusion: 单层Ti中的非局域电阻不仅包含欧姆旁路背景，还存在额外的非局域贡献，该贡献可能与Ti中轨道霍尔效应驱动的轨道输运有关。

Abstract: We investigate nonlocal transport in single-layer Ti Hall bars to explore signatures of orbital-current transport driven by the orbital Hall effect. Despite the negligible spin Hall effect in Ti, we observe a finite nonlocal resistance in the single-layer Ti Hall bar and study its dependence on the central channel width. Finite-element simulations show that the measured signal contains a sizable Ohmic bypass contribution. However, the bypass contribution is strongly suppressed at small channel widths and cannot fully account for the observed nonlocal resistance even when variations in the Ti resistivity are taken into account. Our results therefore suggest an additional nonlocal contribution distinct from the Ohmic bypass background, which may be associated with orbital transport driven by the orbital Hall effect in Ti.

### [16] [Thermodynamic Charge Partition in Accumulation-Layer Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00441)
*Elmar Böckenhoff*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个热力学描述框架，通过将感生面密度在近界面积累层电荷与互补屏蔽电荷之间进行分配，构建了完整的亥姆霍兹自由能、修正的锁定支化学势和偏移释放势，从而将积累层异质结构（accumulation-layer heterostructures）的微分电容、隧穿电流和平台宽度统一于同一耦合热力学结构之中，并通过自洽泊松-薛定谔约化（self-consistent Poisson–Schrödinger reduction）给出可计算的通用主函数和主曲面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论缺乏一个统一的热力学框架来描述积累层异质结构中电荷分配、能路径选择和几何电容效应之间的耦合关系，无法同时解释微分电容、隧穿电流和磁致屏蔽深度等实验观测。

Method: 将感生面密度在近界面积累层电荷与互补屏蔽电荷之间的分配作为中心状态变量，由此构建完整的亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）、修正的锁定支化学势（locked-branch chemical potential）和偏移释放势（shifted release potential）。物理路径通过谱方法（spectrally）选择：可压缩段保持完全屏蔽，不可压缩段沿锁定支演化直到相关能隙触发释放。采用规范的两阶段自洽Poisson-Schrödinger约化，为孤立积累层推导通用主函数（master functions），为有限缓冲层扩展推导主曲面（master surfaces）。

Result: 理论预测的微分电容、隧穿电流和平台宽度来自同一耦合热力学结构的不同投影。与磁电容（magnetocapacitance）和磁隧穿（magnetotunneling）实验数据的对比支持如下物理图像：附近的扩展电荷对积累层进行再填充，且有效屏蔽深度（effective screening depth）随磁场增大而增加。

Conclusion: 该热力学描述统一了积累层异质结构中多个实验可观测量的理论解释，揭示了电荷分配作为核心状态变量的作用，并表明屏蔽深度的磁场依赖性是该理论框架的关键预测和实验验证之一。

Abstract: We develop a thermodynamic description of accumulation-layer heterostructures in which the induced sheet density is partitioned between the near-interface accumulation-layer charge and a complementary screening charge in the surrounding structure. Treating this partition as the central state variable yields a complete Helmholtz free energy, a corrected locked-branch chemical potential, and a shifted release potential that separates energetic path selection from geometric capacitance. The physical path is selected spectrally: compressible segments remain fully screened, whereas incompressible segments evolve along a locked branch until release is triggered by the relevant gap. Differential capacitance, tunnel current and plateau width then emerge as different projections of the same coupled thermodynamic structure. A canonical two-stage self-consistent Poisson--Schrödinger reduction supplies universal master functions for the isolated accumulation layer and master surfaces for its finite-buffer extension, making the theory calculable across density and geometry. Comparison with magnetocapacitance and magnetotunneling data supports a picture in which nearby extended charge refills the accumulation layer and the effective screening depth grows with magnetic field.

</details>


### [17] [Suppressing spin qubit decoherence during shuttling via confinement modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00611)
*Daniel Q. L. Nguyen,Maximilian Rimbach-Russ,Stefano Bosco*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出通过调制约束势阱实现连续动态去耦的“呼吸穿梭”协议，利用空穴自旋系统中的自旋-轨道相互作用在移动过程中持续驱动自旋，从而抑制低频噪声、提升长距离量子比特穿梭的相干性，并在锗空穴自旋量子比特上验证了其可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠的远距离量子比特穿梭（long-range qubit shuttling）是可扩展量子计算架构的关键技术，但移动过程中自旋量子比特的退相干（decoherence）问题限制了其性能。本文旨在通过连续动态去耦（continuous dynamical decoupling）策略提高移动自旋量子比特的相干性（coherence）。

Method: 提出时间与空间“呼吸穿梭”（temporal and spatial breathing shuttling）协议，利用空穴自旋系统（hole-spin systems）中的自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interactions）在移动过程中电学驱动自旋，实现穿戴态穿梭（dressed-state shuttling）。采用滤波器函数形式化（filter function formalism）分析抑制全局与局域磁/电噪声的驱动区间。

Result: 约束调制穿梭（confinement-modulated shuttling）能显著增强传输过程中的相干性，同时揭示了噪声关联长度（correlation length）对性能的限制。在锗空穴自旋量子比特（germanium hole-spin qubits）中的应用表明，该协议可实现抗噪声的远距离相干量子链路（noise-resilient long-range coherent quantum links）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于约束势阱调制的穿梭协议通过连续自旋旋转有效抑制低频噪声，为可扩展量子计算架构中的长距离高保真度量子比特传输提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Reliable long-range qubit shuttling is a powerful tool for scalable quantum computing architectures. We investigate strategies to improve the coherence of moving spin qubits by performing continuous dynamical decoupling by modulating their confinement potential. Specifically, we introduce temporal and spatial breathing shuttling protocols that leverage spin-orbit interactions in hole-spin systems to electrically drive the qubit while moving. This enables efficient dressed-state shuttling, where the spin is continuously rotated during transport, suppressing the effect of low-frequency noise. Using the filter function formalism, we identify driving regimes that efficiently mitigate both global and local magnetic and electric noise sources. We find that confinement-modulated shuttling can significantly enhance coherence during transport, while revealing distinct limitations depending on the correlation length of the noise. Applying our framework to germanium hole-spin qubits, we show that these protocols provide a practical route toward noise-resilient long-range coherent quantum links.

### [18] [Experimental Evidence of Fractional Entropy in Critical Kondo Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00669)
*C. Piquard,A. Veillon,Y. Sato,F. Zanichelli,A. Aassime,A. Cavanna,U. Gennser,A. K. Mitchell,A. Anthore,F. Pierre*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过测量金属-半导体量子电路在双通道和三通道近藤（Kondo）临界点处的低温分数熵 ΔS，直接实验证明了非阿贝尔任意子（non-Abelian anyons）的存在——包括马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero mode）和斐波那契任意子（Fibonacci anyon）。实验获得的熵值与理论预测的量子维度 d 对数关系 ΔS = kB ln(d) 一致，建立了熵测量作为表征奇异量子态的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非阿贝尔任意子因其非整数量子维度 d>1 而有望用于拓扑量子计算中以实现受保护的量子信息编码与处理，但通过传统输运测量对其进行明确表征一直面临挑战。因此，寻找一种可直接验证非阿贝尔任意子特征的新实验方法成为迫切需求。

Method: 研究采用微米尺度的金属岛（metallic island）耦合两个或三个电子引线，构建金属-半导体量子电路，通过调节系统分别达到双通道和三通道近藤临界点（Kondo critical points）。利用测量岛电荷并借助热力学麦克斯韦关系（Maxwell relation），估算这些临界态中涌现的任意子所携带的熵。

Result: 实验观测到分数化的熵值：双通道情况下 ΔS = kB ln(√2)，对应马约拉纳零模；三通道情况下 ΔS = kB ln((1+√5)/2)，对应斐波那契任意子。这些测量值与理论预言的量子维度对数关系 ΔS = kB ln(d) 完全一致，直接揭示了非阿贝尔任意子的存在。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过低温熵测量能够直接表征非阿贝尔任意子的量子维度，为实验鉴定奇异量子态提供了超越传统输运测量的新途径。这一方法有望成为拓扑量子计算研究中表征非阿贝尔任意子的重要工具。

Abstract: Unconventional quantum states defying the ubiquitous Fermi-liquid paradigm can emerge in the presence of strong electronic correlations. Among these, non-Abelian anyons - such as Majorana zero modes and Fibonacci anyons - are of particular interest for topological quantum computing due to their non-integer quantum dimensions d>1, which allows for protected non-local encoding and processing of quantum information. However, despite considerable efforts, the unambiguous characterisation of such anyons via transport measurements has proved challenging. Instead, here we provide experimental evidence for the low-temperature fractional entropy Delta S associated with a single anyon, which directly implies its non-Abelian character through the relation Delta S = kB ln(d). This thermodynamic signature is measured in metal-semiconductor quantum circuits engineered to realize quantum-critical states from frustrated interactions. Using a micrometre-scale metallic island coupled to two or three electronic leads, we tune the system to two-channel and three-channel Kondo critical points. By measuring the island charge and exploiting a thermodynamic Maxwell relation, we estimate the entropy associated with the anyons that emerge in these critical states. Our observations reveal fractional values, exposing non-Abelian anyons. The corresponding scaling dimensions are consistent with theoretical predictions for a Majorana zero mode Delta S = kB ln(sqrt(2)) and a Fibonacci anyon Delta S = kB ln(1 +sqrt(5))/2 for two and three channels. These findings establish entropy measurements as a powerful tool for characterizing exotic quantum states.

</details>

### [19] [On the Asymptotic Causal Structure in Gravitational EFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00089)
*Bruno Bucciotti,Paolo Creminelli,Alessandro Longo,Warin Patrick McBlain,Enrico Trincherini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究引力有效场论（EFT）在黑洞背景下的渐近因果结构，发现时空维度 D>4 时高阶导数算符会导致渐近超光速性从而约束 EFT 的有效范围，而在 D=4 时渐近因果结构与 Schwarzschild 解一致，无量纲时间提前（time advance）出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在引入引力后，超光速性（superluminality）的概念变得微妙，因为不存在与闵可夫斯基光锥（Minkowski light cone）进行不变比较的全局方式。因此需要借助渐近判据——考察 EFT 是否允许信号传播快于渐近时空结构所允许的速度，从而约束 EFT 的有效性范围。

Method: 通过分析黑洞背景中存在高阶导数算符（higher-derivative operators）时的信号传播，研究引力 EFT 的渐近因果结构。首先以代表性算符 $R_{μνρσ}F^{μν}F^{ρσ}$ 为例，随后推广至任意 EFT，论证结论仅依赖于度规的渐近行为。

Result: 在 D>4 时，有效光锥（effective light cones）可导致真正的渐近超光速性，从而约束 EFT 的有效范围。在 D=4 时，渐近因果结构与 Schwarzschild 度规完全一致：瞬时空曲线（prompt null curves）不受高阶导数修正影响，不存在渐近时间提前。

Conclusion: 在 D=4 时空中，可通过两种方式定义超光速性：引入协变截断（covariant cut-off），将理论置于渐近 AdS（asymptotically-AdS）背景中；或施加硬截断（hard cut-off），在有限距离内工作。

Abstract: It is usually assumed that a healthy EFT should not allow superluminal propagation. In the presence of gravity, however, the notion of superluminality becomes subtle, since there is no invariant way to compare with an underlying Minkowski light cone. One can instead resort to an asymptotic criterion: whether the EFT can induce signal propagation faster than what allowed by the asymptotic structure of spacetime. In this work we study the asymptotic causal structure of gravitational EFTs by analysing signal propagation in black-hole backgrounds in the presence of higher-derivative operators. We show that in spacetime dimensions D>4 the effective light cones can lead to genuine asymptotic superluminality, which can be used to constrain the regime of validity of the EFT. By contrast, in D=4 the asymptotic causal structure is universally identical to that of Schwarzschild: prompt null curves remain insensitive to higher-derivative corrections and no asymptotic time advance is possible. We first study the representative operator $R_{μνρσ}F^{μν}F^{ρσ}$, then show that this conclusion is true for any EFT, as it relies only on the asymptotic behaviour of the metric. Finally, we discuss two ways to define superluminality in D=4 spacetimes: introducing a covariant cut-off by putting the theory in an asymptotically-AdS background, or imposing a hard cut-off by working at finite distance.

</details>


### [20] [Topological charges and confined-deconfined phase transition in holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00203)
*Nelson R. F. Braga,William S. Cunha*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息AdS/QCD模型证明，在反德西特空间中引入能量标度会导致拓扑类改变，这种改变对应于由霍金-佩奇相变分隔的禁闭相与退禁闭相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，许多工作为黑洞性质提供了拓扑描述，其中黑洞对应扩展（离壳）参数空间中的拓扑缺陷并带有总拓扑荷。本文旨在利用这一框架，研究规范/引力对偶中禁闭-退禁闭相变与黑洞拓扑类变化之间的关系。

Method: 采用全息AdS/QCD模型（holographic AdS/QCD model），在反德西特空间中引入一个能量标度（energy scale），分析该标度对黑洞拓扑类的影响。

Result: 在反德西特空间中引入能量标度会导致拓扑类（topological class）发生改变；该改变对应着禁闭相（confined phase）与退禁闭相（deconfined phase）的存在，两者在有限临界温度下由霍金-佩奇相变（Hawking Page transition）分隔。

Conclusion: 黑洞拓扑类的变化能够映射全息对偶中的禁闭-退禁闭相变，表明拓扑描述是理解规范/引力对偶中相变行为的一个有效工具。

Abstract: In recent years, many interesting works providing a topological description for black hole (BH) properties have appeared in the literature. In particular, in this framework BHs correspond to topological defects in an enlarged (off-shell) parameter space, with an associated total topological charge. In gauge/gravity duality the transition from the confined to the deconfined phase is mapped into the dominance of a BH phase in the gravity side. Here we show, using a holographic AdS/QCD model, that the introduction of an energy scale in anti-de Sitter (AdS) space results in a change in the topological class. Such a modification corresponds to the existence of confined and deconfined phases, separated by a Hawking Page transition at a finite critical temperature.

### [21] [Perturbative Analysis of CPT-Odd Lorentz-Violating Scalar QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00559)
*J. C. C. Felipe,L. C. T. Brito,A. C. Lehum,B. Altschul,A. Yu. Petrov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 对带伴随标量物质的CPT奇性洛伦兹破缺标量量子色动力学（scalar QCD）进行了完整的一圈重整化群分析，证明了该理论在此阶是可乘性重整化的，并计算了相应的重整化常数和β函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验在包含CPT奇性洛伦兹破缺项的情况下，带有伴随标量物质的标量量子色动力学是否仍能保持可乘性重整化（multiplicative renormalizability），并澄清该理论中洛伦兹破缺校正的紫外发散结构。

Method: 在首选背景矢量（preferred background vector）的一阶近似下，将对应算符视为微扰插入，计算规范场、标量场和鬼场的二点、三点和四点格林函数（Green's functions）的紫外发散部分；在完整的一圈水平上执行重整化群（renormalization group）分析。

Result: 规范扇区出现了通常的Carroll-Field-Jackiw型修正，该修正本征上发散的，但可在特定规范下消失；标量扇区出现对应CPT奇性单导数项；三和四点函数的若干洛伦兹破缺校正是紫外有限的；所有一圈发散均可被经典拉格朗日量中已允许的抵消项吸收。

Conclusion: 该理论在一圈水平上是可乘性重整化的，得到了耦合常数、洛伦兹破缺参数和标量自相互作用的重整化常数及一圈β函数。

Abstract: We perform a complete one-loop renormalization analysis of CPT-odd Lorentz-violating scalar quantum chromodynamics with adjoint scalar matter. Working to first order in the preferred background vector and treating the corresponding operators as perturbative insertions, we compute the ultraviolet-divergent parts of the relevant two-, three-, and four-point Green's functions for the gauge, scalar, and ghost fields. We show that the gauge sector develops the expected Carroll-Field-Jackiw-type correction, which generically turns out to be divergent in our theory, although the divergence vanishes in a certain gauge, while the scalar sector displays the corresponding CPT-odd single-derivative term proportional to the background vector. We further demonstrate that several of the Lorentz-violating corrections the three- and four-point function are ultraviolet finite. All one-loop divergences may be absorbed into counterterms already allowed by the classical Lagrangian, providing an explicit proof of the multiplicative renormalizability of the theory at this order. We also obtain the associated renormalization constants and one-loop $β$-functions for the gauge coupling, the Lorentz violation parameters, and the scalar self-interaction.

### [22] [More on Classical Stability of Hopf-like Solitons of the Toroidal-Twisted type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00757)
*Chao-Hsiang Sheu,Mikhail Shifman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过数值分析证实了在四维标量量子电动力学（QED）中，大尺寸类Hopf孤立子（包括Hopfions和vortons）作为局部能量极小值存在，从而验证了Faddeev-Noemi猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Faddeev和Noemi猜想认为Hopfions及类Hopf孤立子（vortons）可以基于QED内在的扭曲环形结构（twisted toroidal structure）存在，但此前仅在忽略外在曲率（extrinsic curvature）的近似下得到定性或半定量论证，缺乏严格的数值验证。

Method: 本研究采用数值分析方法（numerical analysis），对完整QED理论中的大尺寸类Hopf孤立子进行能量极小化计算，以检验这些构型是否作为局部能量极小值（local energy minima）存在。

Result: 数值分析结果确认，在完整QED理论中，大尺寸类Hopf孤立子确实可以作为局部能量极小值存在；而在Faddeev-Skyrme模型中，这些拓扑孤立子（topological solitons）则成为给定拓扑扇区（topological sector）中的全局极小值（global minima）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为Faddeev-Noemi猜想提供了增强的数值证据，表明QED中确实支持稳定的类Hopf孤立子构型。

Abstract: The Faddeev-Hopf model [1] supporting Hopfions was shown to emerge in the low-energy limit of four-dimensional scalar quantum electrodynamics (QED) with two charged scalar fields [2, 3]. Faddeev and Noemi conjectured that the Hopfions and Hopf-like solitons -- vortons -- can be based on a twisted toroidal structure inherent to QED [4-6]. This conjecture was discussed in detail in [2] in the approximation of negligibly small extrinsic curvature. Qualitative and semi-quantitative arguments were used to demonstrate the validity of the Faddeev-Noemi hypothesis. Here we further enhance the proof by applying a numerical analysis which confirms that large-size Hopf-like solitons exist as local energy minima in the full QED theory (in the Faddeev-Skyrme model they become topological solitons representing the global minima in the given topological sector).

</details>


### [23] [Breakdown of Semiclassical Gravity in Four-Dimensional Black Hole Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00780)
*David A. Lowe,Larus Thorlacius*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在一个四维半经典模型中研究黑洞形成与蒸发，发现在视界退缩后会出现类空“霹雳奇点”（thunderbolt singularity），该奇点延伸至经典曲率预期很小的远处，表明半经典有效场论（effective field theory）在大尺度上失效，并动摇了黑洞信息悖论（black hole information paradox）的标准表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在保持微分同胚不变性（diffeomorphism invariance）并重现单圈迹反常（one-loop trace anomaly）的四维半经典模型中，黑洞的形成与蒸发过程，特别是检验反作用（back-reaction）对时空几何的影响。

Method: 求解球对称零壳层（spherically symmetric null shell）坍缩的量子修正爱因斯坦方程（quantum-corrected Einstein equations），并在求解中包含反作用效应，跟踪黑洞从形成到蒸发的完整演化过程。

Result: 半经典解在发展过程中出现类空霹雳奇点，该奇点在表观视界（apparent horizon）退缩后出现，并延伸至半经典曲率预期很小的远处；该行为源于高阶导数半经典方程的非线性不稳定性（nonlinear instability），并且在具有反常诱导量子修正的模型中具有普遍性。

Conclusion: 霹雳奇点的出现表明半经典有效场论在宏观距离上失效，这动摇了标准黑洞信息悖论的基础。

Abstract: We study black hole formation and evaporation in a four-dimensional semiclassical model that preserves diffeomorphism invariance and reproduces the one-loop trace anomaly. Solving the quantum-corrected Einstein equations for the collapse of a spherically symmetric null shell, we follow the formation and evaporation of a black hole with back-reaction included. The semiclassical solutions develop a spacelike thunderbolt singularity that emerges after the apparent horizon has receded and extends far from the black hole where the semiclassical curvature is a priori expected to be parametrically small. This behavior arises from a nonlinear instability of the higher-derivative semiclassical equations and is generic in models with anomaly-induced quantum corrections. The thunderbolt signals a breakdown of semiclassical effective field theory over macroscopic distances and undermines the standard formulation of the black hole information paradox.

</details>

### [24] [Evidence for Quark Confinement in the Proton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00339)
*Xiangdong Ji,Gerald A. Miller,Chen Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用现有实验数据直接测量了质子内夸克所受的力，发现该力在广泛夸克位置范围内表现为吸引且恒定，从而为量子色动力学（QCD）中的禁闭现象提供了直接证据。该工作为未来电子-离子对撞机实验研究禁闭机制和核质量起源提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然量子色动力学（Quantum Chromodynamics, QCD）是描述夸克-胶子相互作用的理论，且大量实验表明夸克和胶子无法被单独观测（即“禁闭”（confinement）现象），但至今无人能够利用QCD从数学上严格证明禁闭。本文旨在利用现有实验数据定义并测量质子内夸克所受的力，从而获得禁闭的直接证据。

Method: 利用可获得的实验数据，定义并测量质子内夸克所受的力。通过分析该力的性质（是否吸引且恒定）来判断禁闭的成立。

Result: 测量发现，质子内夸克所受的力在广泛的夸克位置范围内表现为吸引且恒定，这一结果直接证实了禁闭现象的存在。

Conclusion: 该工作为未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider）实验提供了方向，旨在实现对禁闭机制和原子核质量起源的严格定量理解。

Abstract: The strong interaction is the fundamental force that holds quarks and the gluon force carriers together to form protons and neutrons and also binds the atomic nucleus. The theory governing quark-gluon interactions is Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD). A wide variety of experimental data teaches us that quarks and gluons cannot be observed in isolation, a phenomenon known as confinement that is unique to QCD. But no one has used QCD to mathematically prove confinement. Here we show how to define and measure the force on quarks in the proton using available experimental data. Direct evidence for confinement is obtained because the force is found to be attractive and constant for a wide range of quark positions. This work guides future experimental efforts at future Electron-Ion Colliders aimed at obtaining a rigorous quantitative understanding of confinement and the origin of nuclear mass.

</details>


### [25] [Twist-2 relations for the twist-3 tensor-polarized distribution function $f_{LT}$ of a spin-1 hadron by the operator-product-expansion method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00430)
*S. Kumano,Kenshi Kuroki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过局域算符乘积展开（local OPE）方法，独立推导出自旋-1强子中张量极化部分子分布函数（tensor-polarized PDFs）$f_{LT}$ 的 Wandzura-Wilczek（WW）类关系与 Burkhardt-Cottingham（BC）类求和规则，为正在美国杰斐逊实验室（JLab）准备的低 $Q^2$ 区电子-氘核深度非弹性散射实验提供理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于美国杰斐逊实验室（JLab）正在准备利用张量极化氘核靶测量电子-氘核深度非弹性散射（deep inelastic scattering）的截面，且实验将在较低 $Q^2$ 区进行，使得扭度-3（twist-3）贡献可能显著，因此需要从理论上深入理解自旋-1强子中张量极化部分子分布函数（tensor-polarized PDFs），特别是 $f_{LT}$ 的行为。

Method: 采用局域算符乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）方法，对自旋-1强子中张量极化 PDF $f_{LT}$ 的 Wandzura-Wilczek（WW）类关系及 Burkhardt-Cottingham（BC）类求和规则进行形式化推导，以此作为建立这些关系的可靠且独立的途径。

Result: 利用局域 OPE 方法，成功推导出 $f_{LT}$ 的 WW 类关系（将 $f_{LT}$ 用 $f_{1LL}$ 表示）以及 BC 类求和规则，这些结果与先前基于非局域算符得到的扭度-2（twist-2）关系一致，从而以独立方法验证了这些关系。

Conclusion: 局域 OPE 方法为自旋-1强子中 $f_{LT}$ 的 WW 类关系和 BC 类求和规则提供了可靠的形式化推导，确认了这些关系的有效性，为 JLab 即将开展的低 $Q^2$ 区张量极化深非弹性散射实验提供了必要的理论框架。

Abstract: In a spin-1 hadron, tensor-polarized parton distribution functions (PDFs) exist. The twist-2 function is $f_{1LL}$ and a twist-3 one is $f_{LT}$. Because an experiment is under preparation at the Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility (JLab) to measure the cross section of electron-deuteron deep inelastic scattering with the tensor-polarized deuteron target, these PDFs need to be understood theoretically. Especially, measurements will be done in a relatively low-$Q^2$ region at JLab, so that twist-3 contributions could become sizable in the cross section. In a previous work, a twist-2 relation was derived for $f_{LT}$ in terms of $f_{1LL}$ by using a nonlocal operator, and it corresponds to the Wandzura-Wilczek (WW) relation between $g_1$ and $g_2$. In addition, another relation similar to the Burkhardt-Cottingham (BC) sum rule was obtained. It is known that a formal way to derive the WW relation and the BC sum rule is to use the operator product expansion (OPE) with local operators. In this work, the WW-like relation and the BC-like sum rule for $f_{LT}$ are derived by using the local OPE method as a reliable independent way to establish these relations.

### [26] [Stability of parton distributions at high $x$: impact of nuclear and power corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00666)
*C. Cocuzza,W. Melnitchouk,N. Sato,A. W. Thomas*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于JAM贝叶斯蒙特卡洛框架，利用包括杰斐逊实验室高Bjorken-x深度非弹性散射数据在内的质子、氘核和A=3核数据，进行了一次全新的全局QCD分析，系统研究了部分子分布函数（PDFs）在不变质量截断、靶质量与高扭修正以及核波函数变化下的稳定性，并给出了相应的核效应预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全局QCD分析对高Bjorken-x区域的PDF约束不足，且对不变质量截断、靶质量修正、高扭修正及核波函数等系统误差的稳定性缺乏系统研究。

Method: 采用JAM贝叶斯蒙特卡洛（JAM Bayesian Monte Carlo）框架，对质子、氘核和A=3核的包含性深度非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering, DIS）数据进行全局QCD分析；系统变化DIS末态不变质量W的截断、靶质量与高扭修正的实现方式以及A=2和3核的核波函数。

Result: u和d夸克PDF（以及d/u比值）在x≈0.8以下相对稳定，可描述低至W²=3.5 GeV²和Q²=m_c²的DIS数据；在共线因子化框架内，高扭修正（higher twist corrections）为正且大致与同位旋无关；核数据描述需要非零的同位旋标量和同位旋矢量核子离壳PDF贡献。

Conclusion: 该分析验证了高x区域PDF的稳定性，并给出了氘核与同位旋标量核子结构函数之比R_D的具体预测。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive new global QCD analysis of unpolarized parton distribution functions (PDFs) based upon proton, deuteron and $A\!=\!3$ data, including the latest inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) measurements from Jefferson Lab at high Bjorken-$x$. Using the JAM Bayesian Monte Carlo framework, we systematically explore the stability of the PDFs with respect to variations in the cuts on the invariant mass $W$ of the DIS final state, the implementation of target mass and higher twist corrections, as well as on the nuclear wave functions for the $A\!=\!2$ and 3 data. We find the $u$ and $d$ quark PDFs (and the $d/u$ ratio) are relatively stable up to $x \approx 0.8$, and able to describe DIS data down to $W^2=3.5$ GeV$^2$ and $Q^2=m_c^2$. Within the collinear factorization framework, the fitted higher twist corrections to DIS are found to be positive, and largely isospin independent. The description of the nuclear data also requires nonzero isoscalar and isovector nucleon off-shell PDF contributions, which gives specific predictions for the ratio, $R_D$, of deuteron to isoscalar nucleon structure functions.

### [27] [Phenomenology of Hypothetical Single-Top Hadronic States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00748)
*Z. Rajabi Najjar,M. Ahmadi,K. Azizi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于双点QCD求和规则（two-point QCD sum rules），对包含单个顶夸克（top quark）的重子（baryon）和介子（meson）组态的质量进行了系统性理论计算，发现部分通道的中心质量略低于组分夸克质量之和，提示可能存在弱束缚（weak binding）或多夸克（multiquark）组态，为未来LHC及FCC等实验提供了第一性原理基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论动机是填补对含顶夸克强子系统（top-containing hadronic systems）质量的系统性第一性原理研究的空白；实验动机是CMS和ATLAS合作组在$t\bar t$阈值附近观测到的赝标量增强（pseudoscalar enhancement）现象。

Method: 采用双点QCD求和规则（two-point QCD sum rules）框架，同时纳入微扰贡献（perturbative contributions）和直至维数八（dimension eight）的非微扰凝聚项（nonperturbative condensates），提取相应基态（ground-state）质量。

Result: $Λ_t$、$Ξ_t$、$Σ_t$、$T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$及$T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{V}}$等通道的中心质量略低于相应组分夸克质量之和；在考虑完整理论不确定度后，更大范围的态一致呈现出弱束缚倾向。

Conclusion: 结果表明多数含顶夸克的重子和介子通道无法排除弱束缚组态的可能性，为LHC及未来对撞机（如FCC）搜索这类系统提供了第一性原理理论基准（first-principles theoretical benchmarks）。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive theoretical study of the masses of possible baryonic and mesonic configurations containing a single top quark. Our analysis includes the baryons $Λ_t$, $Ξ_t$, $Σ_t$, $Ξ'_t$, $Ω_t$, $Ω_{tcc}$, and $Ω_{tbb}$, together with the pseudoscalar and vector mesons $T_{t\bar n}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$, $T_{t\bar n}^{\mathrm{V}}$, $T_{t\bar s}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$, $T_{t\bar s}^{\mathrm{V}}$, $T_{t\bar c}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$, $T_{t\bar c}^{\mathrm{V}}$, $T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$, and $T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{V}}$. Motivated in part by recent experimental indications of a pseudoscalar enhancement near the $t\bar t$ threshold reported by the CMS and ATLAS collaborations, this study is carried out within the framework of two-point QCD sum rules to determine the corresponding ground-state masses by including perturbative contributions and nonperturbative condensates up to dimension eight. For several channels, including the $Λ_t$, $Ξ_t$, $Σ_t$, $T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{Ps}}$, and $T_{t\bar b}^{\mathrm{V}}$ states, the extracted central masses lie slightly below the corresponding sums of constituent quark masses, which may indicate nontrivial binding dynamics or near-threshold multiquark configurations within the uncertainties of the method. Moreover, when the full theoretical uncertainties are taken into account in a conservative manner, a larger subset of the investigated states exhibits a consistent tendency toward weak binding behavior, suggesting that the possibility of loosely bound configurations cannot be excluded for most of the considered baryonic and mesonic channels. These results provide useful first-principles theoretical benchmarks for possible top-containing hadronic systems, which may support future searches at the LHC, along with sensitivity analyses for next-generation facilities such as the FCC.

</details>


### [28] [Pre-inflationary QCD axion stars after moduli domination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00103)
*Edward Hardy,Noelia Sánchez González,Henry Stubbs,Lorenzo Tranchedone*

TL;DR: 该论文指出早期物质主导时期绝热密度扰动的增长，会在弦论启发的参数空间中引起前暴胀QCD轴子暗物质（pre-inflationary QCD axion dark matter）的$\mathcal{O}(1)$涨落；这些涨落与量子金斯尺度（quantum Jeans scale）在$\Lambda$CDM物质-辐射等值时重合，从而坍缩成孤子型“轴子星”（axion stars），其密度可达$10^4\,\mathrm{eV}^4$，连同周围晕体可贡献高达50%的暗物质，并通过瞬态增强或间接天体物理信号揭示非标准宇宙学历史。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索早期物质主导时期对前暴胀QCD轴子暗物质密度扰动的影响，并评估其在弦论（string theory）启发的参数空间中的观测后果。

Method: 基于绝热密度扰动在早期物质主导时期的增长理论，分析前暴胀QCD轴子暗物质的涨落行为；将扰动尺度与$\Lambda$CDM物质-辐射等值时的量子金斯尺度进行对比，确定坍缩条件。

Result: 扰动在物质-辐射等值时与量子金斯尺度重合，导致坍缩形成密度高达$10^4\,\mathrm{eV}^4$的轴子星；这些轴子星及其晕体可包含多达50%的暗物质。

Conclusion: 轴子质量$m_a\lesssim 10^{-5}\,{\rm eV}$时，平滑轴子背景的直接探测可能被抑制，但瞬态增强或间接天体物理信号可揭示非标准宇宙学历史（non-standard cosmological history）。

Abstract: The growth of adiabatic density perturbations during an era of early matter domination induces $\mathcal{O}(1)$ fluctuations in pre-inflationary QCD axion dark matter across a broad, string-theory-motivated parameter space. Remarkably, at $Λ$CDM matter-radiation equality the scale of these perturbations coincides with the quantum Jeans scale, so they collapse to solitonic ``axion stars''. These axion stars have densities up to $10^4\,\mathrm{eV}^4$, and, including their surrounding halos, they contain as much as $50\%$ of dark matter. Direct searches for a smooth axion background can be suppressed, but transient enhancements or indirect astrophysical signals at axion masses $m_a\lesssim 10^{-5}\,{\rm eV}$ would point to a non-standard cosmological history.

### [29] [Reciprocal symmetry and KNO scaling violation in proton-proton collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00128)
*Mustapha Ouchen,Alex Prygarin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析质子-质子碰撞中的带电粒子多重数分布，讨论KNO标度性（KNO scaling）的破坏，从实验数据中提取出KNO破坏修正中的互反对称性（reciprocal symmetry）$z\leftrightarrow 1/z$，并利用该对称性在低不确定度区域提取纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高能质子-质子碰撞中带电粒子多重数分布的特征，特别是KNO标度性的破坏机制，并寻找一种可靠的方法从中提取纠缠熵，以避免分布尾部大不确定性的干扰。

Method: 从ATLAS和CMS在$\sqrt{s}=7,\,8,\,13$~TeV的实验数据中提取KNO标度化概率偏离指数行为（exponential behavior）的修正，识别出互反对称性$z\leftrightarrow 1/z$，推导并验证该对称性在$n=\langle n\rangle$处对多重数分布施加的局部约束条件$P'(\langle n\rangle)=-P(\langle n\rangle)/\langle n\rangle$。

Result: 在实验数据中验证了KNO破坏修正中的互反对称性以及对应的局部约束条件；利用该约束从$n\simeq\langle n\rangle$的低不确定度区域成功提取了纠缠熵。

Conclusion: 互反对称性为从多重数分布中提取纠缠熵提供了一种有效且更精确的方法，避免了分布尾部大不确定性的影响。

Abstract: We analyze the charged particle multiplicity distributions in $p-p$ collisions and discuss the violation of the Koba--Nielsen--Olesen (KNO) scaling. We extract the deviations from the leading exponential behavior of the KNO scaled probability and identify a reciprocal symmetry $z\leftrightarrow 1/z$ in the KNO violating corrections observed in the ATLAS and CMS data at $\sqrt{s}=7,\,8,\,13$~TeV. The symmetry imposes a local constraint on the multiplicity distribution at $n=\langle n\rangle$, namely $P'(\langle n\rangle)=-P(\langle n\rangle)/\langle n\rangle$, which we verify directly in the data. We use this constraint to extract the entanglement entropy from the well-measured region $n\simeq\langle n\rangle$, avoiding the large uncertainties associated with the distribution tail.

</details>


### [30] [Micron-sized Extra Dimensions and Primordial Black Holes: Charges, Rotating, and Memory Burdened](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00252)
*George K. Leontaris,George Prampromis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨在具有两个额外维度的理论中，六维原初黑洞作为暗物质候选者的可行性，发现记忆负担机制为轻质原初黑洞暗物质打开了新的质量窗口，并提供了与Swampland约束、宇宙学、对撞机物理和低能现象学的统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索六维原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）作为暗物质（dark matter）解释的可能性，该理论中基本能标约为10 TeV，可被未来实验触及。

Method: 分析带电和旋转六维黑洞在标准霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）以及记忆负担（memory burden）两种场景下的演化与存活条件，并结合对撞机信号如未来环形对撞机（Future Circular Collider）中的高多重数事件进行约束。

Result: 纯霍金蒸发下仅质量大于10⁸ g的PBHs存活至今；近极端构型寿命延长因子为1/β^(1/2)。记忆负担场景中蒸发被极大抑制，亚克量级PBHs可存活至今，且产生平均多重数⟨N⟩~21的热谱信号。同时，Kaluza-Klein质量分裂Δm与大气中微子能标吻合。

Conclusion: 记忆负担机制为轻质原初黑洞暗物质开辟了新的质量窗口，并暗示了一个整合Swampland约束、宇宙学、对撞机物理与低能现象学的统一理论框架。

Abstract: We explore the possibility of explaining dark matter through six-dimensional (6D) primordial black holes (PBHs) in a theory with two extra dimensions. Interestingly, in this scenario the fundamental energy scale is of the order of $\sim 10$ TeV, accessible by future experiments. We analyse the viability of charged and rotating 6D black holes under standard Hawking evaporation as well as the memory burden scenario. In the case of pure Hawking evaporation, only PBHs with masses $M > 10^8$ g survive to present, while the lifetime of near-extremal configurations is extended by a factor $1/β^{1/2}$, where the parameter $β$ characterizes small deviations from extremality. In the memory burden scenario evaporation is enormously suppressed, and sub-gram mass PBHs can survive to the present epoch. At future colliders such as the Future Circular Collider, these micro black holes produce characteristic high multiplicity events, $\langle N \rangle \sim 21$, with thermal spectra, enabling direct probes of the fundamental scale and the number of extra dimensions. We find that the memory burden mechanism opens a broad new mass window for light PBH dark matter, while the Kaluza-Klein mass splitting $Δm$ aligns with the atmospheric neutrino scale, suggesting a unified framework between Swampland constraints, cosmology, collider physics, and low energy phenomenology.

</details>

It has been proven that any negative periodic perturbation of the equilibrium dynamics generator shifts the spectrum to the left half-plane and, consequently, such a perturbation of mortality leads to the population extinction in any dimension.

### [33] [Understanding Energy Flow and Inefficiency of a Thermomagnetic Generator by Transient Multi-Physics Modelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00017)
*Ali Izadi,Bruno Neumann,Sebastian Fähler*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过多物理场仿真构建了一种属3拓扑的热磁发电机（thermomagnetic generator, TMG）的数字孪生（digital twin），在开路电压和功率输出上分别达到96%和95%的实验验证精度，并利用该模型揭示了TMG效率低和循环频率低两大挑战的根源——通过桑基图（Sankey diagram）分析能量流向以定位低效环节，通过瞬态热流追踪以识别限制频率的因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业及环境中的低温废热（low-grade waste heat）大量浪费，而传统技术回收效率低或不可行。热磁发电机（TMG）因几乎无机械运动部件而具有高可靠性潜力，但现有原型机仍面临效率低和循环频率低两大挑战，且实验手段无法直接揭示其根源。

Method: 采用多物理场仿真（multi-physics simulations）构建属3拓扑TMG的数字孪生（digital twin），在三维空间中耦合磁、热、流体流动和电四个物理域。模型仅使用已知几何与材料参数，并通过当前功率密度最高的TMG实验数据验证。

Result: 仿真模型在开路电压（open-circuit voltage）上达到96%的精度，在功率输出（power output）上达到95%的精度。借助该高精度模型，通过桑基图（Sankey diagram）分析能量流向揭示了低效来源，通过追踪瞬态热流（transient heat flow）确定了限制循环频率的因素。

Conclusion: 所开发的经过验证的数字孪生为设计更高效、更快速的TMG铺平了道路，可加速未来TMG的开发进程。

Abstract: Waste heat recovery improves energy efficiency and reduces greenhouse gas emissions; however, much industrial and environmental heat is wasted at low temperature. Thermomagnetic recovery of waste heat has a high potential for sustainable production of electric energy, especially for low-grade waste heat where conventional technology is inefficient or infeasible. Of particular interest are thermomagnetic generators (TMG) as they require almost no mechanically moving parts, which is beneficial for high reliability. However, all existing prototypes have two remaining challenges: low efficiency and low cycle frequency. In this work, we develop a digital twin of a recent TMG with genus 3 by using multi-physics simulations. We identify shortcomings of previous simulation approaches, and describe why simulations in three dimensions are necessary, which consider coupling between magnetic, thermal, fluid flow, and electrical physics domains. We validate our model, which only uses known geometry and material parameters, by experimental data of the TMG with highest power density today, and attain 96% accuracy in open-circuit voltage and 95% accuracy in power output. This high accuracy allows us to identify the origin of both challenges for TMGs, which are not accessible by experiments. First, we uncover inefficiencies by analyzing the energy flow within a Sankey diagram. Second, we trace the transient heat flow through the generator, which identifies the factors limiting frequency. This paves the way for more efficient and faster TMGs, and their development will be accelerated by our validated digital twin.

### [34] [Programmable Integrated Magnonic Meshes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00290)

Result: 实现了自旋波在波导结构中高效传播数百个波长且保持相位相干性；在耦合波导中观察到完整且周期性的功率转移；移相器实现了任意可调相位延迟。通过级联这些元件，实现了可编程分束器、频率解复用器和相位控制2x2路由器，并进一步构建了多达六输入六输出、七级级联的可编程磁子干涉网格，无需中间放大。

Conclusion: 该直接写入级联网络填补了磁子学可扩展性方面的长期空白，为集成大规模磁子架构在经典与量子处理中的应用提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Integrated circuits are a cornerstone of modern information technology, and analog wave-based architectures could enable fast and efficient processing beyond conventional charge electronics. In magnonics, spin waves provide a highly tunable, compact and energy-efficient medium for on-chip microwave signal transport and processing. However, progress has been limited to isolated elements or short devices, severely limiting the overall functional complexity and scalability. Here we realize the key elements of universal magnonic circuitry, using a single-step direct laser writing process in yttrium iron garnet, and monolithically cascade them in multi-stage programmable devices and networks. Using magneto-optical Kerr effect microscopy, we show efficient spin-wave propagation and preserved phase coherence in waveguide structures for hundreds of wavelengths. In coupled waveguides, we observe complete and periodic power transfer over several coupling lengths, and in phase shifters we achieve arbitrary, tunable phase delays. By cascading these elements, we realize programmable splitters, frequency demultiplexers, and phase-controlled 2x2 routers, where output power and relative phase can be programmed on demand via external fields. Finally, we realize programmable magnonic interferometric meshes for on-chip radio-frequency signal routing, with up to six magnonic inputs and outputs and seven cascaded stages, without the need for intermediate amplification. These direct-write cascaded networks bridge a long-standing gap in magnonic scalability, offering a viable pathway toward integrated, large-scale architectures for both classical and quantum processing.

By utilizing topological numbers, different black hole systems can be categorized into distinct universality classes. This universal classification is particularly evident in thermodynamic limits, offering valuable insights for developing a comprehensive quantum gravity framework. This review highlights the latest advancements in this field. Specifically, we outline fundamental topological frameworks underlying black hole solutions, critical points, Davies points, and the Hawking-Page phase transition. For each scenario, we calculate the associated topological numbers and analyze their physical significance. Furthermore, we explore the practical implications arising from this research.

### [37] [Quantum Noise Fraction and the Thermal Frontier in High-Frequency Gravitational Wave Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00053)
*Sergio Gaudio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个诊断量——量子噪声分数 β——用于确定引力波探测器通过量子增强所能达到的最大灵敏度提升。通过对高频（kHz-GHz）探测器的分析发现，在约230 MHz以下频率，共振质量探测器处于热噪声主导区域（β≈0），只有突破热前沿（ℏω = k_B T ln 3）后才进入量子区域。作者识别出一种具体实现：1 GHz、10 mK的体声波共振器（β = 0.98），并提出基于电路QED读出的压缩声子态引力波探测器方案。即使10^4个此类共振器阵列达到10 dB机械压缩，其灵敏度仍比大爆炸核合成（BBN）对随机背景的约束高出约10^9倍，表明灵敏度差距主要是经典性质的，需要同步提升经典探测器参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高频引力波探测器的量子增强策略缺乏统一的理论限度评估。本文旨在提出一个通用的诊断量 β，量化各类探测器在给定频率和温度下通过量子技术（如压缩态和纠缠态）所能获得的最高灵敏度改善，从而指导实验设计。

Method: 定义量子噪声分数 β，通过比较热噪声与量子噪声的相对大小来判定探测器的量子可增强性。将 β 应用于多种高频（kHz–GHz）引力波探测器提案，包括潮汐耦合的共振质量探测器，并基于热前沿条件（ℏω = k_B T ln 3）划定量子可及区域。针对体声波共振器（BAW resonator）具体设计，采用电路QED（circuit QED）读出机制实现压缩声子态（squeezed phononic states）。

Result: 在稀释制冷温度下，所有频率低于约230 MHz的共振质量探测器均处于热噪声主导区域（β≈0），压缩态和纠缠态的量子增强效果极为有限；仅在热前沿以上，量子区域才可进入。具体实现上，1 GHz、10 mK的体声波共振器达到 β = 0.98。由10^4个此类共振器组成的阵列，在10 dB机械压缩下达到灵敏度 √S_h = 7.6×10⁻²⁶/√Hz，但该值仍比1 GHz处BBN对随机引力波背景的约束高约10^9倍。

Conclusion: 高频引力波探测中的灵敏度差距主要源于经典噪声源，而非量子极限。量子增强（如机械压缩）尽管可以提升性能，但并不能替代经典参数（如质量、耦合强度、热隔离）的进步。未来需要经典与量子技术协同发展，才能弥合当前灵敏度与BBN约束之间的巨大差距。

Abstract: We introduce a diagnostic -- the quantum noise fraction $β$ -- that determines the maximum sensitivity improvement achievable through quantum enhancement for any gravitational wave detector. Applied to the landscape of proposed high-frequency (kHz-GHz) detectors, this diagnostic reveals that resonant mass detectors operating through tidal coupling are thermally dominated ($β\approx 0$) at all frequencies below ~230 MHz at dilution temperatures, rendering squeezing and entanglement limited in effectiveness. Only above this thermal frontier, defined by $\hbar ω= k_B T \ln 3$, does the quantum regime become accessible. We identify a single concrete realization: a bulk acoustic wave resonator at 1 GHz and 10 mK ($β= 0.98$), and propose a gravitational wave detector employing squeezed phononic states via circuit QED readout. An array of $10^4$ such resonators with 10 dB mechanical squeezing reaches $\sqrt{S_h} = 7.6 \times 10^{-26}/\sqrt{\rm Hz}$ -- still a factor ~$10^9$ above the BBN bound on stochastic backgrounds at 1 GHz, indicating that the sensitivity gap remains predominantly classical in origin and that concurrent advances in classical detector parameters will be required.

### [38] [The formalism of energy conservation during particle decay in the Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00114)
*Shurui Zhang,Remo Ruffini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中推导了双粒子相对洛伦兹因子（relative Lorentz factor）的紧致协变表达式，并应用于克尔时空（Kerr spacetime）中的粒子衰变过程。通过局域质心系（local center-of-mass frame）的能量守恒分析表明，母粒子静止质量的损失必须转化为衰变产物的动能；该关系在三个代表性彭罗斯过程（Penrose process）算例中得到解析验证和高精度数值确认（达到机器精度）。这些结果澄清了旋转黑洞能量提取过程中的局域运动学机制，并指出质量损失是衰变产物分离的必要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对弯曲时空中粒子衰变过程的局域能量-动量守恒（local energy-momentum conservation）关系缺乏清晰的协变描述，尤其是在克尔黑洞背景下，质量损失与动能转化之间的必要性尚未被严格证明和验证。

Method: 推导了弯曲时空中两粒子相对洛伦兹因子的紧致协变表达式；利用该表达式在克尔时空框架下建立局域质心系能量守恒方程，将母粒子的静止质量损失与衰变产物动能联系起来，并通过三个代表性彭罗斯过程算例进行解析分析和高精度数值验证。

Result: 母粒子的静止质量损失必须转化为衰变产物的动能，才能在局域质心系中满足能量守恒；该关系在三个彭罗斯过程示例中得到解析确认，且两种等价的守恒公式均达到机器精度。

Conclusion: 本文从局域运动学角度阐明了旋转黑洞能量提取的机制，指出质量损失不是可选的，而是衰变产物能够分离的必要条件。

Abstract: We derive a compact, covariant expression for the relative Lorentz factor of two particles in curved spacetime and apply it to particle decay in Kerr spacetime. This allows us to show that energy conservation in the local center-of-mass frame requires the rest-mass loss of the parent particle to be converted into kinetic energy of the decay products. We verify this relation analytically and confirm it with high-precision reconstructions of three representative Penrose-process examples, for which both equivalent conservation formulas are satisfied to machine precision. These results clarify the local kinematics underlying energy extraction from rotating black holes and show that mass loss is not optional but is required for the decay products to separate.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确的并合残留模型对引力波科学日益重要，包括利用 ringdown 进行引力精确检验、黑洞种群推断和层次并合建模。偏心双星（eccentric binaries）的残留质量、自旋和反冲携带非平凡的偏心印记，在物理上有丰富信息但建模更具挑战，且发展尚不如准圆形（quasi-circular）情形成熟。

Method: 两个模型均基于数值 relativity 模拟训练，覆盖三维参数空间：质量比 $q \leq 4$、偏心率 $e < 0.23$ 以及平均 anomaly $\ell \in [0,2π)$ 弧度（$e$ 和 $\ell$ 均在相对于峰值振幅时刻 $t=-1000M$ 处定义，$M$ 为总质量）。NRSurE_q4NoSpin_Remnant 预测残留性质，NRSurE_q4NoSpin_Dynamics 是描述偏心率与平均 anomaly 时域演化的代理模型（surrogate）。

Result: 模型展示了偏心对残留性质的现象学影响，包括反冲（recoil）的增强或抑制；所有建模量均提供误差估计（error estimates），以支持当前及未来引力波参数估计（parameter-estimation）分析中的可靠使用。

Conclusion: 两个模型将通过开源代码公开发布，为偏心双黑洞并合残留性质的精确建模提供工具，推动引力波数据分析与物理推断。

Abstract: Accurate models of merger remnants are increasingly important for gravitational-wave science, including precision tests of gravity with ringdown, inference of black-hole populations, and modeling hierarchical mergers. For eccentric binaries, remnant mass, spin, and recoil carry nontrivial imprints of eccentricity that are both physically informative and more challenging to model, yet remain less developed than in the quasi-circular case. We present two new models trained on numerical-relativity (NR) simulations of unequal-mass, non-spinning eccentric binary black holes: NRSurE_q4NoSpin_Remnant, which predicts remnant properties, and NRSurE_q4NoSpin_Dynamics, a time-domain surrogate for the evolution of eccentricity and mean anomaly. Both models are trained on NR simulations over a three-dimensional parameter space with mass ratios $q \leq 4$, eccentricity $e < 0.23$, and mean anomaly $\ell \in [0,2π)$ radians, where both $e$ and $\ell$ defined at $t=-1000M$ relative to peak amplitude and $M$ is the total mass. We highlight some applications, including the phenomenological impact of eccentricity on remnant properties and the enhancement or suppression of recoil. We also provide error estimates for all modeled quantities, supporting reliable use in current and future gravitational-wave parameter-estimation analyses. Both models will be made available through open-source codes.

</details>


### [40] [Generalized First Law and Smarr Formula: Beyond Additivity and Extensivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00381)

Method: 为一般球对称时空（spherically symmetric spacetime）在广义熵模型下推导了黑洞热力学第一定律及Smarr关系；同时构建了广义Ruppeiner热力学几何（generalized Ruppeiner thermodynamic geometry），并解析确定了曲率标量（curvature scalar）的通用形式。以Reissner-Nordström黑洞为例，分析了其极值与非极值相变。

Result: 符合Abè型组合规则（Abè-type composition rule）的熵模型导致热力学曲率（thermodynamic curvature）为零，而违背该规则的模型则表现出曲率发散（curvature divergences）现象。

Conclusion: 曲率发散与否可作为检验广义熵模型一致性的几何判据（geometric test），为区分不同熵模型的物理合理性提供了新工具。

Abstract: The study of black hole thermodynamics becomes a central topic in gravitational physics, where the first law and the Smarr relation establish a deep connection between spacetime geometry and thermodynamic laws. As we know, these relations depend on the entropy; any modification to the entropy arising from quantum gravity or generalized statistical mechanics may impact the basic thermodynamic framework of black holes. In this work, we develop a general framework for deriving the first law of black hole thermodynamics and the associated Smarr relation for generic spherically symmetric spacetime under a wide class of generalized entropy models. In addition, a generalized Ruppeiner thermodynamic geometry is developed to utilize the generalized entropy model, from which the curvature scalar is determined in a general form. To demonstrate this framework, we assume the Resinser-Nordström black hole and investigate the corresponding extremal and non-extremal phase transition. Interestingly, our analysis reveals that entropy models consistent with the Abè-type composition rule result in a vanishing thermodynamic curvature, whereas violations of this rule exhibit curvature divergences, suggesting a geometric test for the consistency of generalized entropy models.

### [41] [Gravitational particle production, the cosmological tensions and fast radio bursts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.19770)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于引力真空极化（gravitational vacuum polarization）效应，修正了先前工作中对哈勃常数（Hubble constant）测量的误认，并将分析扩展到σ₈张力和快速射电暴（fast radio bursts）观测。研究发现该效应不影响σ₈张力，但可缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension），并预言快速射电暴测得的哈勃常数与CMB/BAO测量值一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>
