Conclusion: 引力真空极化效应可能区分不同类型的哈勃常数测量差异，但对σ₈张力无实质影响，支持了关于σ₈张力可能并非真实存在的观点。未来可通过更高精度的快速射电暴观测对模型预言进行验证。

Abstract: In [26] it had been found that gravitational particle production (to be more specific, gravitational vacuum polarization) results in an effective increase in the directly measured value of the Hubble constant $H_0$ while it does not affect the value of the Hubble constant derived from energy densities $\bar{H}_0$. It had also been pointed out that this may explain why the Hubble constant $H_0$ determined from direct measurements (such as in SN Ia measurements) and the Hubble constant determined from indirect measurements (such as in CMB calculations in the framework of $Λ$CDM) are different. In the present study, first I correct a misidentification in \cite{Erdem-Universe}, namely, $\hat{H}_0=\left(\frac{\bar{H}_0}{H_0}\right)\bar{H}_0$ (rather than $\bar{H}_0$) is the value of the Hubble constant measured in CMB and BAO measurements. Then I extend the analysis to the $σ_8$ tension, and to determination of the Hubble constant through observations of fast radio bursts. It is observed that inclusion of the effect of gravitational vacuum polarization essentially does not neither mitigate nor exacerbate the $σ_8$ tension (while it mitigates or relieves the Hubble tension). This result is significant in the light of the studies in literature that question existence of a true $σ_8$ tension. Moreover, the present framework predicts that the value of the Hubble constant measured in fast radio bursts is $\hat{H}_0$ as in CMB and BAO measurements. This may be checked with observations in future after more precise and conclusive measurements of $\hat{H}_0$, $\bar{H}_0$, $H_0$.

### [42] [Time-slicing quantum spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00520)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于ADM形式（ADM formalism）的时空分解，将每个空间切片替换为量子黎曼几何，构造时空量子Levi-Civita联络。对模糊球面等空间代数族以及任意时变空间量子度规、位移1-形式（shift 1-form）和时滞函数（lapse function）进行完全求解。

Result: 当空间度规按一阶常微分方程（first order ODE）随时间演化时，结果呈现特别简单的形式；对模糊球面而言，这要求空间度规根据每个时刻$t$的位移向量值进行旋转。此外，完全求解了用离散圆环替代角向的旋转不变时空情形，包括一个新型$\Bbb Z_n$-FLRW模型。

Conclusion: 该构造原则上为大多数（伪）黎曼流形（(pseudo)-Riemannian manifolds）提供了模糊版本（fuzzy versions），从而为弯曲时空量子场论的量子几何推广奠定了代数基础。

Abstract: For quantum field theory on curved spacetimes, a critical role is played by their foliation into spacelike time-slices at each value $t$ of a coordinate time, with corresponding metric in ADM form. We provide a general construction for the spacetime quantum Levi-Civita connection when each spatial slice is replaced by a quantum Riemannian geometry. This is then fully solved for a class of spatial algebras including fuzzy spheres and for any time-dependent spatial quantum metric, shift 1-form and lapse function. The result takes a particularly simple form if the spatial metric evolves in time according to a first order ODE which, in the case of a fuzzy sphere, requires the spatial metric to rotate in time according to the value at each $t$ of the shift vector. As an application, our results provide in principle fuzzy versions of most (pseudo)-Riemannian manifolds. We also fully solve the case of rotationally invariant spacetimes with angular directions replaced by a discrete circle, including a new $\Bbb Z_n$-FLRW model.

Abstract: A modified gravitational model whose action is given by an arbitrary function of the Ricci scalar, the matter Lagrangian density, a scalar field, and its kinetic term is investigated as an extension of the gravitational sector including an additional dynamical degree of freedom. Within this framework, the causal structure of rotating cosmological solutions is analyzed by considering Gödel and Gödel-type spacetimes as background geometries used as theoretical probes of the model consistency. Different matter sources are examined, including a perfect fluid and scalar-field configurations. It is found that the standard Gödel metric is not compatible with the scalar sector of the theory unless the model reduces to the General Relativity limit. In particular, perfect-fluid sources may lead to either causal or noncausal configurations, whereas scalar-field configurations constrain the geometry to the causal limit, preventing the formation of closed timelike curves, highlighting that the scalar field plays a nontrivial dynamical role distinct from that of a cosmological constant.

### [44] [Scalar emission from binary neutron stars in scalar-tensor theories with kinetic screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00580)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过3+1数值模拟，研究了具有动力学屏蔽（kinetic screening）的平移对称标量-张量理论中双中子星的标量辐射。研究发现动力学屏蔽对标量四极矩辐射具有非单调作用——在特定条件下抑制或增强辐射，且该行为对引力波检验引力理论具有潜在影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力理论中，标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories）因动力学屏蔽机制可能绕过太阳系约束，但双致密星系统中的标量辐射行为尚不清楚。本文旨在通过数值模拟填补这一空白，揭示动力学屏蔽对标量发射的非单调影响及其对引力波检验的启示。

Method: 采用3+1数值模拟，在退耦极限（decoupling limit）下研究具有动力学屏蔽的平移对称标量-张量理论（$K$-essence）中的双中子星标量发射。为构建屏蔽半径$r_*$远大于轨道间距的静态双星初值，引入静态场方程的双曲化（hyperbolization）方法，以规避直接时间演化中Keldysh型不稳定性（Keldysh-type breakdown）。

Result: 等质量双星中标量发射由$\ell=m=2$模主导；动力学屏蔽对标量辐射具有非单调作用：当波长$\lambda_{22}\ll r_*$时辐射被抑制，而当$\lambda_{22}\gtrsim r_*$时辐射被增强（相对于Fierz-Jordan-Brans-Dicke理论）。非等质量双星中标量偶极子重新出现，其幅度随质量不对称性线性增长，而四极屏蔽在质量比$\sim 0.6$以上仍接近等质量情形。

Conclusion: 发现的动力学屏蔽非单调行为对基于引力波的引力检验具有潜在意义。对于相对论性双脉冲星（double pulsar），要求$r_*\gg 10^9$~km才能有效抑制标量四极矩；而对于宇宙学动机的$\Lambda$参数，$r_*\sim 10^{11}$~km（对太阳质量源），仅能提供中等程度的抑制。

Abstract: We investigate the scalar emission from binary neutron stars in shift-symmetric scalar-tensor theories with kinetic screening ($K$-essence), using 3+1 numerical simulations in the decoupling limit. To construct static binary initial data in the regime where the screening radius $r_*$ greatly exceeds the orbital separation, we introduce a hyperbolization of the static field equations that bypasses the Keldysh-type breakdown affecting direct time evolutions. For equal-mass binaries, where the scalar emission is dominated by the $\ell=m=2$ mode, kinetic screening acts non-monotonically on the scalar radiation, suppressing or enhancing the quadrupolar amplitude depending on the relative size of $r_*$ and $λ_{22}$ (with $λ_{22}$ the wavelength): for $λ_{22}\ll r_*$ it is suppressed relative to the Fierz-Jordan-Brans-Dicke (FJBD) case, while for $λ_{22}\gtrsim r_*$ it is amplified above FJBD. For unequal-mass binaries a scalar dipole re-emerges, growing linearly with the mass asymmetry, while the quadrupolar screening remains close to the equal-mass case down to mass ratios $\sim 0.6$. The non-monotonic behavior of kinetic screening that we uncover has potential implications for gravitational-wave-based tests of gravity. The relativistic double pulsar, in particular, requires $r_*\gg 10^9$~km to efficiently suppress the scalar quadrupole; for cosmologically-motivated $Λ$, $r_*\sim 10^{11}$~km (for a solar-mass source), giving only moderate suppression.

### [45] [Non-Supersymmetric Baryogenesis from $U(1)$-Breaking Scalar Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00606)
*Surendra Kumar Gour,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非超对称的重子生成机制（baryogenesis），通过具有显式破缺U(1)对称性的广义自相互作用势的复标量场（complex scalar field）的非线性动力学，从对称初始条件动态产生非零的Noether荷密度（Noether charge density），进而在晚期产生恒定的重子-光子比（baryon-to-photon ratio）。三种势形式中，一种参数空间宽泛，一种要求非现实的质量压低，第三种则具有与标量质量无关的良好可预测性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑三类显式破缺全局U(1)对称性的广义自相互作用势，分析复标量场分量演化的非线性源项（nonlinear source terms），证明其能从对称初始条件动态生成非零Noether荷密度，并通过动力学冻入（dynamical freeze-in）机制在晚期使重子-光子比趋于恒定。

Conclusion: 该非超对称机制在假设生成的电荷不对称性能高效转移至标准模型（Standard Model）扇区且冲刷效应（washout effects）可忽略的前提下，能够解释观测到的宇宙重子不对称性。不同势形式的定量特征差异明显，其中第三类势因质量无关性而最具预测性和能标兼容性。

Abstract: We present a non-supersymmetric mechanism for baryogenesis driven by the nonlinear dynamics of a complex scalar field with generalized self-interaction potentials that explicitly break the global $U(1)$ symmetry. Specifically, three representative forms of the interaction potential are considered, which give rise to intricate nonlinear source terms in the evolution of the field components. In all cases, we show that these nonlinear source terms dynamically generate a nonzero Noether charge density from symmetric initial conditions, providing a purely dynamical origin of charge asymmetry. At late times, the charge density scales as $\sim t^{-3/2}$, leading to a constant baryon-to-photon ratio through dynamical freeze-in. While the qualitative behavior is robust across models, the quantitative features depend sensitively on the interaction structure. We find that one class of potentials yields a viable parameter space over a wide range of scalar masses, whereas another requires unrealistically suppressed mass scales. A third scenario stands out in that the final asymmetry is independent of the scalar mass and depends only on the coupling parameter, enhancing predictivity and allowing compatibility across a broad range of energy scales. Assuming efficient transfer of the generated asymmetry to the Standard Model sector and negligible washout effects, the mechanism can account for the observed baryon asymmetry.

### [46] [Dynamical tidal Love numbers of black holes under generic perturbations: Connecting black hole perturbation theory with effective field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00693)
*Sumanta Chakraborty,M. V. S Saketh,Tanja Hinderer,Jan Steinhoff*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为描述双致密星系统中内部结构与动力学及引力波辐射之间的耦合，需要建立系统的有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）框架，将每个致密天体替换为携带内部自由度的世界线（worldline），以编码有限大小效应（finite-size effects）并区分不同类型的致密天体。

Method: 该方法通过建立受扰动黑洞的EFT描述，将自旋、引力电（gravitoelectric）和引力磁（gravitomagnetic）潮汐场之间的耦合纳入框架；随后将EFT与完整黑洞扰动方程的波动解（wave-like solutions）进行匹配（matching），以确定潮汐响应系数。

Result: 获得了旋转黑洞在线性频率阶出现的动力学Love数，并推导了包含耗散（dissipative）和保守（conservative）部分的动力学潮汐响应的近似表达式；同时揭示了由致密天体自旋引起的多极模混合（mixing of multipolar modes）对一致处理的关键作用。

Conclusion: 匹配过程中存在的若干技术细节（尤其是自旋诱导的多极模混合）对于潮汐响应系数的一致确定至关重要，这为更精确地建模双致密星系统的潮汐相互作用及其引力波信号奠定了基础。

Abstract: The foundation for modeling the coupling of the internal structure of compact objects in binary systems to their dynamics and emitted gravitational waves is a systematic effective field theory (EFT) framework, where each compact object is replaced by a worldline endowed with a set of internal degrees of freedom. These degrees of freedom encode finite-size effects and thereby distinguish between different classes of compact objects. Among finite-size effects, tidal interactions play a central role, as they are associated to various kinds of deformations of a body under the influence of external tidal fields. In this work, we analyze the dynamical tidal response of Kerr black holes to generic-spin perturbations, focusing primarily on the scalar and gravitational cases, and working to linear order in frequency. We establish an EFT description of the perturbed black hole that accounts for the couplings between the spin, gravitoelectric and -magnetic tidal fields. We match this to wave-like solutions to the full black hole perturbation equations in order to determine the tidal response coefficients. In particular, we obtain the dynamical Love number, which appears at linear order in frequency for spinning black holes, and derive an approximate expression for the dynamical tidal response, including both dissipative and conservative pieces. We also examine several technical subtleties that arise in the matching procedure, with special emphasis on the mixing of multipolar modes induced by the spin of the compact object, which proves to be essential for a consistent treatment.

</details>


### [47] [Entanglement probes of gravitational Kaluza-Klein spectra: signal hierarchy and model discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00749)
*Yi Zhong,Tao-Tao Sui,Ke Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子引力诱导的纠缠质量（QGEM）作为探测亚毫米距离上牛顿势的额外维度修正的相位敏感探针，比较了三种卡鲁扎-克莱因（Kaluza-Klein）谱情景（RSII、ADD 和 Pöschl-Teller 势模型），发现在 40–80 μm 范围内信号层次为 ADD > gapped > RSII，且通过相位响应的距离扫描可区分 RSII 与 ADD/gapped，但 ADD 与有隙连续谱在归一化轮廓上几乎不可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用量子引力效应（如纠缠相位）作为探针，检测亚毫米尺度上牛顿势的额外维度修正，并区分不同的卡鲁扎-克莱因谱结构。

Method: 比较三种代表性卡鲁扎-克莱因谱情景：Randall-Sundrum II (RSII) 模型、Arkani-Hamed-Dimopoulos-Dvali (ADD) 模型，以及由 Pöschl-Teller 势建模的有隙连续谱（gapped continuum）。在 d=40–80 μm 范围内，依据当前短程引力测试的基准参数，计算纠缠相位、并发度（concurrence）和归一化相位响应轮廓。

Result: 在该距离窗口内，信号强度呈现稳定层次：ADD > gapped > RSII。保守参数下，ADD 信号在较小间距时超过名义纠缠阈值，gapped 基准仅在窗口低端可分辨，RSII 始终低于阈值；更乐观的近景参数下，三种谱信号均显著超过阈值。归一化距离扫描的相位响应可清晰区分 RSII 与 ADD 及 gapped 情况，但 ADD 与有隙连续谱在归一化轮廓上几乎无法区分。

Conclusion: 量子引力诱导纠缠质量（QGEM）的相位观测量可作为亚毫米尺度上卡鲁扎-克莱因谱结构的互补判别工具，但其对 ADD 与有隙连续谱的鉴别能力有限。

Abstract: Quantum-gravity-induced entanglement of masses (QGEM) provides a phase-sensitive probe of extra-dimensional corrections to the Newtonian potential at submillimeter separations. We compare three representative Kaluza-Klein spectral scenarios: the Randall-Sundrum II (RSII) and Arkani-Hamed-Dimopoulos-Dvali (ADD) models, and the case of a gapped continuum modeled by a Pöschl-Teller potential. We evaluate the entangling phase, concurrence, and normalized phase-response profiles over $d=40$-$80\,μ\mathrm{m}$ using representative benchmark parameters guided by current short-range gravity tests. In this range, the signal exhibits a stable hierarchy: ADD $>$ gapped $>$ RSII. For conservative experimental parameters, the ADD signal surpasses the nominal entanglement threshold at smaller separations, whereas the gapped benchmark is resolvable only at the lower end of the window, and RSII remains below resolution. In a more optimistic near-term scenario, all three spectral signatures comfortably exceed the threshold. We further show that normalized distance scans of the phase response clearly separate the RSII benchmark from the ADD and gapped cases, whereas ADD and the gapped continuum remain nearly indistinguishable in normalized profile. QGEM phase observables therefore provide a complementary discriminator of Kaluza-Klein spectral structure at submillimeter scales.

### [48] [Locality versus Fock-space structure in East-type models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00091)
*Achilleas Lazarides*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究量子East模型的变体：受随机矩阵理论启发，将Fock空间中的连接随机化（实空间非局域化），同时保留磁化近邻扇区结构。结果发现仍存在从退局域化相到局域化相的转变，表明对于East型约束模型，关键因素是Fock空间的图结构而非自旋翻转的几何局域性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究量子多体系统中局域动力学约束（local kinetic constraints）如何导致慢动力学或完全多体局域化（many-body localisation），并厘清Fock空间连接结构与几何局域性何者更为关键。

Method: 对量子East模型（quantum East model）进行修改，借鉴随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）将Fock空间中的连接随机化，使其在实空间中变为非局域（nonlocal），同时保留各磁化（magnetisation）近邻扇区的组织方式。

Result: 修改后的模型仍存在两个截然不同的相：一个退局域化相（delocalised phase）和一个局域化相（localised phase），相变特征得以保留。

Conclusion: 对于East型约束模型（East-type constrained models），决定局域化行为的关键因素是Fock空间中的图结构（graph structure），而非自旋翻转在几何空间中的局域性（geometric locality）。

Abstract: Local kinetic constraints in quantum many-body systems can generate slow dynamics or complete many-body localisation. Here we focus on a modification of the quantum East model: Inspired by random matrix theory, we randomise the connectivity in Fock space (rendering it nonlocal in real space) while preserving its organisation into neighbouring magnetisation sectors. We find that there is still a transition between two distinct phases, one delocalised and the other localised. We conclude that, for East-type constrained models, the essential ingredient is the structure of the graph in Fock space rather than geometric locality of spin flips.

Result: 遗传算法在所有实验场景下均能准确恢复参考参数，XGBoost精调则在较简单场景中显著提升了参数估计的准确性。

Conclusion: 该混合计算框架为难测量的野火参数提供了系统化的估计方法，展示了混合计算方法在野火建模与森林管理中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Wildfires are among the most severe disturbances affecting forest ecosystems, with over 50,000 hectares burned in Patagonia, Argentina, during 2025 alone. This study implements a Reaction-Diffusion-Convection (RDC) model to simulate wildfire spread in the Steffen and Martin Lakes area, a region severely impacted by fires. By integrating high-resolution maps of slope, wind velocity, and vegetation, we conducted three computational experiments of increasing complexity to simulate fire propagation across heterogeneous landscapes.
  We employed a Genetic Algorithm (GA) to recover reference model parameters by maximizing the spatial overlap between simulated and reference burned areas. Subsequently, parameter estimates were refined using XGBoost to improve accuracy. Results demonstrate that the GA accurately recovers reference parameters across all scenarios, while the XGBoost fine-tuning significantly enhances accuracy in simpler cases. This integrated framework offers a systematic approach for estimating difficult-to-measure wildfire parameters, demonstrating the potential of hybrid computational methods for wildfire modeling and forest management.

### [50] [Parity-dependent reentrant topology in a Su--Schrieffer--Heeger chain with power-law quasiperiodic modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00543)
*Yusheng Niu,Hui Liu,Zhihao Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链中由幂律准周期调制的胞内跳跃导致的再入拓扑相变，揭示了奇偶性依赖的再入拓扑相形成机制，并给出了零模逆局域化长度的精确解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链中，由幂律准周期调制的胞内跳跃（intracell hopping）所引发的再入拓扑相变（reentrant topological transitions），特别是调制函数形式（光滑幂律极限与符号函数极限之间的插值）对拓扑相图的影响。

Method: 结合零模逆局域化长度（zero-mode inverse localization length）的解析计算与实空间拓扑指标（real-space topological indicator）的数值评估，分析β→0、β→∞以及有限β三种情况下的拓扑相图。对n=1,2,3,4情形给出逆局域化长度的精确解析表达式。

Result: 确定性准周期调制可在有限参数窗口内诱导类似拓扑安德森绝缘体（TAI-like）的再入拓扑相。再入拓扑的形成依赖于指数n的奇偶性：奇次幂调制可从清洁平庸区|t₁|>1诱导再入，而偶次幂调制仅能从负清洁平庸区t₁<-1诱导再入。有限β结果表明奇偶依赖结构在两极限情况间的插值过程中保持稳健。

Conclusion: 再入拓扑相的奇偶效应源于调制是否保留或移除cos x的符号结构。进一步提出了电路实现方案（electrical-circuit implementation），并讨论了再入平庸-拓扑-平庸转变的可实验探测特征。

Abstract: We investigate reentrant topological transitions in a one-dimensional Su--Schrieffer--Heeger chain with power-law quasiperiodically modulated intracell hopping. The modulation is characterized by a positive integer exponent $n$ and a tunable parameter $β$, which continuously interpolates between the smooth power-law quasiperiodic limit and a sign-function limit that becomes square-wave-like for odd $n$ and uniform for even $n$. By combining analytical calculations of the zero-mode inverse localization length with numerical evaluations of a real-space topological indicator, we determine the topological phase diagrams in the $β\to 0$, $β\to\infty$, and finite-$β$ regimes. We show that deterministic quasiperiodic modulation can induce TAI-like reentrant topological phases within finite parameter windows. The formation of these phases depends crucially on the parity of $n$: for positive modulation strength, odd-power modulations can induce reentrant topology from the clean trivial regime $|t_1|>1$, whereas even-power modulations allow such reentrance only from the negative clean trivial regime $t_1<-1$. Exact analytical expressions for the zero-mode inverse localization length are obtained for $n=1,2,3,4$, yielding explicit or implicit transition conditions. The finite-$β$ results demonstrate that the parity-dependent structure remains robust throughout the interpolation between the two limiting cases. This parity effect originates from whether the modulation preserves or removes the sign structure of $\cos x$. We further propose an electrical-circuit implementation and discuss experimentally accessible signatures of the reentrant trivial--topological--trivial transition.

### [51] [Beyond Continuity: Simulation-free Reconstruction of Discrete Branching Dynamics from Single-cell Snapshots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00545)
*Junda Ying,Yuxuan Wang,Bowen Yang,Peijie Zhou,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出非平衡薛定谔桥（Unbalanced Schrödinger Bridge, USB），一种无需仿真的学习框架，用于从破坏性快照数据中推断单细胞分辨率下的随机、非保守（如增殖与凋亡）的细胞轨迹，通过为个体细胞同时建模布朗运动和离散生灭跳跃，解决了分支薛定谔桥问题，并在模拟与真实数据上优于或可比于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从破坏性快照数据中推断细胞轨迹面临着随机性（stochasticity）及细胞增殖与凋亡等非保守质量动态（non-conservative mass dynamics）的挑战。现有非平衡最优传输（Unbalanced Optimal Transport）方法将质量视为连续流体，在群体层面进行推断，无法捕捉单细胞分辨率下离散、跳跃式的生灭事件，而这对理解谱系分支与命运决定至关重要。

Method: USB方法通过引入无需仿真的训练目标，有效求解分支薛定谔桥（Branching Schrödinger Bridge, BSB）问题，为个体细胞同时建模布朗运动（Brownian motion）和离散生灭跳跃，提供严格的微观解释，并有效扩展至高维组学数据。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据集上，USB的轨迹重建性能达到或优于确定性基线方法，并能在单细胞分辨率下实现生灭动态的现实离散仿真。

Conclusion: USB为融合随机性与非平衡效应的细胞动态学习提供了一个仿真自由的框架，在单细胞分辨率下兼顾轨迹重建与离散生灭过程的建模，扩展了现有最优传输方法的能力边界。

Abstract: Inferring cellular trajectories from destructive snapshots is complicated by the challenges of stochasticity and non-conservative mass dynamics such as cell proliferation and apoptosis. Existing unbalanced Optimal Transport (OT) methods treat mass as a continuous fluid, performing inference at the population level. However, this macroscopic view often fails to capture the discrete, jump-like nature of birth-death events at single-cell resolution, which is essential for understanding lineage branching and fate decisions. We present Unbalanced Schrödinger Bridge (USB), a simulation-free framework for learning underlying dynamics that effectively integrates both stochastic and unbalanced effects which also models the discrete, jump-like birth-death dynamics at single-cell resolution. Theoretically, USB provides a tractable solution to the Branching Schrödinger Bridge (BSB) problem, offering a rigorous microscopic interpretation where individual cells undergo both Brownian motion and discrete birth-death jumps. Technically, the method implements an efficient solver by introducing a simulation-free training objective that effectively scales to high-dimensional omics data. Empirically, we demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that USB not only achieves trajectory reconstruction performance better than or comparable to deterministic baselines but also uniquely enables realistic discrete simulation of birth-death dynamics at single-cell resolution.

</details>


### [52] [Cross-fluctuation phase transitions reveal sampling dynamics in diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.00124)
*Sai Niranjan Ramachandran,Manish Krishan Lal,Suvrit Sra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文基于统计物理中的中心矩统计量——交叉涨落（cross-fluctuations），分析了基于分数的扩散模型（score-based diffusion models）中样本分布的采样动力学。研究发现样本演化过程中存在尖锐的离散跃迁（transitions），这些跃迁可被高阶交叉涨落检测到。利用这一发现可提升采样效率、加速条件生成和稀有类别生成，并改进零样本图像分类和风格迁移任务。该框架统一了离散马尔可夫链理论、相分析（phase analysis）与现代生成建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于分数的扩散模型在采样过程中缺乏对分布演化结构和跃迁行为的深入理解；传统的网格搜索或重训练方法效率低下。建立一种理论框架来刻画采样轨迹中的离散跃迁，并据此提升采样效率和下游任务性能，是本文的核心动机。

Method: 引入统计物理中的交叉涨落（cross-fluctuations）作为中心矩统计量，分析无偏各向同性正态分布（unbiased isotropic normal distribution）向目标分布演化过程中的跃迁行为。推导了方差保持型随机微分方程（variance-preserving SDEs）下交叉涨落的闭式解，该解对反向轨迹高效可计算。

Result: 发现样本演化呈尖锐的离散跃迁，并逐步揭示精细结构；该过程可逆。这些跃迁可通过 n 阶交叉涨落（$n^{\text{th}}$-order cross-fluctuations）的间断性检测到。利用跃迁检测直接提升了采样效率，加速了类别条件生成和稀有类别生成，并在无需昂贵网格搜索或重训练的条件下改进了图像分类和风格迁移两项零样本任务。

Conclusion: 该框架将有限马尔可夫链中经典的耦合（coupling）与混合（mixing）概念与连续动力学统一，并推广至随机 SDE 和非马尔可夫采样器。本文由此桥接了离散马尔可夫链理论、相分析与现代生成建模。

Abstract: We analyse how the sampling dynamics of distributions evolve in score-based diffusion models using cross-fluctuations, a centered-moment statistic from statistical physics. Specifically, we show that starting from an unbiased isotropic normal distribution, samples undergo sharp, discrete transitions, eventually forming distinct events of a desired distribution while progressively revealing finer structure. As this process is reversible, these transitions also occur in reverse, where intermediate states progressively merge, tracing a path back to the initial distribution. We demonstrate that these transitions can be detected as discontinuities in $n^{\text{th}}$-order cross-fluctuations. For variance-preserving SDEs, we derive a closed-form for these cross-fluctuations that is efficiently computable for the reverse trajectory. We find that detecting these transitions directly boosts sampling efficiency, accelerates class-conditional and rare-class generation, and improves two zero-shot tasks--image classification and style transfer--without expensive grid search or retraining. We also show that this viewpoint unifies classical coupling and mixing from finite Markov chains with continuous dynamics while extending to stochastic SDEs and non Markovian samplers. Our framework therefore bridges discrete Markov chain theory, phase analysis, and modern generative modeling.

</details>


### [53] [Trees to Flows and Back: Unifying Decision Trees and Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00414)
*Sai Niranjan Ramachandran,Suvrit Sra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文建立了层次化决策树（hierarchical decision trees）与扩散过程（diffusion processes）在极限条件下的数学对应关系，统一了两类模型，并揭示了共享的优化原则——全局轨迹分数匹配（GTSM，Global Trajectory Score Matching），梯度提升（gradient boosting）在该原则下渐进最优。通过TreeFlow和DSM-Tree两个实例验证了方法的概念价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 决策树与扩散模型分属离散层次化和连续动态两类看似不同的模型体系，缺乏统一的数学框架来理解其内在关联。

Method: 通过建立层次化决策树与扩散过程在适当极限条件下的精确数学对应关系，统一两类模型，并推导出共享的优化原则——全局轨迹分数匹配（GTSM）。

Result: 提出TreeFlow方法，在表格数据生成上达到更高保真度和2倍的计算加速；提出DSM-Tree蒸馏方法，将层次化决策逻辑迁移至神经网络，在多个基准上匹配教师模型性能，误差在2%以内。

Conclusion: 两类模型在数学上存在深层统一性，共享GTSM优化原则，梯度提升是该原则下的渐进最优策略。这一统一框架具有实际应用价值，可用于提升生成质量和计算效率，以及实现决策逻辑的神经网络蒸馏。

Abstract: Decision trees and diffusion models are ostensibly disparate model classes, one discrete and hierarchical, the other continuous and dynamic. This work unifies the two by establishing a crisp mathematical correspondence between hierarchical decision trees and diffusion processes in appropriate limiting regimes. Our unification reveals a shared optimization principle: \emph{Global Trajectory Score Matching (GTSM)}, for which gradient boosting (in an idealized version) is asymptotically optimal. We underscore the conceptual value of our work through two key practical instantiations: \treeflow, which achieves competitive generation quality on tabular data with higher fidelity and a 2\times computational speedup, and \dsmtree, a novel distillation method that transfers hierarchical decision logic into neural networks, matching teacher performance within 2\% on many benchmarks.

### [54] [Bilinear formalism for Schwarzian KP and Harry Dym hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00235)
*Vadim Prokofev,Anton Zabrodin*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文在双线性形式（bilinear formalism）框架下研究了Schwarzian KP（SchKP）和Harry Dym两大可积层次（integrable hierarchies），证明了SchKP可重构为一对KP tau函数（tau-functions）的积分双线性方程（integral bilinear equation），且它们的任意线性组合仍为KP tau函数；Harry Dym层次则作为SchKP的Lax-Sato表述导出。论文还讨论了与Bäcklund-Darboux变换的关系，并揭示了SchKP到多分量KP层次（multi-component KP hierarchy）的自然嵌入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将双线性形式这一在KP、modified KP、BKP、Toda格点等可积层次中行之有效的框架，推广到Schwarzian KP和Harry Dym层次，以统一其代数结构与变换理论。

Method: 借鉴modified KP层次的双线性表述，将Schwarzian KP重构为一对KP tau函数满足的积分双线性方程；在此基础上利用Lax-Sato表述导出Harry Dym层次；并通过分析多分量KP层次揭示了SchKP的自然嵌入结构。

Result: 建立了SchKP与KP tau函数之间的精确双线性对应关系，证明了任意线性组合的闭合性；将Harry Dym层次明确置于SchKP的Lax-Sato框架下；指出SchKP与Bäcklund-Darboux变换的密切联系；并给出了SchKP到多分量KP层次的自然嵌入。

Conclusion: 双线性形式为Schwarzian KP和Harry Dym层次提供了统一的数学描述，揭示了它们与KP家族及相关变换（Bäcklund-Darboux）的内在联系，拓展了可积层次的双线性理论应用范围。

Abstract: We consider the Schwarzian KP and Harry Dym hierarchies in the framework of the bilinear formalism which is well known for such integrable hierarchies as KP, modified KP, BKP, Toda lattice and other. We show that, similarly to the bilinear formulation of the modified KP hierarchy, the Schwarzian KP can be reformulated as an integral bilinear equation for a pair of KP tau-functions with the property that any linear combination of them is again a tau function of the KP hierarchy. The Harry Dym hierarchy is then obtained as the Lax-Sato formulation of the SchKP one. The close connection with Backlund-Darboux transformations for integrable hierarchies is also discussed. Besides, it is shown that the SchKP hierarchy has a natural embedding into the multi-component KP hierarchy.

</details>

### [55] [A new family of weighted double Hurwitz numbers and a new ELSV-type formula with $Ω$-classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00584)
*Alexander Alexandrov,Boris Bychkov,Petr Dunin-Barkowski,Maxim Kazarian,Sergey Shadrin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在系统展示和进一步发展超几何KP tau函数与曲线模空间相交理论之间相互作用的技术，并解决此类上下文中ELSV型公式推导的微妙问题。

Method: 以加权双Hurewitz数为具体载体，结合对数拓扑递归中的$x-y$对偶性框架，系统运用并精炼超几何KP tau函数与曲线模空间相交理论之间的技术手段，推导ELSV型公式。

Result: 推导出一个新的、以$Ω$-类显式表达的ELSV型公式，并澄清了该语境下ELSV型公式推导中的若干微妙之处。

Conclusion: 本文的工作深化了对超几何KP tau函数与曲线模空间相交理论之间联系的理解，并为对数拓扑递归与相交理论之间的相互作用提供了新的显式结果。

Abstract: We analyze a new family of weighted double Hurwitz numbers that was introduced as a notable example in the context of the $x-y$ duality for logarithmic topological recursion. We use this family to systematically demonstrate, refine and develop techniques that play a crucial role in the interaction of hypergeometric (Orlov--Scherbin) KP tau functions and intersection theory of moduli spaces of curves. In particular, we discuss the subtleties related to the derivation of the ELSV-type formulas in this context and derive a new, explicit ELSV-type formula in terms of the so-called $Ω$-classes.

### [56] [Essential Duality and Maximal Non-signalling Extensions in Algebraic Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00075)
*Hassan Nasreddine*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 在可加性条件下，算子代数 $\mathcal{A}(O)$ 在 $B(\mathcal{H})$ 内部的最大冯·诺伊曼代数扩张——其内自同构相对于所有类空间隔区域不传递信号——是 $\mathcal{A}(O')'$；该最大性等价于本质对偶性（essential duality）成立。若本质对偶性不成立，则存在真扩张且保持非信号性（non-signalling）特性；否则任何真扩张必然引入信号性操作。研究还给出了楔交恒等式与本质对偶性的等价刻画，将其识别为给定表示中的操作性最大性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在可加性假设下，量子场论（quantum field theory）中区域代数 $\mathcal{A}(O)$ 在何种条件下能实现“最大非信号性扩张”（maximal non-signalling extension），即其内自同构（inner automorphisms）不向类空间隔（spacelike-separated）区域传递信号；并厘清本质对偶性（essential duality）在该最大性中的角色。

Method: 采用纯代数（purely algebraic）证明，不依赖Araki相对熵（Araki relative entropy）在证明中的使用，尽管后者作为信号性的定量诊断工具被提及；利用算子代数理论、冯·诺伊曼代数（von Neumann algebra）的扩张构造以及Kraus算子（Kraus operators）框架处理完全正映射。

Result: (1) 在可加性下，最大冯·诺伊曼代数扩张为 $\mathcal{A}(O')'$；(2) $\mathcal{A}(O)$ 满足该最大性当且仅当本质对偶性成立；(3) 本质对偶性失败时，可构造真扩张，其所有内自同构及Kraus算子所在的正规完全正映射均非信号性；(4) 提供了楔交恒等式 $\mathcal{A}(O')' = \bigcap_{W \supset O}\mathcal{A}(W)$ 及本质对偶性的等价刻画。

Conclusion: 本质对偶性被识别为给定表示中的一个操作性最大性条件（operational maximality condition）；Araki相对熵可作为信号性的定量诊断工具；研究揭示了区域代数扩张与信号性之间的代数-几何对偶关系。

Abstract: We show that, under additivity, the maximal von Neumann algebra extension of $\mathcal{A}(O)$ inside $B(\mathcal{H})$ whose inner automorphisms are non-signalling with respect to all spacelike-separated regions is $\mathcal{A}(O')'$. Consequently, $\mathcal{A}(O)$ is maximal with respect to this property if and only if essential duality holds.
  The proof is purely algebraic. When essential duality fails, we construct a proper extension all of whose inner automorphisms, and more generally all normal completely positive maps admitting Kraus operators in the algebra, are non-signalling. Under essential duality, any proper extension necessarily admits a signalling operation. An entropic formulation using Araki relative entropy provides a quantitative diagnostic of signalling, though it is not used in the proof.
  Additional structural results include the wedge-intersection identity $\mathcal{A}(O')' = \bigcap_{W \supset O}\mathcal{A}(W)$ and equivalent characterisations of essential duality. These results identify essential duality as an operational maximality condition within the given representation.

</details>


### [57] [A Unified Framework for Locally Stable Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00088)
*Zhi Li,Raz Firanko,Timothy H. Hsieh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的理论框架，用于刻画平衡、非平衡及亚稳态区域中纯态与混合态的物质相。核心概念是“局域稳定态（locally stable states）”，并证明了局域稳定性等价于短程关联（short range correlation），且该性质在局域可逆通道下保持不变，从而定义了局域稳定相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的物质相分类方法多针对平衡态纯态或混合态分别展开，缺乏一个能够同时涵盖平衡、非平衡及亚稳态的统一框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，提出一个基于局域可操作性（local operational property）的普适性刻画方法。

Method: 引入“局域稳定态”概念，其定义为任何局域操作（包括后选择（post selection））均可通过一个局域通道（local channel）逆转。从该操作定义出发，通过数学证明建立局域稳定性与短程关联（关联函数与条件互信息（conditional mutual information）的衰减）之间的等价关系。进一步证明该性质在局域可逆通道下不变，从而定义局域稳定相。此外，利用局域稳定性推导非线性关联子（包括保真度关联子（fidelity correlator））的衰减以及规范纯化（canonical purification）中关联的衰减，连接纯态与混合态。

Result: 建立了局域稳定性与短程关联之间的等价性；证明了局域稳定性在局域可逆通道下的不变性；证明了局域稳定性蕴含一类非线性关联子的衰减以及规范纯化中关联的衰减；证明了局域稳定（短程关联）态上的后选择可通过局域通道实现；证明了量子马尔可夫链（quantum Markov chain）可通过非线性可观测量（nonlinear observable）的局域可计算性来刻画。

Conclusion: 本文提出的局域稳定相框架为统一分类平衡、非平衡及亚稳态物质相提供了基础。两个独立兴趣的辅助结果（后选择的局域可实现性与量子马尔可夫链的局域可计算性刻画）进一步支持了该框架的普适性和理论价值。

Abstract: We propose a unifying framework for characterizing pure and mixed state phases of matter across equilibrium, non equilibrium, and metastable regimes. We introduce the concept of locally stable states, defined by the operational property that any local operation (including post selection) can be reversed by a local channel. We prove that local stability is equivalent to a state being short range correlated, defined by the decay of both correlations and conditional mutual information. We demonstrate that these properties are invariant under locally reversible channels, thus defining locally stable phases. Furthermore, we prove that local stability implies both the decay of a family of nonlinear correlators, including the fidelity correlator, and the decay of correlations in the canonical purification, thus bridging the gap between mixed and pure states. Along the way, we establish two results which may be of independent interest: we show that post-selection on locally stable (short range correlated) states can be implemented via local channels and that quantum Markov chains can be characterized by the local computability of nonlinear observables.

</details>


### [58] [Topological Charge of Causality at a PT-Symmetric Exceptional Point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00117)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现PT对称开放二聚体（PT-symmetric open dimer）中的线性响应（linear response）因果性并非传统认为的二元属性，而是携带拓扑荷（topological charge）；在奇异点（exceptional point）处，反射系数的极点迁移使布拉斯克绕数（Blaschke winding number）从0跳变至1，导致标准Kramers-Kronig（KK）关系失效，其破坏标度律为幂律形式，并可通过太赫兹时域光谱（THz time-domain spectroscopy）实验直接测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将线性响应中的因果性视为二元属性——响应函数要么在上半平面解析，要么不解析。本文旨在揭示在PT对称开放二聚体中，因果性实际上携带拓扑荷，从而为因果性破坏提供一种新的、可连续变化的拓扑描述。

Method: 推导了PT对称开放二聚体的精确反射系数，分析了增益-损耗参数跨越奇异点时反射系数极点的迁移行为；通过计算布拉斯克绕数的变化，建立了因果性破坏的拓扑刻画；推导了残差修正的色散关系（dispersion relation），并提出了太赫兹时域光谱测量方案。

Result: 随着增益-损耗参数跨越奇异点，反射系数的一个极点迁移到上半平面，布拉斯克绕数从0跳变到1；标准KK重建产生一个由极点残差（pole residue）确定的洛伦兹残差（Lorentzian residual）。单端口几何中，KK破坏的标度律为Δ_KK ~ |γ - γ_c|^ν，其中ν ≈ -1.08，表明破坏在阈值处最强，在破缺相内部减弱。

Conclusion: 因果性在PT对称开放二聚体中以拓扑荷形式存在，其破坏具有连续可调的标度行为，而非简单的二元属性。推导的残差修正色散关系成立，且所提太赫兹时域光谱协议可通过测量残差本身直接探测拓扑荷，为实验验证提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Causality in linear response is conventionally treated as a binary property: a response function is either analytic in the upper half-plane or it is not. We show that in a PT-symmetric open dimer it instead carries a topological charge. As the gain-loss parameter crosses the exceptional point, a single pole of the reflection coefficient migrates into the upper half-plane, the Blaschke winding number jumps from 0 to 1, and standard Kramers-Kronig (KK) reconstruction acquires a Lorentzian residual fixed by the pole residue. The transition is sharp, protected by the codimension-one structure of the exceptional point, and directly measurable in a one-port reflection experiment. Most strikingly, the violation magnitude scales as Delta_KK ~ |gamma - gamma_c|^nu with nu ~ -1.08 in the single-port geometry: the breakdown of standard KK is strongest at threshold and weakens deeper in the broken phase. We derive the exact reflection coefficient, verify the residue-corrected dispersion relation, and propose a THz time-domain spectroscopy protocol that detects the topological charge through the residual itself.

</details>


### [59] [Asymptotic Replacement for Quantum Channel Products with Applications to Inhomogeneous Matrix Product States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00157)
*Lubashan Pathirana*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套面向有限维量子信道乘积的乘积级迹-Dobrushin 理论（product-level trace-Dobrushin theory），并将其应用于左规范 CPTP 规范下的确定性与平稳随机非齐次矩阵积态（matrix product states, MPS）。研究表明，迹-Dobrushin 系数的衰减等价于迹范数遗忘；在随机情形下，迹-Dobrushin 李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）的几乎必然负性保证了淬火迹范数记忆丧失以及指数收敛到唯一动态平稳的随机替换信道（random replacement channel）。这些信道估计可进一步迁移至非齐次 MPS，给出无限体积极限、边界稳定性及相关性界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信道乘积的遗忘性（trace-norm forgetting）是理解非平衡量子系统与张量网络态热力学极限的关键，但现有理论缺乏面向乘积级系统的系统化分析框架。

Method: 建立乘积级迹-Dobrushin 理论，定义中心化迹-Dobrushin 系数（centered trace-Dobrushin coefficient）以量化对输入态的残余依赖；在随机情形下通过次可乘性（submultiplicativity）引入迹-Dobrushin 李雅普诺夫指数；利用信道的 \(\varrho\)-混合剖面对退火估计进行分类分析。

Result: 确定情形下，系数衰减等价于渐近替换为移动替换信道（moving replacement channel）；随机情形下，指数几乎必然负性等价于淬火遗忘，并给出指数收敛；独立环境给出退火指数估计，混合环境给出超多项式估计；这些估计可转移至非齐次 MPS，得到迹闭有限体积态的无限体积极限及边界稳定性。

Conclusion: 所建立的乘积级迹-Dobrushin 理论统一了确定性和随机量子信道乘积的遗忘性分析，并为非齐次矩阵积态提供了系统性的无限体积极限与相关性控制工具。

Abstract: We develop a product-level trace-Dobrushin theory for finite-dimensional quantum channel products and apply it to deterministic and stationary random inhomogeneous matrix product states in left-canonical CPTP gauge. For a product of channels, the centered trace-Dobrushin coefficient quantifies the residual dependence on the input state, and its decay is the criterion for trace-norm forgetting. In the deterministic setting, this decay is equivalent to asymptotic replacement by a moving replacement channel. For two-sided products, pullback forgetting produces a unique boundary state, which determines the canonical replacement family. For stationary random CPTP cocycles, submultiplicativity of the product coefficient yields a trace-Dobrushin Lyapunov exponent. We prove that the almost sure negativity of this exponent is equivalent to quenched trace-norm memory loss and gives exponential forward and pullback convergence to a unique dynamically stationary random replacement channel. When the \(\varrho\)-mixing profile of the channel environment tends to zero, we obtain annealed super-polynomial estimates, while independence gives annealed exponential estimates. Finally, we transfer these estimates to inhomogeneous matrix product states whose auxiliary transfer maps are CPTP. These channel estimates transfer to deterministic and stationary random inhomogeneous MPS, giving infinite-volume limits of trace-closed finite-volume states, quantitative boundary stability, and correlation bounds governed by the same auxiliary product coefficients.

</details>


### [60] [Graph-theory measures capture weak ergodicity breaking on large quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00094)
*Heiko Georg Menzler,Rafał Świętek,Mari Carmen Bañuls,Fabian Heidrich-Meisner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过福克空间（Fock space）的图论表示，引入图能量中心性（graph-energy centrality）作为刻画封闭量子多体系统中弱遍历性破缺（weak ergodicity violation）相变的解析度量，可计算至热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究封闭量子多体系统中由模型参数控制的弱遍历性破缺相变，并寻找能够解析计算而非仅适用于小系统大小的诊断工具。

Method: 将量子系统在福克空间（Fock space）中表示，借助图论（graph theory）度量进行分析；引入图能量中心性（graph-energy centrality）并考察其分布的特征变化。

Result: 图能量中心性的分布能够捕捉已知的弱遍历性破缺相变特征；该度量可对数百格点的大系统进行解析计算，部分情形下甚至可延拓至热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）。

Conclusion: 基于福克空间的图能量中心性度量在运动学约束量子模型（kinetically constrained quantum model）中成功识别出弱遍历性破缺相变及伴随的玻璃态动力学（glassy dynamics）。

Abstract: We study the onset of weak ergodicity violations in closed quantum many-body systems and focus on cases in which they occur through a transition that is controlled by a model parameter. Our analysis is based on representing quantum systems in Fock space and utilizes graph-theoretical measures. As a main result, we show that the recently introduced graph-energy centrality captures known weak ergodicity-breaking transitions via characteristic changes in its distribution. While most numerical tools are limited to small system sizes, our measure can be calculated analytically for large systems of many hundreds of sites and in some cases, even in the thermodynamic limit. We conclude by demonstrating the applicability of our Fock-space based measure to a kinetically constrained quantum model, where we find evidence for a weak ergodicity-breaking transition accompanied by glassy dynamics.

</details>


### [61] [Scalable spin-nematic squeezing in multi-level dipole-interacting Rydberg atom arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00096)
*Sakshi Bahamnia,Thomas Bilitewski*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在偶极相互作用里德伯原子阵列中，三能级（自旋-1）系统产生计量学有用纠缠的机制，通过自旋向列压缩（spin-nematic squeezing）和单轴/双轴扭转动力学，实现了可扩展的纠缠生成，其量子 Fisher 信息（quantum Fisher information）可达 $F_Q \propto N^2$，为超出量子比特（qubit）框架的量子纠缠研究提供了理论第一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子计量与纠缠生成研究主要集中在两能级量子比特（qubit）系统，对更高维度的量子比特系统（qudit）中可扩展纠缠生成的机制尚缺乏系统理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究三能级（自旋-1）系统中偶极相互作用如何产生可扩展的计量学有用纠缠。

Method: 在自旋-四极矩算子（spin-quadrupolar operator）基下，将相互作用哈密顿量分解为有效的 SU(2) 子空间（effective SU(2) subspaces）。对于对称相互作用，建立了从初态乘积态（product initial states）到亮-暗流形（bright and dark manifolds）内有效单轴扭转（one-axis twisting）的映射；对于反对称相互作用，结合微波驱动实现了双轴反向扭转（two-axis countertwisting）机制。

Result: 对称相互作用下，压缩参数（squeezing parameter）标度行为为：全连接耦合时 $\xi^{2}\propto N^{-2/3}$，二维偶极耦合时 $\xi^{2}\propto N^{-0.5}$。反对称相互作用下，全连接耦合可实现 $\xi^{2}\propto N^{-0.7}$ 的压缩。两种情况下量子 Fisher 信息均达到 $F_Q \propto N^{2}$。

Conclusion: 本文为基于偶极相互作用的量子比特系统（qudit）中可扩展纠缠生成提供了首个理论分析，其结论直接适用于当前光镊里德伯原子实验，为超越量子比特框架的量子计量与纠缠研究开辟了新路径。

Abstract: We study the generation of metrologically useful entanglement in a three-level (spin-1) system naturally realized in arrays of dipole-interacting Rydberg atoms confined in optical tweezers. In the spin-quadrupolar operator basis, the interaction Hamiltonian decomposes into effective SU(2) subspaces, within which quench dynamics from product initial states generate scalable spin-nematic squeezing. For symmetric interactions, we identify a mapping to effective one-axis twisting within bright and dark manifolds and demonstrate that the squeezing parameter scales as $ξ^{2}\propto N^{-2/3}$ ($ξ^{2}\propto N^{-0.5}$) with system size for all-to-all (two-dimensional dipolar) couplings. In both cases the quantum Fisher information reaches $F_Q\propto N^{2}$. For antisymmetric interactions supplemented by a microwave drive we find a distinct two-axis countertwisting mechanism. This results in squeezing $ξ^{2}\propto N^{-0.7}$ for all-to-all interactions and moderate squeezing for dipolar interactions in 2D. Our results constitute a first theoretical step beyond the well-studied qubit setting toward scalable entanglement generation in qudit systems with dipolar interactions, directly relevant to current Rydberg tweezer experiments.

</details>


### [62] [Nonreciprocity-enriched steady phases in open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00101)
*Ding Gu,Zhanpeng Fu,Zhong Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了非互易性（nonreciprocity）与对称性缺陷（symmetry defects）及空间边界（spatial boundaries）的相互作用，可以产生超越传统自发对称性破缺（spontaneous-symmetry-breaking）范式的稳态相。具体表现为，强非互易性将边界转变为对称性缺陷的源与汇，同时在体区赋予这些缺陷手性动力学（chiral dynamics），从而形成畴壁行波相（domain-wall traveling-wave phase）。此外，即使在没有对称性破缺的情况下，稳态也会表现出反常手性弛豫（anomalous chiral relaxation），源于稳定性矩阵中的非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易性对开放量子系统（open quantum systems）的能谱和动力学有深远影响，但其对长时间稳态物质相（steady-state phases of matter）的作用此前尚未被充分探索。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用具有Z₂对称性的玻色模型（bosonic model），分别研究周期边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）和开放边界条件（open boundary conditions）下的稳态行为。结合平均场理论（mean-field theory）和截断维格纳模拟（truncated Wigner simulations）对相变、序参量（order parameter）和戈德斯通模式（Goldstone-mode）涨落进行表征。

Result: 周期边界条件下仅存在常规对称相和对称性破缺相；开放边界条件下，足够强的非互易性可诱导出畴壁行波相。此外，即使没有对称性破缺，稳态也会因非厄米趋肤效应而表现出反常手性弛豫：局域涨落在趋近边界时被手性放大，并最终衰减。

Conclusion: 非互易性、对称性缺陷与边界的协同效应可生成超越传统对称性破缺范式的稳态相，该结论在三维空间中得到验证。

Abstract: Nonreciprocity can profoundly alter the spectra and dynamics of open quantum systems, yet its impact on the long-time steady-state phases of matter has remained largely unexplored. Here we show that the interplay of nonreciprocity, symmetry defects, and spatial boundaries can generate phases beyond the standard spontaneous-symmetry-breaking paradigm. We demonstrate this mechanism by showing that sufficiently strong nonreciprocity turns boundaries into sources and drains of symmetry defects, while simultaneously endowing these defects with chiral dynamics in the bulk. As a result, the conventional uniform symmetry-broken state gives way to a domain-wall traveling-wave phase, in which symmetry defects form a persistent chiral wave. We showcase this mechanism in a bosonic model with \(Z_{2}\) symmetry, where periodic boundary conditions support only the conventional symmetric and symmetry-broken phases, whereas open boundary conditions allow the traveling-wave phase. We further show that even in the absence of symmetry breaking, the steady state can exhibit anomalous chiral relaxation: owing to the non-Hermitian skin effect in the stability matrix, local fluctuations are chirally amplified as they approach a boundary, where they eventually decay. Combining mean-field theory with truncated Wigner simulations, we characterize these phases, analyze the order parameter and Goldstone-mode fluctuations of the traveling-wave phase, and confirm its existence in three spatial dimensions.

</details>


### [63] [Optically detected nuclear magnetic resonance of carbon-13 in bulk diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00152)
*Maxwell D. Aiello,Janis Smits,Yaser Silani,Andris Berzins,David Lidsky,Bryan A. Richards,Amilcar Jeronimo Perez,Chandrasekhar Ramanathan,Sebastián C. Carrasco,Jabir Chathanathil,Michael Goerz,Vladimir Malinovsky,Dmitry Budker,Sean Lourette,Andrey Jarmola,Victor M. Acosta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种基于金刚石中13C核自旋的光学检测核磁共振技术，利用微波频率扫描下的Landau-Zener跃迁在氮-空位（NV）电子自旋与远程13C核自旋之间双向转移自旋极化，实现了约10^16个极化核自旋的光学极化和读出，在8-20 mT磁场下获得超过0.5%峰-峰值的核自旋依赖荧光对比度及约2 ms的核自旋退相位时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于光学检测核磁共振（optically detected nuclear magnetic resonance）的精密测量对自旋跃迁频率的绝对偏移具有极高的灵敏度，在基础物理实验和惯性传感中有重要应用。本文旨在探索金刚石中13C核自旋作为固态实现候选系统的可行性，以期在毫特斯拉或更低磁场下实现对大量相干核自旋的高保真读出。

Method: 该方法利用微波频率扫描下的态选择性Landau-Zener跃迁（state-selective Landau-Zener transitions），在氮-空位（Nitrogen-Vacancy, NV）电子自旋与远程13C核自旋之间实现自旋极化的双向转移。实验采用天然同位素丰度金刚石，氮密度约为0.5-10 ppm，通过光学手段检测13C Ramsey谱学。

Result: 实现了约10^16个极化核自旋的光学读出，核自旋依赖荧光对比度超过0.5%峰-峰值（peak-to-peak）。核自旋退相位时间T2*约为2 ms，同核偶极解耦（homonuclear dipolar decoupling）仅带来有限改善，表明其受限于附近NV电子自旋的纵向自旋弛豫。在8-20 mT磁场范围内，对比度和退相位时间相当。每个NV中心可在核自旋退极化前光学读出约100个核的自旋状态。

Conclusion: 本文演示的技术可解释为一种重复读出（repetitive readout）方法，为固态平台中大规模核自旋系综的高保真光学检测提供了可行路径，在基础物理精密测量和惯性传感领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Precision measurements based on optically detected nuclear magnetic resonance offer exquisite sensitivity to absolute shifts in spin transition frequencies, with potential applications in fundamental physics experiments and inertial sensing. We investigate 13C nuclear spins in diamond as a candidate system for solid-state implementations, which hold the promise for high-fidelity readout of large numbers of coherent nuclear spins in millitesla or lower magnetic fields. We demonstrate a technique that allows for both optical polarization and readout of large ensembles of ~10^{16} polarized nuclear spins. Our method takes advantage of state-selective Landau-Zener transitions under microwave frequency sweeping, which bidirectionally transfer spin polarization between Nitrogen-Vacancy (NV) electron spins and remote 13C nuclear spins. Using natural isotopic abundance diamonds with nitrogen densities of ~0.5-10 ppm, we perform optically-detected 13C Ramsey spectroscopy and realize a nuclear-spin-dependent fluorescence contrast exceeding 0.5% peak-to-peak. We observe nuclear spin dephasing times T2*~2 ms that only modestly improve with homonuclear dipolar decoupling, indicating that they are limited by the longitudinal spin relaxation of nearby NV electron spins. We study the magnetic field dependence of the optical readout and find comparable contrast and dephasing times for magnetic fields in the range 8-20 mT. Our method can be interpreted as a type of repetitive readout, where each NV center optically reads out the spin state of ~100 nuclei before nuclear spins depolarize.

### [64] [Topological protection of local quantum Fisher information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00770)
*Marcin Płodzień,Jan Chwedeńczuk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明，在多体量子系统中，拓扑相（topological phase）可以阻止局域编码信息的退局域化，以Kitaev链中的Majorana零模为例，通过边界量子Fisher信息（QFI）的非零平台维持指数级长时间的信息保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多体量子系统中，幺正动力学（unitary dynamics）通常会使局域编码的信息退局域化，导致单站点计量灵敏度（metrological sensitivity）丧失。研究旨在探索拓扑相能否阻止这种信息分散。

Method: 通过解析推导开放Kitaev链中局域量子Fisher信息（local QFI）的精确表达式，识别出机制为两个Majorana正交分量（Majorana quadratures）空间分离至链的两端，产生边界编码轴不对称性（encoding-axis asymmetry），并通过数值模拟验证对淬火无序和宇称保持相互作用的鲁棒性。

Result: Majorana零模使边界QFI维持非零平台，持续时间为系统尺寸的指数长。边界编码轴不对称性能够区分拓扑边界记忆与普通局域子隙信号（localized subgap signal）。该不对称性对中等淬火无序（quenched on-site disorder）具有鲁棒性，且在宇称保持相互作用（parity-preserving interactions）下边界平台仍保持可见。

Conclusion: 拓扑相可以提供一种防止多体量子系统中信息退局域化的机制。协议仅需乘积态初始化、哈密顿量演化和单站点读出，实验实现可行性较高。

Abstract: In many-body quantum systems, unitary dynamics generically delocalize locally encoded information, causing single-site metrological sensitivity to vanish. We analytically demonstrate that a topological phase can prevent this dispersal. In the open Kitaev chain, a Majorana zero mode fixes the boundary quantum Fisher information (QFI) at a nonzero plateau that persists for times exponentially long in system size. We derive exact analytical expressions for the local QFI and identify the mechanism as the spatial separation of the two Majorana quadratures to opposite ends of the chain. This separation produces a boundary encoding-axis asymmetry that distinguishes topological boundary memory from a generic localized subgap signal. We show numerically that the asymmetry is robust to moderate quenched on-site disorder, while the boundary plateau remains visible under parity-preserving interactions in finite-size real-time simulations. The protocol requires only product-state initialization, Hamiltonian evolution, and single-site readout.

</details>


### [65] [Entanglement capacity of complex networks from quantum walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00772)
*Pravy Prerana,Sascha Wald*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对离散时间量子行走（discrete-time quantum walks）在复杂网络中的量子传输问题，提出了一种基于源-目标二分（source-target bipartition）的通用纠缠度量（entanglement measure），该度量无需固定希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的因子分解，适用于不规则网络，并揭示了网络连通性（connectivity）与图匹配（graph matchings）对纠缠生成的约束机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在规则结构上，硬币-行走者纠缠（coin-walker entanglement）已被广泛用于刻画量子传输及支持量子算法协议，但该度量依赖于固定的希尔伯特空间因子分解，无法直接应用于更复杂的不规则网络。因此，亟需一种不依赖特定结构分解的通用纠缠度量。

Method: 引入一种基于二分（bipartition）的纠缠度量——源-目标纠缠（source-target entanglement），该二分将每个节点同时赋予源与目标两种角色，从而适用于一般网络结构。通过理论分析建立网络连通性与该纠缠上界之间的联系，并借助图匹配（graph matchings）揭示纠缠生成的底层结构。

Result: 网络连通性对源-目标纠缠施加了一个上界；图匹配被识别为控制纠缠生成的根本结构。在随机图（random graphs）中，提高图的连通性会降低可达到的纠缠量，从而建立了一个结构依赖的量子关联约束。

Conclusion: 该研究为一般网络中的量子纠缠提供了一种不依赖固定因子分解的度量方式，揭示了网络拓扑对量子关联的根本性约束，对复杂网络上的量子传输与量子信息处理具有潜在指导意义。

Abstract: Discrete-time quantum walks provide a natural framework for quantum transport on complex networks. On regular structures, coin-walker entanglement has been widely used to characterize quantum transport and to support quantum algorithmic protocols. However, this notion relies on a fixed Hilbert space factorization separating coin and position and is therefore not directly applicable to more complex, irregular structures. Here we introduce an entanglement measure for general networks based on a bipartition that assigns each node two roles, acting as both a source and a target. The resulting bipartition defines the source-target entanglement, a measure for general networks, motivated by coin-walker entanglement. We show that the connectivity of the network imposes an upper bound on this entanglement and identify graph matchings as the underlying structure governing entanglement generation. We further illustrate that in random graphs improving graph connectivity reduces the attainable entanglement, establishing a structure-dependent constraint on quantum correlations.

</details>

### [66] [Criticality on Rényi defects at (2+1)$d$ O(3) quantum critical points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00104)
*Yanzhang Zhu,Zhe Wang,Meng Cheng,Zheng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模量子蒙特卡洛模拟，系统研究了(2+1)维O(3) Wilson-Fisher量子临界点附近Rényi纠缠熵的普适标度行为，发现沿Rényi缺陷线存在多个缺陷普适类（ordinary、special、extraordinary），且对于extraordinary纠缠割，Rényi指数可诱导缺陷上的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子临界点处，Rényi纠缠熵的普适标度行为由红外理论中余二维Rényi（锥形）缺陷的普适类控制；本文旨在系统研究该缺陷线上的临界关联，并澄清先前观测到的Rényi熵标度对微观晶格细节的依赖之谜。

Method: 采用大规模量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，在实现O(3) Wilson-Fisher普适类量子相变的(2+1)维量子自旋模型中，沿Rényi缺陷线系统研究临界关联函数。

Result: 固定Rényi指数n时，存在多个Rényi缺陷普适类，其缺陷上的O(3)序参量具有不同的临界指数。按与表面临界性（surface criticality）的关系，将这些普适类归类为ordinary、special和extraordinary。对于extraordinary纠缠割，还发现了随Rényi指数变化的缺陷相变证据。

Conclusion: 缺陷普适类在决定Rényi熵普适标度中起关键作用，为理解Rényi熵标度对微观晶格细节的依赖提供了理论框架。

Abstract: At a quantum critical point, the universal scaling behavior of Rényi entanglement entropy is controlled by the universality class of the codimension-two Rényi (or conical) defects in the infrared theory. In this work we perform a systematic study of critical correlations along Rényi defect lines in (2+1)d quantum spin models realizing quantum phase transitions described by the O(3) Wilson-Fisher universality class, using large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations. We present numerical evidence that, for a fixed Rényi index $n$, there exist multiple Rényi defect universality classes, with distinct critical exponents for the O(3) order parameter on the defect. These universality classes are realized by choosing microscopically different entanglement cuts in lattice models, which we classify as ordinary, special and extraordinary according to their relation to surface criticality. For the extraordinary entanglement cut, we further find evidence for a phase transition on the defect as a function of the Rényi index. Our results highlight the key role of defect universality classes in determining the universal scaling of Rényi entropy, and provide a framework for understanding the previously observed dependence of Rényi entropy scaling on microscopic lattice details.

### [67] [Quantized Collective Fluctuations in Correlated Fermion Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00211)
*S. S. Onuchin,Ya. S. Lyakhova,L. D. Silakov,A. N. Rubtsov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在涨落局域场（FLF）方法框架下，提出了其量子扩展版本Q-FLF，通过纳入选定的玻色子松原频率（Matsubara modes）来描述关联费米子系统中的量子集体涨落。以半满一维Hubbard链为测试系统，计算了格林函数、总能量和反铁磁磁化率，结果表明该方法能够高效且选择性地表征单个玻色子模的贡献：低频玻色子模对总能量和反铁磁磁化率等积分可观测量有定量影响，而精确描述单粒子性质则需包含高频玻色子模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米子系统中的集体激发对其物理性质至关重要，发展描述这些激发及其与费米子自由度耦合的高效理论方法是一项重要挑战。本文旨在解决量化集体涨落中单个玻色子模（bosonic modes）对关联费米子体系可观测量贡献的问题。

Method: 在FLF方法基础上，将其辅助场从经典处理扩展为包含选定的玻色子松原频率（Matsubara modes）的量子化描述，提出Q-FLF（Quantum Fluctuating Local Field）方法。以半满一维Hubbard链作为测试系统，计算格林函数（Green's function）、总能量和反铁磁磁化率（antiferromagnetic susceptibility）。

Result: Q-FLF方法能够高效且选择性地表征单个玻色子模的贡献。低频松原频率对总能量和反铁磁磁化率等积分可观测量具有定量影响；精确描述单粒子性质则需要包含高频玻色子模。

Conclusion: 所提出的Q-FLF方案为关联费米子体系中量子集体涨落的选择性描述提供了一种高效的理论工具，明确了不同频率玻色子模对不同类型可观测量的差异化贡献。

Abstract: Collective excitations in fermionic systems play a crucial role in determining their physical properties. An important challenge is to develop efficient theoretical approaches for describing these excitations and their coupling to fermionic degrees of freedom. In this work, we revisit the problem of quantifying the contributions of individual bosonic modes of collective fluctuations to observable properties of correlated fermion systems within the framework of the Fluctuating Local Field (FLF) method. Whereas the auxiliary field in this method was previously considered only classically, we formulate its systematic extension termed Quantum FLF (Q-FLF) that incorporates selected bosonic Matsubara modes, thus tailoring it to description of quantum collective fluctuations. As a testbed, we apply the approach to a half-filled one-dimensional Hubbard chain and compute the Green's function, the total energy, and the antiferromagnetic susceptibility. Our results demonstrate that the proposed scheme enables an efficient and selective characterization of the contributions of individual bosonic modes. In particular, low Matsubara frequencies are found to have a quantitative impact on integrated observables such as total energy and antiferromagnetic susceptibility. At the same time, an accurate description of single-particle properties requires inclusion of higher-frequency bosonic modes.

### [68] [Electrical detection of spin-flip transition in metal/Na5Co15.5Te6O36 heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00491)
*Hirotsugu Tagami,Takuya Kawada,Yuki Shiomi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: MR异常主要源于NCTO中Co网磁结构变化引起的磁致伸缩应变效应。Pt/NCTO与Cu/NCTO的高场MR斜率反号表明，在诱导铁磁态中，界面自旋积累与磁化强度的相互作用是影响MR效应的重要因素。

Abstract: We report on the longitudinal magnetoresistance (MR) in thin metal films on an Ising-type antiferromagnetic insulator, Na5Co15.5Te6O36 (NCTO). Steep changes in the MR spectra with hysteresis were observed at spin-flip transitions driven by magnetic fields applied along the easy axis of the NCTO crystal. The MR jumps almost follow step-like changes in magnetization at the spin-flip transition. At very low temperatures where Co moments are partially frozen, the MR anomalies exhibit a tunnel-magnetoresistance-like shape. The observed MR anomalies at the spin-flip transition are attributed to strain effects via magnetostriction upon the magnetic-structure change of the Co nets in NCTO, because similar MR jumps are observed in both Pt/NCTO and Cu/NCTO. Interestingly, we found that the high-field slopes of the MR spectra show opposite signs between Pt/NCTO and Cu/NCTO at low temperatures. Because the opposite signs of the high-field MR are prominent below the antiferromagnetic transition temperature of NCTO, the interaction between the interface spin accumulation and magnetization is likely to contribute to the MR effect in the induced ferromagnetic state.

### [69] [Induced discommensurations in the lock-in transition of charge-density waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00521)
*Katsuhiko Inagaki,Satoshi Tanda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过数值退火方法研究了McMillan自由能框架下电荷密度波（charge-density wave）的锁定相变，发现公度态（commensurate state）中可激发失配结构（discommensurations），从而驱动系统转向非公度态（incommensurate state）。这一过程由拓扑不变量（topological invariants）主导，且与o-TaS₃中电流诱导的非公度结构的衍射实验结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解电荷密度波（charge-density wave）中锁定相变（lock-in transition）的波函数轮廓（wave profiles）及其临界行为，特别是失配结构（discommensurations）在公度态（commensurate state）中的激发机制和拓扑起源。

Method: 采用数值退火（numerical annealing）方法求解McMillan自由能（McMillan's free energy），获取临界值附近的波函数轮廓，并与先前研究进行对比验证。

Result: 数值退火方法复现了先前研究结果。临界值附近的波函数轮廓包含失配结构。在公度态中可激发失配结构，使系统转向非公度态。这些波函数轮廓来源于拓扑不变量（topological invariants）。失配结构的激发方向有利于恢复非公度态的原始波长。该结果与o-TaS₃中电流诱导非公度结构的衍射实验一致。

Conclusion: 提出了公度态中失配结构的激发机制及其拓扑起源，阐明了McMillan自由能对此过程的决定性作用，并通过实验观测验证了理论预测的一致性。

Abstract: We studied McMillan's free energy of the lock-in transition in charge-density waves. The wave profiles near the critical value were obtained by numerical annealing. First, we demonstrated that our method reproduces the previous studies. The obtained wave profiles include discommensurations near the critical value. Then, we calculated possible wave profiles in the commensurate state. We found that discommensurations are able to be excited in the commensurate state, leading the system to turn out to an incommensurate state. We proposed that these wave profiles result from topological invariants. Moreover, excitation of the discommensurations is favorable for the direction to the original wavelength of the incommensurate state. This is attributed to the nature of McMillan's free energy. The current-induced incommensurations, which we discovered with the diffraction study of $o$-TaS$_3$ [Inagaki \textit{et al.}, J. Phys. Soc. Jpn. 77, 093708 (2008)], is consistent with this study.

</details>


### [70] [Incommensurate Magnetic Ordered Phase with Enhanced Low-Temperature Magnetic Specific Heat in SmAu$_3$Al$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00540)
*Ryuji Higashinaka,Takuma Iwami,Kohsuke Saitou,Takashi U. Ito,Chihiro Tabata,Koji Kaneko,Takashi Ohhara,Ryoji Kiyanagi,Akiko Nakao,Jumpei G. Nakamura,Wataru Higemoto,Akihiro Koda,Shinsaku Kambe,Yuji Aoki,Tatsuma D. Matsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过中子散射与μ子自旋旋转实验，发现SmAu₃Al₇单晶中存在两个连续的磁有序相变（T_N=2.8 K, T^*=0.9 K），确认了非公度（incommensurate）长程磁有序，并排除了先前提出的部分无序态假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究SmAu₃Al₇单晶中低温磁有序态的本质，澄清先前研究中关于部分无序态（partially disordered state）的争议，并为非公度磁有序（incommensurate magnetic ordering）与低温磁比热增强之间的关联提供实验依据。

Method: 对SmAu₃Al₇单晶分别进行中子散射（neutron scattering）与μ子自旋旋转（muon spin rotation, μSR）测量，结合磁布拉格峰（magnetic Bragg peaks）分析与自发内场（spontaneous internal field）谱形判断磁有序结构。

Result: 在T_N=2.8 K以下观察到非公度传播矢量q=(0.30, 0, 1.33)的磁布拉格峰；μSR在T_N以下探测到自发内场，且谱形与非公度磁有序一致；在T^*=0.9 K处未发现磁结构异常，表明上下两个转变温度区间的磁结构本质不变；确认磁有序为空间均匀的长程有序态（long-range ordered state），而非部分无序态。

Conclusion: SmAu₃Al₇的磁基态是非公度长程磁有序态，排除了部分无序态的可能性；该非公度磁有序可能与低温磁比热（magnetic specific heat）增强存在关联。

Abstract: Neutron scattering and muon spin rotation ($μ$SR) measurements on single-crystal SmAu$_3$Al$_7$ reveal magnetically ordered states associated with successive transitions at $T_{\rm N}$ = 2.8 K and $T^*$ = 0.9 K. Magnetic Bragg peaks appear below $T_{\rm N}$ with an incommensurate (IC) propagation vector ${\bf q}$ = (0.30, 0, 1.33). $μ$SR detects spontaneous internal fields below $T_{\rm N}$, and the spectral shape is consistent with the IC magnetic ordering. No anomalies are observed at $T^*$, indicating that the magnetic structure remains essentially unchanged below and above $T^*$. The magnetic order is revealed to be a spatially homogeneous long-range ordered state, rather than a partially disordered state proposed in earlier studies. The possible connection between the IC magnetic order and the enhanced low-temperature magnetic specific heat is discussed.

</details>


### [71] [Dynamical magnetotropic susceptibility as a new probe of Kitaev materials and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00568)
*João C. Inácio,J. Schwab,G. Rakhmanova,S. Safari,V. Zambra,H. Nasir,S. Paschen,K. A. Modic,Fakher F. Assaad,Toshihiro Sato*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了磁致旋磁化率（magnetotropic susceptibility）$k(ω)$，定义为悬臂振荡晶体在磁场中的扭矩与角位移振幅之比。通过线性响应理论（linear response theory）在通用关联电子模型中对$k(ω)$进行推导，并重点以Kitaev材料$α$-RuCl$_3$为例进行数值计算，发现低能标度行为来源于主导Kitaev耦合，且这种标度行为不受光学声子（optical phonons）影响。该探针可用于研究均匀电荷涨落（uniform charge fluctuations），尤其适用于Kondo破坏量子临界性（Kondo destruction quantum criticality）等体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁致旋磁化率$k(ω)$是一种探测超低频（ultra-low-frequency）均匀涨落的新探针，但目前对其普适理论推导及其在不同体系（如金属、绝缘磁体、量子临界点等）中的物理含义尚缺乏系统性理解。本文旨在从线性响应理论出发，建立$k(ω)$与自旋、电荷自由度的关联，并探索其在Kitaev材料及其他新奇量子体系中的应用。

Method: 首先，在线性响应理论（linear response theory）框架下，针对包含电荷和自旋自由度的通用关联电子哈密顿量（correlated-electron Hamiltonian），推导出$k(ω)$的表达式。数值部分采用辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo）结合基于机器学习的符号问题优化（machine-learning-based sign-problem optimization）方法，对$α$-RuCl$_3$的多个模型进行计算。

Result: 对于绝缘自旋系统，静态磁致旋磁化率$k(0)$对磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）敏感，有限频率的虚部$k''(ω)$可探测均匀动力学自旋磁化率（uniform dynamical spin susceptibility）。对于金属体系，识别出涡电流（eddy currents）会导致低频阻尼。针对$α$-RuCl$_3$的计算表明，观测到低温下$k(0)/T$随$B/T$的标度行为源于主导Kitaev耦合，非主导Kitaev耦合的参数集不呈现此标度。该标度在包含光学声子后仍然稳健。通过复现实验$k(0)$数据的参数集计算$k''(ω)$，显示局域磁矩特征，并在Larmor频率处出现单峰。

Conclusion: 磁致旋磁化率$k(ω)$是一种有效的低能探针，可用于研究均匀自旋和电荷自由度。其在Kitaev材料$α$-RuCl$_3$中呈现的标度行为证实了主导Kitaev耦合的关键作用。该探针的广泛应用前景尤其体现在Kondo破坏量子临界性（Kondo destruction quantum criticality）相关的均匀电荷涨落探测，对奇异金属性（strange metallicity）和非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: The magnetotropic susceptibility $k(ω)$ probes ultra-low-frequency uniform fluctuations. For a crystal mounted on an oscillating cantilever in a magnetic field, it is defined as the ratio of torque to angular-displacement amplitude. Its real and imaginary parts determine the oscillation-frequency shift and crystal-induced damping. It is a low-energy probe of uniform $q=0$ spin and charge degrees of freedom. We demonstrate this by deriving $k(ω)$ within linear response theory for a generic correlated-electron Hamiltonian with charge and spin degrees of freedom. Although it covers metallic and insulating magnets, correlated paramagnets, and exotic quantum critical points, we focus on limiting cases. For insulating spin systems $k(0)$ is sensitive to magnetic anisotropy whereas its finite-frequency imaginary part probes uniform dynamical spin susceptibility even in spin-symmetric models. For metallic systems we identify when eddy currents cause low-frequency damping. Our numerical results focus on Kitaev-material magnetotropic response. Using auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo with machine-learning-based sign-problem optimization we compute $k(ω)$ for several models proposed for $α$-RuCl$_3$. The observed low-temperature scaling of $k(0)/T$ with $B/T$ results from dominant Kitaev couplings: parameter sets without dominant Kitaev coupling do not exhibit this scaling. It remains robust upon inclusion of optical phonons. Beyond the static response, $k''(ω)$ for the $α$-RuCl$_3$ parameter set reproducing the experimental $k(0)$ data shows local-moment features at high and low $T$, with a single peak at the Larmor frequency. Beyond Kitaev systems we highlight broader applications. Probing ultra-low-energy uniform charge fluctuations is pertinent to Kondo destruction quantum criticality, of broad interest in strange metallicity and unconventional superconductivity.

</details>

### [72] [Low-temperature Depletion of Superfluid Density in the Absence of Galilean Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00274)
*Viktor Berger,Nikolay Prokof'ev,Boris Svistunov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 基于Popov流体动力学作用量（hydrodynamic action）的泛函形式，本文发展了一种普适理论，描述了在伽利略不变性（Galilean invariance）被破坏的超流体中超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）随低温的变化规律，并发现了热力学量的普适标度（$T^{d+1}$ 和 $1/L^{d+1}$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Landau超流理论中，正常组分的低温流动由声子风（phonon wind）主导；但当超流体由于无序、多孔介质或晶格势而破坏伽利略不变性时，该图像不再适用，声子风不再是超流组分耗散的唯一来源。因此，需要建立更一般的理论框架来描述这类系统中的超流行为。

Method: 基于含有非简谐项（anharmonic terms）的Popov流体动力学作用量，建立超流刚度的低温依赖性的普适理论；通过固定流体动力学作用量中由伽利略不变性决定的若干参数，该理论可退化为Landau结果作为特例，并利用相互作用晶格玻色子的数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 该理论揭示了超流体低温热力学的普适标度行为：对于一大类热力学量，有限温度（finite-$T$）效应与有限尺寸（finite-size, $L$）效应分别服从 $T^{d+1}$ 和 $1/L^{d+1}$ 的标度律，两者之间存在内在联系。论文还讨论了该定律的实验探测方案，并与现有文献进行了比较。

Conclusion: 本文所发展的普适理论成功将Landau超流理论推广到伽利略不变性被破坏的情形，并揭示了有限温度与有限尺寸效应之间的内在标度关系，为更广泛的超流体系统提供了统一的热力学描述。

Abstract: Landau theory of superfluidity associates low-temperature flow of the normal component with the phonon wind. This picture does not apply to superfluids in which Galilean invariance is broken either by disorder, porous media, or lattice potential, and the phonon wind is no longer solely responsible for depletion of the superfluid component. Based on Popov's hydrodynamic action with anharmonic terms, we present a general theory for low-temperature ($T$) dependence of the superfluid stiffness, which reproduces Landau result as a special case when several parameters of the hydrodynamic action are fixed by Galilean invariance, and validate it with numerical simulations of interacting lattice bosons. In a broader context, our approach reveals universal low-temperature thermodynamics of superfluids with an intrinsic connection between finite-$T$ and finite-size ($L$) effects implying universal scaling, $T^{d+1}$ and $1/L^{d+1}$, respectively, for a large class of thermodynamic quantities. We discuss the experimental detection of this law, and compare our prediction to the existing literature.

</details>

### [74] [Quantum corrections to the Josephson dynamics: a population-imbalance approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00571)
*Oliver Hideg,Sofia Salvatore,Luca Salasnich*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文利用布居数不平衡作为唯一动力学变量，研究两个弱耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）中约瑟夫森动力学（Josephson dynamics）的量子修正，通过单圈量子有效作用量（one-loop quantum effective action）计算有效势（effective potential）和有效质量（effective mass）的解析表达式，并导出量子修正后的约瑟夫森频率（Josephson frequency）。数值对比表明，在强相互作用区域，布居数不平衡描述优于互补的纯相位描述（phase-only approach）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对两个弱耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中约瑟夫森动力学的描述通常使用相位和布居数不平衡两个变量，但仅保留布居数不平衡作为单一动力学变量时，量子修正效应尚未得到充分研究，尤其是在质量依赖于坐标（position-dependent mass）的情形下。

Method: 从双变量作用量（two-variable action）出发，推导出包含位置依赖质量的布居数不平衡拉格朗日量（imbalance-only Lagrangian），并通过对称排序（symmetric operator ordering）进行量子化。采用协变背景场方法（covariant background-field method），完全考虑质量的坐标依赖性，计算单圈量子有效作用量，从而得到经典势（classical potential）和质量的前沿量子修正。

Result: 得到了有效势和有效质量的显式表达式，并导出了量子修正后的约瑟夫森频率。通过与双位点玻色-哈伯德模型（two-site Bose-Hubbard model）的严格对角化（exact diagonalization）数值比较，发现布居数不平衡描述在强相互作用区域优于纯相位描述。

Conclusion: 布居数不平衡方法在强相互作用区域自然有效，且比相位方法更准确，为研究此类系统中的量子修正提供了一种更优的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate quantum corrections to the Josephson dynamics of two weakly coupled Bose-Einstein condensates using the population imbalance as the sole dynamical variable. Starting from the two-variable action, we derive the imbalance-only Lagrangian with a position-dependent mass and quantize it via symmetric operator ordering. The leading quantum corrections to the classical potential and mass are computed via the one-loop quantum effective action, using a covariant background-field method that fully accounts for the coordinate dependence of the mass. This yields explicit expressions for the effective potential and the effective mass, from which we derive the quantum-corrected Josephson frequency. Numerical comparison with exact diagonalization of the two-site Bose-Hubbard model shows that the imbalance-only formulation outperforms the complementary phase-only approach in the regime of strong interactions, which is the natural domain of validity of the population-imbalance description.

</details>


### [75] [Atomic Interferometry with Spin-Orbit-Coupled Spin-1 Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00596)
*Renfei Zheng,Junying Wu,Josep Cabedo,Alessio Celi,Zhihao Lan,Weiping Zhang,Lu Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种基于拉曼缀饰玻色气体（Raman-dressed Bose gas）与自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的量子干涉仪方案，利用可调的自旋混合相互作用实现超越标准量子极限的干涉灵敏度，并通过自旋-动量锁定引致的密度条纹提供空间分辨的相位读出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在传统量子干涉仪中，态制备与相位印记难以独立控制，且可调纠缠生成手段有限，限制了干涉灵敏度的进一步提升。

Method: 利用拉曼缀饰与自旋-轨道耦合，使原子-光耦合混合自旋与动量自由度，在低能区域形成有效旋量凝聚体（effective spinor condensate），其自旋混合相互作用可独立于原子密度进行调节。该可控性支持基于有效时间反演的类回波（echo-type）协议，并利用有效旋量哈密顿量中的临界区域生成纠缠。

Result: 该方案能在超越标准量子极限（standard quantum limit）的条件下增强干涉灵敏度。同时，缀饰模式的自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）产生空间密度调制，可作为干涉相位的替代读出手段；即使在有效旋量描述中常规自旋可观测量不敏感的情况下，仍能从自旋-轨道诱导的密度条纹位移中提取相位信息。

Conclusion: 拉曼缀饰旋量气体可作为非线性原子干涉术（nonlinear atomic interferometry）的灵活平台，兼具可控的自旋混合动力学与空间分辨的相位读出能力。

Abstract: We propose and analyze a quantum interferometry scheme based on a Raman-dressed Bose gas with spin-orbit coupling. In this system, the atom-light coupling mixes spin and momentum degrees of freedom, giving rise, in the low-energy regime, to an effective spinor condensate whose spin-mixing interaction can be tuned independently of the atomic density. This controllability enables a separation between state preparation and phase imprinting, and provides a natural route to echo-type protocols based on effective time reversal. Within this framework, critical regimes of the effective spinor Hamiltonian can be used to generate entanglement and enhance interferometric sensitivity beyond the standard quantum limit. In addition, the spin-momentum locking of the dressed modes gives access to spatial density modulations that provide an alternative readout of the interferometric phase. In particular, phase information can be extracted from the displacement of spin-orbit-induced density stripes even when conventional spin observables are insensitive within the effective spinor description. Our results identify Raman-dressed spinor gases as a flexible platform for nonlinear atomic interferometry, combining controllable spin-mixing dynamics with spatially resolved phase readout.

</details>


### [76] [Entropy transport through a superfluid quantum point contact: A Keldysh field-theory approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00679)
*Davide Bertolusso,C. J. Bolech,Thierry Giamarchi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 利用Keldysh形式主义（Keldysh formalism）和BCS平均场模型，研究了化学势梯度下由量子点接触（quantum point contact）连接的两个超冷中性费米气体储库中的物质和熵输运，发现了熵电流在弹道结极限下的低电压振荡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展超冷费米气体中粒子输运研究至熵输运（entropy transport）领域，特别是在BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer）超流态下的非平衡稳态特性。

Method: 采用BCS平均场模型描述两端的引线（leads），并利用Keldysh形式主义推导非平衡稳态下的粒子流和熵流，分析不同结透明度（junction's transparency）参数下的电流-偏压特性。

Result: 证实了粒子流已知的典型行为，并首次将计算推广至BCS区域的熵流；熵流在弹道结极限（ballistic junction limit）下的低电压区域表现出振荡行为。

Conclusion: 熵流在低电压下的振荡行为揭示了超冷费米气体在BCS超流态下熵输运的新特征，为理解量子点接触中的热力学输运提供了理论依据，并与幺正区域（unitary regime）的冷原子实验观测具有可比性。

Abstract: We study the matter and entropy transport between two ultra-cold neutral Fermi-gas reservoirs linked by a quantum point contact under a chemical-potential gradient. We describe the two leads with a BCS mean-field model and derive the current-bias characteristics for both particle and entropy transport. We compute the out of equilibrium steady-state currents by using the Keldysh formalism. In accordance with previous works in the literature, we confirm the well-known behavior for the particle current and extend the computation to the entropy current in the BCS regime. The entropy current shows an oscillatory behavior at low voltage in the ballistic junction limit. We analyze the results for a wide range of values of the junction's transparency. We also compare our findings with experimental results in cold atomic gases in the unitary regime.

### [77] [Sizes of witnesses in Covtree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00622)
*Jette Gutzeit,Kimia Shaban,Karen Yeats,Stav Zalel*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究未标记偏序集（unlabelled posets）集合的最小见证（minimal witness）的大小上界问题，受到量子引力中因果集（causal set）方法的启发。结果表明，不存在形如 n+k+c 的线性上界；通过引入下集交换图（exchange graph of downsets）这一新工具，证明了所有最小见证 Q 满足 |Q| ≤ nk - n，并在 k=3 时给出了更紧的上界 |Q| ≤ (3/2)(n+1)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机源自量子引力中的因果集方法（causal set approach），该方法试图将时空结构建模为偏序集。在此框架下，理解偏序集集合与其最小见证之间的结构关系，对于刻画因果集的基本性质具有重要意义。

Method: 论文引入了一种新的组合工具——下集交换图（exchange graph of downsets），用以研究未标记偏序集集合的见证结构。通过该工具，作者对最小见证的大小进行了上界推导，并分别针对一般情形和 k=3 的特例进行了分析。

Result: 证明了对于任意常数 c，不存在形如 n+k+c 的线性上界。利用下集交换图，得到了所有最小见证 Q 满足 |Q| ≤ nk - n 的通用上界；当 k=3 时，存在一个最小见证 Q 满足 |Q| ≤ (3/2)(n+1) 的更优上界。

Conclusion: 论文明确指出，最小见证的大小无法由简单的线性函数 n+k+c 所界定，但可以通过新引入的下集交换图工具获得多项式级别的上界。这为因果集方法中偏序集的结构分析提供了新的理论工具和定量结果。

Abstract: Given a set $Γ$ of $k$ unlabelled posets, each of size $n$, we say that a poset $Q$ is a \emph{witness} to $Γ$ if $Γ$ is the set of downsets of size $n$ of $Q$. We say that $Q$ is a \emph{minimal witness} if it does not contain a proper downset that is itself a witness to $Γ$. Motivated by the causal set approach to quantum gravity, we study the upper bound on the size of minimal witnesses as a function of $n$ and $k$. We show that there is no linear upper bound of the form $n+k+c$ for any constant $c$. We introduce the \emph{exchange graph of downsets} as a new tool to study this scenario, and use it to show that all minimal witnesses $Q$ satisfy the bound $|Q|\leq nk-n$, and that when $k=3$ there is at least one minimal witness $Q$ that satisfies the bound $|Q|\leq \frac{3}{2}(n+1)$.

</details>

### [78] [$ρ$ mesons in finite magnetic field and finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00561)
*Zhiyang Liu,Min Zhou,Yvming Tian,Rui Zhou,Guoyun Shao,Shijun Mao*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文利用双味Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型，在Ritus方案和Schwinger方案下推导了有限磁场和温度下ρ介子（ρ meson）传播子的解析形式，求解极点方程发现多重质量解，并分析了质量随磁场和温度的变化行为，结果与格点QCD（LQCD）模拟一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限磁场和温度下研究强子性质对理解量子色动力学（QCD）相结构和强子谱至关重要，而ρ介子质量谱在强磁场下的行为尚需系统研究。

Method: 采用双味Nambu-Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型，充分考虑外磁场导致的平移不变性破缺，分别在Ritus方案和Schwinger方案下推导ρ介子传播子的解析形式，并通过求解极点方程（pole equation）获得介子质量。

Result: 零温下，M_{ρ^{-}_{+}}、M_{ρ^{0}_{+}}和M_{ρ^{±}_{0}}随磁场增大而增加；M_{ρ^{+}_{+}}先减小后饱和；M_{ρ^{0}_{0}}对磁场不敏感。有限温度下，固定磁场时，四个/五个最低质量解均随温度升高而下降，高温下趋近于组分夸克质量之和；不同ρ介子（ρ_+^{0,±}与ρ_0^{0,±}）的质量解在有限磁场和温度下可能发生简并（degenerate）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了ρ介子质量谱在磁场和温度作用下的多重解结构及其演化规律，结果与现有LQCD模拟一致，为理解强磁场下强子物理提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: The mass spectra of $ρ$ mesons ($ρ_{Q=\pm 1}^{s_z=0,\pm 1}$ and $ρ_{Q=0}^{s_z=0,\pm 1}$) at finite magnetic field and temperature are studied in frame of the two-flavor Nambu-Jona-Lasinio model. Fully considering the breaking of translational invariance induced by external magnetic field, the analytical form of $ρ$ meson propagators have been derived in the Ritus scheme and Schwinger scheme, which gives the same algebraic formula. When solving the pole equation of $ρ$ meson propagators, multiple solutions of the meson mass appear due to the dimension reduction of their constituent quarks in magnetic fields. At vanishing temperature, we focus on the $ρ$ meson masses $M_ρ$ corresponding to the lowest value solution of the pole equation. $M_{ρ^{-}_+}$, $M_{ρ^{0}_+}$ and $M_{ρ^{\pm}_0}$ increase with magnetic field. $M_{ρ^{+}_+}$ firstly decreases and then becomes saturated with increasing magnetic field. $M_{ρ^0_0}$ is not sensitive to magnetic field. These results are consistent with the available LQCD simulations. At finite temperature, we discuss the lowest four/five solutions of $ρ$ meson masses $M^{i=0,1,2,3,4}_ρ$. With fixed magnetic field, they decrease with temperature, and approach the mass sum of their constituent quarks at high temperature. The mass solution $M^{i}_ρ$ for different mesons $ρ_+^{0,\pm}$ and $ρ_0^{0,\pm}$ may become degenerate at finite magnetic field and temperature.

</details>

### [79] [On Dingle's rebuttal of the special theory of relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00057)
*Justo Pastor Lambare*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文从历史与教学角度回顾了赫伯特·丁格尔（Helbert Dingle）在1972年著作《Science At the Crossroads》中对狭义相对论（special relativity）一致性的批评，指出其论证存在谬误，并分析了这一事件在物理学史及更广泛科学史上的特殊意义。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 丁格尔对狭义相对论的错误批判在“民科”社群中长期流传，本文旨在从历史与教学的双重视角澄清这一谬误，并揭示其作为科学史案例的特殊价值。

Method: 采用历史综述与教学分析相结合的方法，回顾丁格尔事件的发生背景、论证内容及其后续影响。

Result: 丁格尔的论证本质上是谬误的（fallacious），但该事件成为物理学史中一个奇特篇章，并在民科社群中持续被援引。

Conclusion: 丁格尔的案例兼具历史与教学意义，有助于理解科学争议的形成与传播机制，以及错误论证在非专业群体中的长期生命力。

Abstract: In his 1972 book Science At the Crossroads, Helbert Dingle attacked the consistency of special relativity through a fallacious argument championed by the crank community even to this day. Dingle's affair is a curious chapter in the history of physics and, more generally, science. We briefly review Dingle's case from a historical and didactic perspective.
