### [80] [Training a neural network to rapidly identify candidate gravitational-wave events in the lower mass gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00391)
*Nayyer Raza,Man Leong Chan,Daryl Haggard,Ashish Mahabal,Jess McIver,Audrey Durand,Alexandre Larouche,Hadi Moazen*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文训练了一个名为GWSkyNet-MassGap的神经网络模型，用于同时预测引力波候选事件中是否存在低质量间隙（lower mass gap）内的天体成分（$P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$）以及是否涉及中子星（NS）（$P_{\mathrm{NS}}$），从而辅助电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart）的后续观测决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大质量中子星（neutron star, NS）与最小质量黑洞（black hole, BH）之间的边界物理尚不确定。目前电磁观测在约2–5 $M_{\odot}$的所谓低质量间隙（lower mass gap）内缺乏发现，但引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测表明该间隙可能并非空无一物。快速判断候选引力波事件是否包含该间隙内的天体，有助于评估电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart）的可探测性，从而指导后续观测资源的分配。

Method: 作者训练了一个名为GWSkyNet-MassGap的神经网络（neural network）模型，该模型能够同时预测候选并合事件中存在低质量间隙组分的概率（$P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$）和涉及中子星的概率（$P_{\mathrm{NS}}$）。模型通过推断源的啁啾质量（chirp mass）信息来产生上述预测。

Result: 模型对啁啾质量$\mathcal{M}_c\gtrsim15~M_{\odot}$的高质量并合事件能够做出正确预测；但对于低质量系统，预测精度较差，因为需要双星质量比（binary mass ratio）信息来打破质量简并（mass degeneracy）。在LVK第四次观测运行第一阶段（O4a）的候选事件上，模型对$P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$的平均预测误差为9%，对$P_{\mathrm{NS}}$的平均预测误差为6%。

Conclusion: GWSkyNet-MassGap模型能够快速预测引力波候选事件中的质量间隙组分和中子星属性，具有一定准确性。未来可通过进一步开发，使其快速预测候选事件的源啁啾质量（source chirp mass），以应用于后续观测运行。

Abstract: The physics governing the boundary between the most massive neutron stars (NSs) and the least massive black holes (BHs) is currently uncertain, but could potentially be constrained with new observations. While NSs have been observed with masses up to $\sim2~M_{\odot}$, there is a dearth of electromagnetic observations of compact objects in the $\sim2-5~M_{\odot}$ range, known as the lower mass gap. Recent observations of gravitational-wave (GW) signals from binary mergers detected by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration indicate that this gap is likely not empty. Rapidly distinguishing whether a candidate GW event has components in this purported mass gap can indicate the likelihood of a detectable electromagnetic counterpart, and thus inform decisions for follow-up observations. In this work we train a neural network model, GWSkyNet-MassGap, that simultaneously predicts the probability that a candidate merger has a component in the lower mass gap ($P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$) and the probability that it involves a NS ($P_{\mathrm{NS}}$). We find that the model is able to infer information about the source chirp mass to predict $P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$ and $P_{\mathrm{NS}}$, leading to correct predictions for high-mass mergers with $\mathcal{M}_c\gtrsim15~M_{\odot}$, but less accurate predictions for lower-mass systems which require knowledge of the binary mass ratio to break the mass degeneracy. For candidate events in the first part of LVK's fourth observing run (O4a), the model has a mean prediction error of 9% for $P_{\mathrm{MassGap}}$ and 6% for $P_{\mathrm{NS}}$. The model could be further developed to rapidly predict the source chirp mass for candidate events in future observing runs.

</details>


### [81] [Beyond Bragg-Mirrors for Gravitational Wave Telescopes: A Fabrication Tolerant Hybrid Metasurface-Bragg Mirror Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00714)
*Christian Kranhold,Mika Gaedtke,Markus Walther,Falk Eilenberger,Stefanie Kroker,Thomas Siefke*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文针对ET-Pathfinder引力波探测器的需求，提出了一种混合超表面-布拉格（hybrid metasurface–Bragg）反射镜设计，通过将容错性高的单层超表面与反共振法布里-珀罗（Fabry–Perot）间隔层及缩减的布拉格（Bragg）堆栈相结合，在考虑制造公差和线边缘粗糙度（line-edge roughness）的条件下实现了约99.9%的反射率（95%产率水平），并通过仅七层布拉格对补偿剩余透射，使总热位移噪声比项目预算低约一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器（gravitational-wave detectors）中高反射率测试质量镜的涂层热噪声（coating thermal noise）是10–300 Hz频段的主要限制因素，ET-Pathfinder需要在1.55微米波长下同时实现极高反射率与低温低热噪声。传统介质布拉格（Bragg）反射镜反射率高但涂层过厚，而超表面（metasurface）镜可减少涂层噪声却受制于制造公差和线边缘粗糙度（line-edge roughness），因此需要一种能兼顾光学性能与制造可行性的新方案。

Method: 设计了一种混合超表面-布拉格（hybrid metasurface–Bragg）反射镜结构，包括容错性高的单层超表面、反共振法布里-珀罗（Fabry–Perot）间隔层和缩减的介质布拉格（Bragg）堆栈。光学性能通过全波电磁模拟（full-wave electromagnetic simulations）评估，制造稳健性采用截断高斯蒙特卡罗分析（truncated-Gaussian Monte Carlo analysis）进行评价，线边缘粗糙度（line-edge roughness）作为系统性边缘平滑效应纳入考虑。

Result: 理想超表面反射率超过99.999%；考虑制造不确定性和线边缘粗糙度后，95%产率水平下超表面反射率限制在约99.9%。通过仅七层布拉格（Bragg）对即可补偿剩余透射；该混合构型的总热位移噪声（total thermal displacement noise）比ET-Pathfinder预期的涂层噪声预算（coating-noise budget）低约一个数量级。

Conclusion: 受制造限制的超表面反射率可在混合架构中得到补偿，这为下一代引力波探测器实现了减薄的涂层厚度和降低的热噪声，验证了该混合反射镜概念的可行性和工程适用性。

Abstract: Coating thermal noise in high-reflectivity test-mass mirrors is a major limitation for future gravitational-wave detectors, especially in the 10--300 Hz band. ET-Pathfinder therefore requires mirror coatings that combine very high reflectance at 1.55 micrometer with low thermal noise under cryogenic conditions. Conventional dielectric Bragg mirrors provide high reflectance but require thick coatings, whereas metasurface mirrors can reduce coating-related noise but are limited by fabrication tolerances and line-edge roughness. We present a hybrid metasurface--Bragg mirror concept tailored to ET-Pathfinder. The design combines a fabrication-tolerant one-layer metasurface, an anti-resonant Fabry--Perot spacer, and a reduced dielectric Bragg stack. Optical performance is evaluated using full-wave electromagnetic simulations, while fabrication robustness is assessed with a truncated-Gaussian Monte Carlo analysis. Line-edge roughness is included as a systematic edge-smoothing effect. The resulting reflectance distributions are used to determine the minimum Bragg-stack support required to meet system-level specifications. The ideal metasurface exceeds 99.999% reflectance. When fabrication uncertainties and line-edge roughness are included, the metasurface reflectance is limited to about 99.9% at the 95% yield level. The remaining transmission can be compensated by a supporting Bragg stack with as few as seven layer pairs. For this configuration, the hybrid mirror achieves a total thermal displacement noise about one order of magnitude below the projected ET-Pathfinder coating-noise budget. These results show that fabrication-limited metasurface reflectance can be compensated within a hybrid architecture, enabling reduced coating thickness and thermal noise for next-generation gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>

### [82] [A New Robust Constraint on the Self-interaction Cross-section of Dark Matter with Double Radio Relic Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00093)
*M. James Jee,Dongak Park,Wonki Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出利用双射电遗迹（double radio relics）测量的激波间距离（shock-to-shock distance）作为并合计时器，来约束暗物质自相互作用截面（SICS）。通过对11个对称双射电遗迹星系团并合系统的分析，得到暗物质自相互作用截面σ/m < 0.22 cm²/g 的68%上限，这是首个完全边缘化质量不确定性、视角、碰撞速度、并合相位、碰撞参数和气体轮廓斜率等多种系统不确定性的星系团碰撞约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 并合星系团是测量暗物质自相互作用截面（self-interaction cross-section, SICS）的理想实验室，但此前基于星系-质量偏移（galaxy-mass offsets）的方法受限于数值模拟中偏移量本身很小，且并合相位、几何和初始条件未知，导致解释复杂化。

Method: 引入激波间距离（shock-to-shock distance，由双射电遗迹示踪）作为并合计时器（merger chronometer），用于标记过中心后（post-pericenter）的动力学相位。由于并合激波的传播速度几乎与SICS无关，而暗物质晕间距离受自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）拖曳效应而减小，因此两个距离的比值可直接转化为对σ/m的约束。

Result: 对11个拥有对称双射电遗迹（symmetric double radio relics）的星系团并合系统进行分析，得到暗物质自相互作用截面σ/m < 0.22 cm²/g 的68%置信上限。这是首个从星系团碰撞中完全边缘化质量不确定性、视角、碰撞速度、并合相位、碰撞参数和气体轮廓斜率等参数得到的约束。

Conclusion: 新提出的激波间距离方法有效克服了传统星系-质量偏移方法的局限性，为利用并合星系团约束暗物质自相互作用提供了更鲁棒的途径。所得约束完全边缘化了多种系统不确定性，增强了结果的可靠性。

Abstract: Merging galaxy clusters are a promising laboratory for measuring the self-interaction cross-section (SICS) of dark matter. However, previous studies have focused on galaxy-mass offsets, which numerical simulations have shown to be intrinsically small because galaxies remain tightly coupled to the dominant dark matter potential even with significant self-interaction. Their interpretation is further complicated by unknowns of the merger phase, geometry, and initial conditions. In this paper, we overcome these obstacles by introducing the shock-to-shock distance, traced by double radio relics, as a merger chronometer that time-stamps the post-pericenter dynamical phase. Because the propagation speed of merger shocks is nearly independent of the SICS, while the halo-to-halo distance is depressed by SIDM-induced drag, the ratio of the two distances translates directly into a constraint on sigma/m. Applying this method to a gold sample of eleven cluster mergers hosting symmetric double radio relics, we determine a 68% upper limit on the SICS of sigma/m < 0.22 cm^2/g. This is the first constraint from cluster collisions that fully marginalizes over mass uncertainty, viewing angle, collision speed, merger phase, impact parameter, and gas profile slope.

</details>


### [83] [A consistent formulation of stochastic inflation I: Non-Markovian effects and issues beyond linear perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00476)
*Diego Cruces,Tomotaka Kuroda*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）中非马尔可夫性（non-Markovianity）的起源及其对非线性扰动理论（nonlinear perturbation theory）的影响。通过施温格-凯尔迪什（Schwinger–Keldysh）形式，将噪声项分解为“确定性”与“随机性”两部分，发现二次噪声项（quadratic-noise terms）对一致描述非线性扰动至关重要，而标准截断通常不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在随机暴胀的施温格-凯尔迪什框架中，红外（IR）朗之万方程（Langevin equations）的噪声项由紫外（UV）模式在随机红外背景上演化决定，而紫外模式演化依赖于红外扇区的历史，导致内在的非马尔可夫动力学。现有研究通常忽略二次噪声项，本文旨在澄清非马尔可夫性的微扰结构并评估该截断的合理性。

Method: 采用微扰方法，将紫外模式解推导至二阶，并将噪声贡献分解为两部分：一是通过对一阶紫外解围绕背景轨迹进行泛函泰勒展开（functional Taylor expansion）得到的确定性贡献；二是来自紫外模式方程中噪声变量二次项的真正随机贡献。

Result: 在标准截断下，确定性贡献在吸引子（attractor）背景中退化为马尔可夫修正，而在非吸引子（non-attractor）相中可能变为依赖于历史的非马尔可夫项。此外，随机贡献与确定性贡献处于同一微扰阶次，表明标准截断通常不一致，二次噪声项对于非线性扰动的自洽处理是必要的。

Conclusion: 本文阐明了随机暴胀中非马尔可夫性的微扰结构，并为在标准形式之外系统处理二次噪声效应提供了基础。

Abstract: We investigate the origin of non-Markovianity in stochastic inflation and its implications for nonlinear perturbation theory. In the Schwinger--Keldysh formulation, the noise terms sourcing the infrared (IR) Langevin equations are determined by ultraviolet (UV) modes evolving on top of the stochastic IR background. Since the UV-mode evolution generally depends on the past history of the IR sector, the resulting stochastic dynamics is intrinsically non-Markovian. Working perturbatively, we derive the UV-mode solutions up to second order and decompose the corresponding noise contributions into two parts. The first is a ``deterministic'' contribution, generated by the functional Taylor expansion of the first-order UV solution around the background trajectory. The second is a genuinely ``stochastic'' contribution, originating from terms in the UV-mode equations that are quadratic in the noise variables and are usually neglected in the standard formulation of stochastic inflation. Under this conventional truncation, the deterministic contribution reduces to a Markovian correction in attractor backgrounds, whereas it could become history dependent in non-attractor phases and gives rise to non-Markovian terms involving integrals over first-order IR perturbations. We finally show that the stochastic contribution is of the same perturbative order as the deterministic one, which indicate that the conventional truncation is generically inconsistent and quadratic-noise terms may be required for a consistent treatment of nonlinear perturbations in stochastic inflation. Our analysis clarifies the perturbative structure of non-Markovianity and provides the basis for a systematic treatment of quadratic-noise effects beyond the standard formulation.

</details>


### [84] [DESI and Gravitational Wave Constraints Challenge Quintessential α-Attractor Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00735)
*Changcheng Jing,George Alestas,Sachiko Kuroyanagi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文对α-吸引子精质通胀（alpha-attractor quintessential inflation）模型进行了全数值研究，从暴涨期到暗能量主导期完整追踪标量场演化，并精确计算了原初引力波谱。结合DESI、ACT及ΔNeff约束，发现该模型在计入引力波对有效相对论自由度贡献的约束后被排除，主要原因是引力波丰度受限时标量谱指数ns过小。最终给出了受约束参数下的原初引力波功率谱，指出其低频部分有望被未来CMB B模式实验探测，高频部分可被引力波干涉仪实验探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精质通胀（quintessential inflation）模型能同时描述暴涨（inflation）和动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy），后者近期因DESI观测结果而备受关注。该模型在暴涨后存在动力学主导（kination）阶段，可在高频增强原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves），因此有必要利用最新观测数据对其进行精确约束。

Method: 采用全数值（fully numerical）方法，从暴涨期到暗能量主导期完整追踪标量场演化。利用包括DESI和ACT在内的最新观测数据约束模型参数，并计入引力波对有效相对论自由度数目（ΔNeff）的贡献所施加的限制。

Result: 一旦计入ΔNeff约束，该模型因标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）ns过小而被排除。在约束后的参数值下，给出了原初引力波功率谱（primordial gravitational wave power spectrum），表明低频部分可为未来CMB B模式实验所探测，高频部分可为引力波干涉仪实验所探测。

Conclusion: α-吸引子精质通胀模型在同时满足ΔNeff约束与观测数据时面临困难，其预测的ns值过小导致模型被否定。尽管如此，约束后的引力波谱仍为未来低频CMB B模式实验和高频引力波干涉仪实验提供了可检验的探测前景。

Abstract: Quintessential inflation models provide a framework that simultaneously describes inflation and dynamical dark energy, the latter of which has recently received growing support from DESI observations. A distinctive feature of these models is the kination phase after inflation, which enhances primordial gravitational waves at high frequencies. In this work, we study a class of alpha-attractor quintessential inflation models using a fully numerical approach that follows the scalar-field evolution from inflation to the dark-energy-dominated era, allowing us to compute with high precision both the dynamics of dark energy and the primordial gravitational wave spectrum. Using the latest observational data, including DESI and ACT, we constrain the model parameters and show that the model becomes disfavored once constraints from the gravitational-wave contribution to the effective number of relativistic degrees of freedom, Δ Neff, are included. This is because the model predicts a scalar spectral index ns that becomes too small to remain consistent with observations when the gravitational-wave abundance is constrained to stay below the Δ Neff bound. Finally, we present the resulting primordial gravitational wave power spectrum computed using our constrained parameter values, which highlights prospects for detection by future CMB B-mode experiments at low frequencies and by gravitational-wave interferometer experiments at high frequencies.

</details>

### [85] [Classical limit of the Pauli-Fierz dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00228)
*Lucas Jougla,Nikolai Leopold*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在经典极限（$\hbar \rightarrow 0$）下，严格推导出Pauli-Fierz哈密顿量（Pauli-Fierz Hamiltonian）生成的薛定谔演化（Schrödinger evolution）可由牛顿-麦克斯韦方程（Newton-Maxwell equations）有效近似，并通过显式的收敛速率估计验证了近似对特殊初始数据类的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在从量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）的非相对论模型出发，在经典极限下严格建立其与经典电动力学（classical electrodynamics）牛顿-麦克斯韦方程之间的联系。

Method: 采用经典的Pauli-Fierz哈密顿量作为非相对论量子电动力学模型，在$\hbar \rightarrow 0$的经典极限下，对薛定谔时间演化进行渐近分析，并推导出收敛速率（rate of convergence）的显式估计。

Result: 严格推导出牛顿-麦克斯韦方程可作为薛定谔演化的有效动力学近似，并给出了显式的收敛速率估计，为特定初始数据类（a special class of initial data）下的近似有效性提供了理论证明。

Conclusion: 该工作通过另一种推导途径补充了先前研究，提供了收敛速率的定量估计，从而验证了在经典极限下量子电动力学向经典电动力学过渡的严格性。

Abstract: We study the Schrödinger evolution generated by the Pauli-Fierz Hamiltonian, a model for nonrelativistic quantum electrodynamics, in the classical limit $\hbar \rightarrow 0$. In this regime, we rigorously derive the Newton-Maxwell equations of classical electrodynamics as effective dynamics approximating the time evolution. Our result complements prior work by an alternative derivation that provides explicit estimates on the rate of convergence, justifying the validity of the approximation for a special class of initial data.

### [86] [Unraveling the Bott spiral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00316)
*Arun Debray,Cameron Krulewski,Luuk Stehouwer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建并计算了Queiroz–Khalaf–Stern研究的对称性保护拓扑相（SPTs）Bott螺旋的同伦论模型。利用K-理论（K-theory）和反射正性可逆场论（IFTs）分别建模自由与相互作用费米子SPTs，并定义了Atiyah–Bott–Shapiro定向的一个扭曲推广以构造自由到相互作用映射，同时定义了IFTs的螺旋映射来模拟该情境下的维度约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Hason–Komargodski–Thorngren提出的关于该背景下维度约化的问题，并揭示自由到相互作用映射的同伦论一般性质，特别是K-理论与IFTs对对称性数据的敏感度差异。

Method: 采用同伦论（homotopy theory）方法，使用K-理论建模自由费米子SPTs，使用反射正性可逆场论（reflection-positive invertible field theories）建模相互作用费米子SPTs；定义Atiyah–Bott–Shapiro定向的扭曲推广以构造自由到相互作用映射；定义IFTs的螺旋映射（spiral maps）来模拟维度约化；使用初等交换2-群的扭曲ko-同调（twisted ko-homology）的一个新型4-周期描述进行计算。

Result: IFTs比K-理论对输入对称性数据更敏感——仅指定Altland–Zirnbauer类不足以定义IFT的对称性类型；相互作用侧Bott周期性的残余依赖于两个32阶超特殊群（extraspecial groups of order 32）之间的同构。

Conclusion: 建立了SPTs Bott螺旋的自由和相互作用模型间的同伦论联系，为理解维度约化提供了新框架，并揭示了对称性数据在自由与相互作用理论中的本质差异。

Abstract: We construct and compute a homotopy-theoretic model for the Bott spiral of symmetry-protected topological phases (SPTs) studied by Queiroz--Khalaf--Stern. We model free and interacting fermionic SPTs using K-theory and reflection-positive invertible field theories (IFTs), resp., and define a twisted generalization of the Atiyah--Bott--Shapiro orientation to produce a free-to-interacting map. We also define and compute spiral maps of IFTs to model dimensional reduction in this context, answering a question of Hason--Komargodski--Thorngren. Our analysis highlights two general aspects of homotopical free-to-interacting maps. First, IFTs are more sensitive than K-theory is to the input symmetry data; in particular, the specification of an Altland--Zirnbauer class is insufficient information to define symmetry type for an IFT. Second, the remnant of Bott periodicity on the interacting side relies on an isomorphism of two extraspecial groups of order 32. Our computations use a novel 4-periodic description of a sector of the twisted ko-homology of elementary abelian 2-groups.

### [87] [Generalized Fourier Transforms for Momentum-Space Construction on Riemannian Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00403)
*Seramika Ariwahjoedi,Muhammad Farchani Rosyid,Andika Kusuma Wijaya*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在任意黎曼流形上通过谱分解定义广义傅里叶变换（GFT）的方法，解决了弯曲空间中动量空间的简并性问题，并建立了基于几何对称性的动量标签空间分类框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将傅里叶分析从平坦空间推广到弯曲空间时，谱简并性（spectral degeneracy）使得传统“动量空间”概念不再清晰，亟需建立一种系统化的几何方法以在黎曼流形上定义有意义的模式分解。

Method: 在黎曼流形上通过拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的谱分解定义广义傅里叶变换（Generalized Fourier Transform, GFT），要求该变换是等距同构且其核对角化该算子。通过构造局部、对称性适配的最大阿贝尔交换集（maximal Abelian commuting set, MASA）来解析简并扇区，提出生成这些交换算子的构造性算法，并引入双重分类体系。

Result: 证明了所定义的GFT满足广义Parseval-Plancherel定理；动量标签空间F（离散、连续或混合类型）反映了几何对称性约束；区分了由真等距群（true isometries）引起的酉变换与由坐标适配的简并解析方案引起的k空间标记变化，二者在L²[Σ]上仍保持酉等价。

Conclusion: 本研究为弯曲空间上的模式分解提供了基于对称性适配的调和分析框架，为后续动力学应用奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We extend Fourier analysis to curved spaces by defining a Generalized Fourier Transform (GFT) on any Riemannian manifold $Σ$ via spectral decomposition. Under minimal requirements that the transform is an isometric isomorphism and has a kernel diagonalizing the Laplace-Beltrami operator, we prove that the GFT satisfies a generalized Parseval-Plancherel theorem. To resolve the spectral degeneracy that obscures "momentum space" in such settings, we require the degenerate sector to be resolved by a local, symmetry-adapted maximal Abelian commuting set (a fiberwise MASA), constructed from geometric differential operators, most notably from Killing data when such symmetries are available. We provide a constructive algorithm for generating these commuting operators and show that the resulting momentum label spaces $\mathcal{F}$ (discrete, continuous, or mixed) reflect geometric symmetry constraints. We introduce a dual classification: (i) by MASA completeness and Stackel separability, and (ii) by the topology of $\mathcal{F}$. Finally, we distinguish unitary changes induced by true isometries (which preserve the GFT structure) from changes of coordinate-adapted degeneracy resolution/separation schemes, which may induce inequivalent $k$-space labelings (e.g. Cartesian vs spherical constructions in $\mathbb{R}^{3}$) while remaining unitarily equivalent on $\mathcal{L}^{2}\left[Σ\right]$. This symmetry-adapted harmonic analysis is intended as a foundation for curved-space mode decompositions; dynamical applications are developed in the subsequent work.

</details>


### [88] [Strong-disorder expansion of the root-averaged density of states for the Anderson model on the Bethe lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00478)
*Masahiro Kaminaga*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了强无序条件下Bethe格点上Anderson模型的根平均态密度（root-averaged density of states），证明其具有全纯延拓（holomorphic continuation）和实解析密度，并给出了强无序展开的首项与修正项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强无序体系中，根平均谱测度（root-averaged spectral measure）的性质尚需严格理论刻画，特别是其解析性与展开形式。

Method: 结合树图上的随机游走展开（random-walk expansion）与单点Stieltjes变换的复分析论证（complex-analytic argument），证明缩放后的平均对角预解式（scaled averaged diagonal resolvent）具有全纯延拓。

Result: 根平均态密度测度在缩放能窗（scaled energy window）$λI$上绝对连续，密度函数实解析（real analytic）且具有有限阶强无序展开；所有奇次系数为零，偶次系数由树上短闭游走的占据分布（occupation profiles of short closed walks）决定；对均匀单点分布显式计算了首个非零修正项。

Conclusion: 该工作为强无序Bethe格点Anderson模型的根平均态密度提供了严格的解析性证明和显式展开结构，揭示了树图几何与无序分布的相互作用。

Abstract: We study the root-averaged density of states for the Anderson model on the Bethe lattice in the strong-disorder regime. Here the density of states means the root-averaged spectral measure, not a finite-volume eigenvalue counting limit. We assume that the single-site distribution has compact support and has a locally analytic density on an interval $I^\sharp$ containing a given interval $I$. Combining the random-walk expansion on the tree with a complex-analytic argument for the single-site Stieltjes transforms, we prove that the scaled averaged diagonal resolvent has a holomorphic continuation to a complex neighborhood of $I$ for all sufficiently large $λ$. By the Stieltjes inversion formula, the root-averaged density of states measure is absolutely continuous on the scaled energy window $λI$, and its density is real analytic and has a finite-order strong-disorder expansion there. In the scaled form $E=λξ$, the leading coefficient is the local density of the single-site distribution. All odd coefficients vanish, and the higher coefficients are finite sums determined by occupation profiles of short closed walks on the tree. For the uniform single-site distribution, we compute the first nonzero correction term explicitly.

</details>


### [89] [Reflection Symmetry, APS Boundary Conditions, and Equivariant Spectral Flow on a Warped Cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00589)
*Taro Kimura,Sanchita Sharma*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限扭曲圆柱上扭曲狄拉克算子的反射对称性与Atiyah-Patodi-Singer (APS)边界条件。证明了仅当全纯参数$2A\in\mathbb Z$时反射提升为酉对称，并分析了反射迹在APS调和空间上的局域化行为；进而研究了参数依赖情形下的谱流与不变量的分解及退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扭曲狄拉克算子在有限扭曲圆柱上的反射对称性与APS边界条件的相容性，以及参数变化下谱流（spectral flow）与等变不变量的结构。

Method: 利用反射提升条件推导全纯参数$A$的整性约束；通过角动量模式配对与APS块的酉等价性分析反射迹的局域化；结合$O(2)$等变性与$RO(O(2))$值分解处理参数依赖情形。

Result: 反射提升为酉对称当且仅当$2A\in\mathbb Z$；反射迹在APS调和空间上局域到唯一的自配对零模扇区。固定规范平凡全纯时谱流具有$RO(O(2))$值分解；全纯变化时等变性消失，不变量退化为模二奇偶性（mod-two parity）。

Conclusion: 反射对称性对扭曲狄拉克算子的APS边界条件施加了严格的量化条件，且参数依赖下等变不变量的结构会从表示环值退化为符号级不变量。

Abstract: We study reflection symmetry and Atiyah-Patodi-Singer (APS) boundary conditions for twisted Dirac operators on a finite warped cylinder. For a complex line twist with holonomy parameter $A$, we show that the reflection lifts to a unitary symmetry of the twisted Dirac setting if and only if $2A\in\mathbb Z$. In the resulting reflection-compatible fixed-holonomy case, reflection pairs opposite shifted angular modes, and the paired APS blocks are unitarily equivalent. The reflection trace on the APS harmonic space localizes to the unique self-paired zero-mode sector. We then turn to parameter-dependent versions of the model. For fixed gauge-trivial holonomy, the family remains pointwise \(O(2)\)-equivariant, and its spectral flow admits an \(RO(O(2))\)-valued decomposition. For genuinely varying holonomy, pointwise \(O(2)\)-equivariance is lost along the path. The representation-ring-valued invariant is then replaced by a residual sign-level invariant: the mod-two parity of the APS crossing events.

### [90] [Cartan Fluxes in $SU(3)$ Lattice Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25003)
*Tereza Mendes,Luis E. Oxman,Gustavo M. Simões,Rafael C. S. Tonhon*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种在格点杨-米尔斯理论（lattice Yang-Mills theory）中探测中心涡旋（center vortices）和磁单极（monopoles）的新方法。该方法通过固定最大阿贝尔规范（Maximal Abelian gauge, MAG）并适当分解链接组态以寻找所谓的卡当流（Cartan fluxes），从而敏感地检测中心荷（center charges）的内在简并性（intrinsic degeneracy）。讨论对SU(N)规范理论具有一般性，但应用主要聚焦于SU(3)情形，并指出对SU(2)情形该参数化等价于通常方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中心涡旋和磁单极在格点杨-米尔斯理论中扮演关键角色，但传统探测方法未能充分敏感地检测这些拓扑物体（topological objects）之间相互作用与关联所依赖的中心荷（center charges）的内在简并性（intrinsic degeneracy）。现有方法在捕捉这一简并性方面存在局限，因此需要开发一种对中心荷内在结构更敏感的新探测手段。

Method: 该方法基于固定最大阿贝尔规范（Maximal Abelian gauge, MAG），对链接组态（link configuration）进行适当分解，从而寻找所谓的卡当流（Cartan fluxes）。通过这种方式，该方法能够对中心荷（center charges）的内在简并性（intrinsic degeneracy）产生响应，实现对中心涡旋和磁单极的探测。讨论在SU(N)规范理论框架下具有一般性，但应用主要集中在SU(3)情形。

Result: 对于SU(2)情形，该文提出的参数化（parametrization）方案等价于通常的标准方案。论文的分析表明该方法能够有效检测中心荷的内在简并性，从而更准确地揭示中心涡旋与磁单极之间的相互作用与关联。

Conclusion: 该文提出的基于最大阿贝尔规范和卡当流分解的新方法，为在格点杨-米尔斯理论中探测中心涡旋和磁单极提供了一种对中心荷内在简并性敏感的改进手段。该方法在SU(3)情形下具有新的应用价值，而对SU(2)情形则与已有标准方法等价，因而为更广泛的SU(N)规范理论中的拓扑结构研究提供了统一的框架。

Abstract: We propose and analyze a new method of detecting center vortices and monopoles in lattice Yang-Mills theory. This procedure is sensitive to the intrinsic degeneracy of the center charges, which play a crucial role in how these topological objects interact and correlate with one another. Our approach is based on fixing the Maximal Abelian gauge (MAG) and decomposing the link configuration in a suitable way to look for so-called Cartan fluxes. Our discussion is general for $SU(N)$ gauge theory, but we focus our applications on the $SU(3)$ case. For the $SU(2)$ case, our proposed parametrization is equivalent to the usual one.

</details>

### [91] [Once-excited random walks on general trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.16934)
*Duy-Bao Le,Tuan-Minh Nguyen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义树上一次激发随机游走（once-excited random walk）的相变行为，其中每个顶点放置一块“饼干”，首次访问时游走呈有偏随机游走，之后退化为对称随机游走；在随机环境中，证明了在多项式增长的树上存在瞬态性与递归性之间的尖锐相变（sharp phase transition），临界阈值由树的分支-破产数（branching-ruin number）决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在激发随机游走（excited random walk）模型中，现有研究多聚焦于特定树结构或确定性偏置参数，尚缺乏对一般树上随机偏置环境下相变行为的统一刻画。

Method: 采用随机环境建模，将偏置参数（bias parameters）设为独立随机变量；在每个顶点放置单块“饼干”，首次访问时激发有偏随机游走，之后退化为对称随机游走；利用分支-破产数作为树结构的关键度量。

Result: 在多项式增长的一般树上，该过程表现出瞬态性与递归性之间的尖锐相变；相变临界阈值由树的分支-破产数唯一确定。

Conclusion: 该结果将激发随机游走的相变理论从特定的树结构推广至一般多项式增长树，为随机环境中非马氏过程（non-Markovian process）的临界行为提供了统一分析框架。

Abstract: We study once-excited random walks on general trees, modeled by placing a single "cookie" at each vertex. Each cookie acts as a metaphorical reward that is consumed upon the first visit to the vertex where the cookie is placed. On that initial visit, the walk is in an excited state and behaves like a biased random walk. Once the cookie is consumed, the process reverts to a symmetric random walk on all subsequent visits. We consider a random environment in which the bias parameters are independent random variables. We prove that the process exhibits a sharp phase transition between transience and recurrence on general trees with polynomial growth, where the critical threshold is determined by the branching-ruin number of the tree.

</details>


### [92] [Persistence in perturbed contact models in continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00148)
*S. Pirogov,E Zhizhina*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究局部灾难是否会导致种群灭绝，通过放宽接触过程（contact process）的临界性条件，证明死亡率局部高峰通常不会导致灭绝，并利用费曼-卡克公式（Feynman-Kac formula）刻画了非临界条件下的不变测度族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者在前期工作（PZ-PPI）中已为局部紧度量空间上的接触过程建立了不变测度存在的充分条件，其中关键假设是临界平衡条件（critical regime condition）——即平均出生率与死亡率之间保持平衡。本文旨在探究当该平衡条件被打破（即非临界情形）时，系统是否仍能维持不变测度，以及局部灾害是否必然导致种群灭绝。

Method: 弃用临界性条件，假设出生率与死亡率的平均平衡被打破。此时，接触模型的关联函数（correlation functions）演化由一类非局部卷积型算子（nonlocal convolution type operator）加上负势函数（negative potential）的扰动所决定。

Result: 证明了死亡率局部高峰通常不会导致种群灭绝。此外，即便没有临界性条件，仍然存在一族不变测度（invariant measures）。

Conclusion: 在非临界条件下，局部接触过程仍具有丰富的不变测度结构，这些测度可通过费曼-卡克公式加以描述。该结论表明局部灾害并不构成种群灭绝的充分原因。

Abstract: Can a local disaster lead to extinction? We answer this question in this work. In the paper \cite{PZ-PPI} we considered contact processes on locally compact metric spaces with state dependent birth and death rates and formulated sufficient conditions on the rates that ensure the existence of invariant measures. One of the crucial conditions in \cite{PZ-PPI} was the critical regime condition, which meant the existence of a balance between birth and death rates in average. In the present work, we reject the criticality condition and suppose that the balance condition is violated. This implies that the evolution of the correlation functions of the contact model under consideration is determined by a nonlocal convolution type operator perturbed by a (negative) potential. We show that local peaks in mortality do not typically lead to extinction. We prove that a family of invariant measures exists even without the criticality condition and these measures can be described using the Feynman-Kac formula.

</details>


### [93] [Royen's proof of the Gaussian correlation inequality as a supersymmetric dimensional reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00533)
*Yichao Huang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文从超对称（supersymmetric）视角重新审视Royen对高斯相关不等式（Gaussian correlation inequality）的证明，指出其关键元素可自然解释为从$\mathbb{R}^{3|2}$到$\mathbb{R}^{1|0}$的超对称维度约化（supersymmetric dimensional reduction），并将该推广延伸至半整数多变量伽马分布情形，展示了超对称局域化方法（supersymmetric localization method）在证明连续参数相关不等式中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高斯相关不等式是概率论与统计力学中的一个重要不等式，Royen给出了一个简洁但直观背景不清晰的证明。作者希望从超对称视角揭示该证明的几何本质，并为超对称方法在相关不等式中的应用提供范例。

Method: 采用超对称维度约化框架，将Royen证明中的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）论证中的辅助多变量伽马分布（multivariate Gamma distributions）重新解释为超对称径向变量（supersymmetric radial variable）的体分量（body），并从$\mathbb{R}^{3|2}$约化至$\mathbb{R}^{1|0}$；进一步将半整数情形推广为从$\mathbb{R}^{k+2|2}$到$\mathbb{R}^{k|0}$的维度约化。

Result: Royen证明中的关键数学对象（如多变量伽马分布）在超对称框架下获得了自然的几何解释；超对称维度约化方法能够统一处理整数与半整数多变量伽马分布情形；展示了超对称局域化方法在证明含连续参数的相关不等式中的有效性。

Conclusion: 超对称方法为理解高斯相关不等式的证明提供了新的几何视角，并可作为一种通用工具推广至更广泛的相关不等式问题。

Abstract: We revisit Royen's proof of the Gaussian correlation inequality from a supersymmetric point of view. Many key elements in Royen's proof of this inequality have natural geometric interpretations in terms of supersymmetric dimensional reduction from $\mathbb{R}^{3|2}$ to $\mathbb{R}^{1|0}$. In particular, the auxiliary multivariate Gamma distributions appearing in Royen's Laplace-transform argument arise naturally as the body of a supersymmetric radial variable on $\mathbb{R}^{3|2}$. The generalization to the half-integer multivariate Gamma case also follows naturally as a dimensional reduction from $\mathbb{R}^{k+2|2}$ to $\mathbb{R}^{k|0}$. This provides an example in which the supersymmetric localization method is applied to prove correlation inequalities with continuous parameters.

### [94] [Cosmic Ray Physics with the KM3NeT Telescopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00232)
*Brían Ó Fearraigh*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了KM3NeT中微子望远镜利用大气缪子进行物理研究、探测器标定及系统误差约束的进展，并通过引入Daemonflux大气模型显著缓解了“缪子谜题”中数据与蒙特卡洛模拟之间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KM3NeT基础设施通过光电倍增管探测中微子与海水相互作用产生的切伦科夫辐射（Cherenkov radiation），同时也能探测穿透深海的大气缪子（atmospheric muons）。为了充分利用这些缪子进行物理分析，需要解决数据与蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟之间的系统性偏差——即“缪子谜题”（Muon Puzzle）。

Method: KM3NeT包含两个探测器：位于地中海不同深度的ARCA和ORCA，两者具有不同的规模与光探测元件密度，整体上提供广阔的大气缪子能量覆盖。研究基于KM3NeT/ORCA最初6个探测单元的数据进行大气缪子中微子通量测量，并将Daemonflux大气轻子模型引入蒙特卡洛事件生成器，用于模拟大气缪子簇射（muon bundles）。

Result: 引入Daemonflux模型后，大气缪子数据与蒙特卡洛模拟之间的偏差得到显著缓解，实现了对KM3NeT大气缪子数据的全面描述。同时，利用这些缪子进行了探测器标定，并约束了如仪器海水光学性质等系统不确定性。

Conclusion: KM3NeT中的大气缪子可用于多种物理研究，包括中微子通量测量、探测器标定以及系统误差约束。Daemonflux模型的引入有效解决了数据-模拟差异问题，提升了模拟的可靠性。

Abstract: The KM3NeT research infrastructure instruments a large volume of seawater using photomultiplier tubes, which are sensitive to the Cherenkov radiation stimulated by the products of neutrino interactions in the water, as well as that stimulated by atmospheric muons which penetrate the sea depths. The KM3NeT/ARCA and KM3NeT/ORCA detectors are situated at different depths in the Mediterranean Sea, with different extension and densities of the photo-detection elements. Although operating independently, taken as a whole the two detectors provide a wide energy coverage for the atmospheric muons flux. Through the detection and analysis of these atmospheric muons, a variety of physics studies are possible with the KM3NeT telescope. A measurement of the atmospheric muon neutrino flux has been carried out with data from the initial six detection units of the KM3NeT/ORCA detector. Relatedly to the atmospheric muon flux, the recent atmospheric lepton model `Daemonflux' has been incorporated into the KM3NeT Monte Carlo event generator for atmospheric muon bundles. This has resulted in a stark alleviation of the atmospheric muon data-Monte Carlo simulation discrepancy - a systemic issue in cosmic ray experiments referred to as the `Muon Puzzle' - and a comprehensive description of the atmospheric muon data in KM3NeT. These atmospheric muons are also used in the calibration of the detectors, as well as constraining systematic uncertainties in the detectors such as the optical properties of the instrumented seawater. An overview of these topics, and other cosmic ray analyses, is presented.

### [95] [Observation of the rare decay $η$ $\to$ $μ^+μ^-$e$^+$e$^-$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00615)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有衰变过程 η → μ⁺μ⁻e⁺e⁻ 此前尚未被实验观测到，研究旨在首次实现该衰变道的实验发现，并检验现有理论预测。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在CERN LHC采集的质心能量√s = 13.6 TeV的质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度38.0 fb⁻¹，2022年采集），利用高率双缪子触发（high-rate dimuon trigger）选取信号事件，并以 η → μ⁺μ⁻γ 衰变道作为归一化参考进行分支比测量。

Result: 测得分支比 ℬ(η → μ⁺μ⁻e⁺e⁻) = (2.4 ± 0.8)×10⁻⁶，不确定度包含统计与系统误差以及归一化道 ℬ(η → μ⁺μ⁻γ) 的不确定度。该数值比现有实验上限低约两个数量级。

Conclusion: CMS合作组首次实现了 η → μ⁺μ⁻e⁺e⁻ 稀有衰变的实验观测，测量结果与近期理论预言一致，显著推进了该衰变道的实验认知。

Abstract: A first observation of the rare decay $η$ $\to$ $μ^+μ^-$e$^+$e$^-$ is reported by the CMS Collaboration at the CERN LHC. The result is based on a proton-proton collision data sample at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 38.0 fb$^{-1}$, acquired in 2022 using a high-rate dimuon trigger. Using the $η$ $\to$ $μ^+μ^-γ$ decay channel for normalization, the branching fraction is measured to be $\mathcal{B}$($η$ $\to$ $μ^+μ^-$e$^+$e$^-$) = (2.4 $\pm$ 0.8)$\times$ 10$^{-6}$, with the uncertainty including statistical and systematic sources as well as the $\mathcal{B}$($η$ $\to$ $μ^+μ^-γ$) uncertainty. This result is close to two orders of magnitude smaller than the existing limit, and is consistent with recent theoretical predictions.

### [96] [Almost global large deviations principle for the KdV equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00484)
*Riccardo Berforini D'Aquino,Ricardo Grande*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了环面上带有随机初值的Korteweg-de Vries方程在长时间尺度上的极端波形成问题，建立了解的上确界的大偏差原理，揭示了弱非线性区间的极端波主要由色散聚焦（阶段准同步化）主导，而非共振能量交换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解可积系统中极端波的生成机制，特别是在长时间尺度下大幅值波动的概率行为与主导物理机制。

Method: 结合Birkhoff正则形式分析（Birkhoff normal form analysis）与概率论证，利用可积动力学的稳定性来控制长时间尺度下相位准同步化（phase quasi-synchronization）的概率。

Result: 对任意固定的自然数$n$，在多项式时间尺度$t \leq ε^{-n}$上建立了解的上确界的大偏差原理（large deviations principle），识别了观测到异常大幅值概率的领先阶渐近行为；证明弱非线性下色散聚焦是极端波形成的主导机制。

Conclusion: 在可积设定下，Fourier模量几乎守恒，极端波无法通过共振能量交换产生，只能源于相干结构或色散聚焦；后者在弱非线性区起主导作用。

Abstract: We study extreme wave formation for the Korteweg-de Vries equation on the torus with random initial data of average size $ε$. We establish a large deviations principle for the supremum of the solution over arbitrarily long polynomial timescales $t \leq ε^{-n}$ for any fixed natural number $n$. This identifies the leading-order asymptotics of the probability of observing unusually large amplitudes. In this integrable setting, the dynamics evolves on invariant tori where Fourier moduli are almost conserved, ruling out mechanisms for extreme wave formation based on resonant energy exchange. As a result, large amplitudes can only arise through coherent structures or dispersive focusing, which corresponds to the quasi-synchronization of many phases. We show that the latter is dominant in the weakly nonlinear regime. Our approach combines a Birkhoff normal form analysis with probabilistic arguments, exploiting the stability of the integrable dynamics to control the probability of phase quasi-synchronization over long timescales.

</details>

### [97] [Graph theoretic derivation of mutual linearity for transient probabilities and hitting time distributions in Markov networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00135)
*Julian B. Voits,Ulrich S. Schwarz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过全子式矩阵-树定理（all-minors matrix-tree theorem）从图论角度证明了不可约时齐马尔可夫网络（irreducible, time-homogeneous Markov network）中占据概率与网络流（network currents）的互线性（mutual linearity）在非平稳态（non-stationary regime）也成立，推导出非平稳响应比（response ratios）的显式组合表达式，并将结果推广至首次击中时间密度（hitting time densities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究在拉普拉斯空间（Laplace space）中建立了平稳态与非平稳态下马尔可夫网络的互线性性质，但非平稳态的响应比缺乏显式组合表达式，且该性质是否可从图论角度统一理解尚不明确。

Method: 采用全子式矩阵-树定理（all-minors matrix-tree theorem），将互线性性质的推导置于图论框架（graph theoretic formulation）中，得到非平稳响应比的显式组合表达式（explicit combinatorial expressions）。

Result: 平稳态结果作为长时间极限（long-time limit）自然导出；短时渐近行为（small-time asymptotics）由底层图中的最短路径距离（minimal path distances）完全决定；互线性性质进一步推广至首次击中时间密度（hitting time densities）。

Conclusion: 互线性性质具有统一的图论基础，非平稳响应比可由组合方式显式表达，且该性质可扩展至首次击中时间密度等更广泛的量。

Abstract: For irreducible, time-homogeneous Markov networks, mutual linearity has recently been established for both occupation probabilities and network currents in the stationary regime as well as in the non-stationary regime in Laplace space. The derivation of this property for the stationary distribution utilized the Markov-chain tree theorem, which also allows for an explicit combinatorial expression of the response ratios under variation of a single transition rate. The extension of this result was proven at the trajectory level by employing the Doob-Meyer decomposition. By employing the all-minors matrix-tree theorem, we show that this property also follows from a graph theoretic formulation and derive explicit combinatorial expressions for the non-stationary response ratios. The stationary result follows as the long-time limit and we also show that the small-time asymptotics are entirely determined by minimal path distances in the underlying graph. Finally we use the graph theoretic approach to prove that mutual linearity also extends to hitting time densities.

</details>


### [98] [Activated random walk exhibits self-organized criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00207)
*Christopher Hoffman,Tobias Johnson,Matthew Junge,Josh Meisel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文首次从数学上证明了1维激活随机游走模型（activated random walk model）能快速混合到具有幂律雪崩（power-law avalanches）的平稳态，且其极限临界密度等于固定能量版本的临界值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自组织临界性（self-organized criticality）理论已提出五十年，但从未有数学模型被严格证明能展现其假定的临界行为；已有的阿贝尔沙堆模型（abelian sandpile model）因混合缓慢而表现出非普适行为（nonuniversal behavior），亟需一个可证明的严格例子。

Method: 论文以1维激活随机游走模型为研究对象，通过数学证明的方法，分析该模型在固定能量版本（fixed-energy model）下的相变临界点，进而证明其自组织版本能快速混合（mix quickly）并收敛到具有幂律雪崩的平稳态。

Result: 1维激活随机游走模型快速混合到平稳态；该平稳态产生幂律雪崩；其极限临界密度恰好等于固定能量版本的临界值。

Conclusion: 该结果为同类自组织临界性理论的严格数学证明开创了先例，支持了Dickman等人关于自组织临界态与固定能量模型临界态等价的核心假说。

Abstract: To explain the ubiquity of power laws and fractals in nature, Bak, Tang, and Wiesenfeld formulated simple conditions for a system to self-organize into a critical state. Dickman, Muñoz, Vespignani, and Zapperi postulated that the self-organized critical state matches the critical state in corresponding fixed-energy models undergoing traditional phase transitions. Although the theory has been applied broadly over the past five decades, no mathematical model has been proven to exhibit the conjectured behavior. Indeed, the originally proposed abelian sandpile model displays nonuniversal behavior stemming from its slow mixing. Marking the first result of its kind, we prove that the 1-d activated random walk model mixes quickly into a stationary state with power-law avalanches and limiting critical density that equals the critical value for the fixed-energy version.

### [99] [Fixed points and crossovers for the hysteresis scaling of dynamic mean-field models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00567)
*Jiapeng Yang,Fan Zhong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究发现一阶相变（first-order phase transitions）在不同驱动速率和噪声条件下呈现出多种普适类（universality classes），并通过重整化群（renormalization group）理论确认其受不同不动点（fixed points）控制的标度行为，数值结果验证了完整曲线塌缩（curve collapse）的普适标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究显示一阶相变中存在受三次不动点（cubic fixed point）控制的普适标度行为，但动态平均场四次模型（dynamic mean-field quartic model）中磁滞（hysteresis）现象在不同驱动速率下展现出新的标度指数，这促使研究者系统探究驱动速率和噪声对一阶相变普适类的影响。

Method: 基于重整化群理论（renormalization group theory）进行系统的标度分析（scaling analysis），研究平均场四次模型中不同驱动速率和有无噪声条件下的一阶相变行为，并利用数值模拟验证理论预测的完整曲线塌缩（full curve collapse）及不同不动点之间的交叉行为（crossovers）。

Result: 发现大驱动速率下出现了源于临界现象（critical phenomena）的新指数；同一平均场模型根据驱动速率大小和噪声存在与否，表现出多个不同的普适类，每个普适类具有由对应不动点决定的确定普适标度指数。

Conclusion: 该研究进一步确认了一阶相变中存在普适标度行为，揭示了不同不动点之间的交叉以及完整曲线塌缩的标度律，拓展了对一阶相变普适类的理解。

Abstract: Phase transitions are divided into first-order phase transitions and continuous ones in current classification. While the latter shows striking phenomena of scaling and universality, the former is generically characterized by discontinuous jumps in extensive variables and pronounced hysteresis. Recent studies have demonstrated universal scaling behavior controlled by a cubic fixed point in first-order phase transitions. However, more recent investigations into the hysteresis in a dynamic mean-field quartic model driven through its first-order phase transitions have revealed new scaling exponents for different driving rates. Here, we discover a new exponent for large driving rates arising surprisingly from critical phenomena and show that, depending on the magnitude of the driving rates and on the absence or presence of noise, the same mean-field model remarkably exhibits several universality classes with definite universal scaling exponents governed by their corresponding fixed points through a systematic scaling analysis based on renormalization group theory. The theories and their various crossovers between different fixed points along with complete universal scaling of full curve collapse are verified by numerical results. This further confirms universal scaling in first-order phase transitions.

</details>

### [101] [Renormalized entropy production for optimal transport in jump processes: Make conservative forces optimal again](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00656)
*Andreas Dechant,Jann van der Meer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对离散状态空间中的跳跃过程（jump processes），证明保守力（conservative forces）虽不能最小化熵产生（entropy production），但可唯一地最小化一种称为重整化熵产生（renormalized entropy production）的新量，并通过数值算例加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续空间扩散过程中保守力与熵产生的最小化之间存在明确联系，但这一关系在离散状态空间的跳跃过程中不成立。论文旨在揭示离散情形下保守力的优化角色，并定义一种新的熵产生量来建立该联系。

Method: 通过理论推导定义重整化熵产生这一新量，并证明保守力是其唯一的最小化元；同时，对比该量与标准熵产生在有限时间优化问题中的概念与物理差异，辅以数值算例进行说明。

Result: 对于离散状态空间中的跳跃过程，尽管保守力不最小化标准熵产生，但保守力唯一地最小化重整化熵产生。非保守力在远离平衡且存在高能垒时对熵产生最小化的作用更显著。

Conclusion: 重整化熵产生是一种与标准熵产生具有共享性质但又存在关键区别的量，保守力在这种新的优化框架下再次获得了唯一的最优地位。

Abstract: For continuous-space diffusion processes, there is a strong connection between conservative forces and entropy production. For a given time evolution of the system's state, the entropy production is minimized when the system is driven by a unique conservative force. However, this relation does not extend to jump processes on a discrete state space. In this case, the forces that minimize the entropy production are generally nonconservative, this effect is more pronounced far from equilibrium in the presence of high energy barriers. Here we show that, while conservative forces do not minimize the entropy production for a given time evolution, they are nevertheless uniquely characterized as the minimizer of a quantity we dub the renormalized entropy production. This work explores the properties this quantity shares with entropy production as well as crucial differences between them. We also discuss the conceptual and physical differences between the corresponding optimization problems in finite time. Our theoretical calculations are illustrated with explicit numerical examples.

</details>


### [102] [Reconstruction of spin structures from topological charge distributions via generative neural network systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00732)
*Kyra H. M. Klos,Jan Disselhoff,Michael Wand,Karin Everschor-Sitte,Friederike Schmid*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过将物理约束和傅里叶空间信息引入Wasserstein生成对抗网络，提出一种能够根据指定的宏观模式与热力学参数生成微观自旋构型的生成模型。以二维XY模型为测试案例，该模型在Kosterlitz-Thouless相变温度以下准确复现了磁化率、磁化强度、螺旋模量和自旋-自旋关联等物理量，但在比热方面存在偏差；拓扑数据分析进一步揭示了近临界温度下常规关联函数无法捕捉的全局自旋关联结构差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域拓扑缺陷（localized topological defects）天然具有多尺度特性：其微观构型依赖于具体物理系统，而拓扑特征与相互作用可在宏观尺度上用粒子表示（particle representation）描述。然而，确定特定缺陷模式对应的物理性质往往需要底层微观结构信息。现有方法难以同时兼顾宏观模式与微观构型的一致性。

Method: 本文将物理约束（physical constraints）和傅里叶空间信息（Fourier-space information）引入Wasserstein生成对抗网络（Wasserstein generative adversarial neural network, WGAN），构建了一个能够生成与指定宏观模式和热力学参数一致的微观自旋构型的生成模型。以二维XY模型（two-dimensional XY model）为测试案例，该模型中涡旋-反涡旋对（vortex-antivortex pairs）充当长程相互作用的缺陷。

Result: 在Kosterlitz-Thouless相变（Kosterlitz-Thouless transition）温度以下的广泛温度范围内，模型生成的自旋构型能够准确复现磁化强度（magnetization）、磁化率（susceptibility）、螺旋模量（helicity modulus）和自旋-自旋关联（spin-spin correlations）。但比热（specific heat）的复现存在偏差，表明模型在高阶能量涨落（higher order energy fluctuations）的再现方面存在局限性。基于拓扑数据分析（topological data analysis）的补充分析揭示了近临界温度下全局自旋关联结构（global spin-correlation structures）的细微差异，这些差异是常规关联函数无法体现的。

Conclusion: 本文结果展示了生成式方法（generative approaches）用于缺陷主导自旋系统（defect-dominated spin systems）多尺度研究的潜力与当前局限，同时强调了拓扑方法（topological methods）作为表征临界行为（critical behavior）工具的独特价值。

Abstract: Localized topological defects inherently possess a multiscale character. While their microstructure configuration depends on the specific physical system, their topological features and mutual interactions can be described on the macroscale in terms of a particle representation. However, determining the physical properties associated with a given defect pattern often requires knowledge of the underlying microscopic structure. In this work, we extend a Wasserstein generative adversarial neural network by incorporating physical constraints and Fourier-space information to generate microscopic spin configurations consistent with prescribed macroscopic patterns and thermodynamic parameters. Using the two-dimensional XY model as a test case, where vortex-antivortex pairs act as long-range interacting defects, we show that the model generates spin configurations that accurately reproduce magnetization, susceptibility, helicity modulus, and spin-spin correlations over a wide range of temperatures below the Kosterlitz-Thouless transition. At the same time, deviations in the specific heat reveal limitations in reproducing higher order energy fluctuations. A complementary analysis based on topological data analysis uncovers subtle differences in global spin-correlation structures at near critical temperatures that are not apparent from conventional correlation functions alone. These results demonstrate both the promise and current limitations of generative approaches for multiscale studies of defect-dominated spin systems and at the same time highlight topological methods as valuable tools for characterizing critical behavior.

</details>

### [103] [Dilute Zn alloying in biodegradable Mg wires: microstructure, mechanical performance, and degradation behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00221)
*Jiří Ryjáček,Leonard Hlodák,Jiří Liška,Jan Pinc,Tomáš Herma,Karel Tesař*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了Zn含量低于室温固溶度极限的稀Mg-Zn合金线材，发现所有成分均能获得细小等轴再结晶晶粒（5.0–5.9 μm）及良好的拉伸性能（抗拉强度246–256 MPa，延伸率23–28%），其中Zn含量对力学性能影响有限，但弯曲行为主要由挤压织构控制，且不同腐蚀介质中降解行为差异显著，表明稀Mg-Zn线材是可吸收骨固定器件的简单材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀Mg-Zn线材在可降解小型骨固定器件领域具有重要应用前景，但Zn含量（尤其低于室温固溶度极限）对加工态细线材微观组织、力学性能和降解行为的系统影响尚不明确，亟需建立成分–工艺–性能的关联。

Method: 制备Mg-0.4Zn、Mg-0.6Zn、Mg-0.8Zn和Mg-1.5Zn四种合金，通过单步直接热挤压（single-step direct hot extrusion）加工为细线材，并采用关联显微组织分析、拉伸测试、弯曲实验及体外降解实验进行综合表征。

Result: 所有合金均获得完全再结晶的等轴细晶组织，晶粒尺寸5.0–5.9 μm；抗拉强度246–256 MPa，延伸率23–28%。Zn含量对晶粒尺寸和拉伸性能影响有限，但低Zn合金出现明显的尖锐屈服点。弯曲行为主要由挤压织构控制，通过孪生（twinning）与去孪生（detwinning）实现可逆塑性。模拟体液（simulated body fluid）中7天内即发生快速局部降解并丧失力学完整性，而DMEM基培养基更接近预期的体内响应。

Conclusion: 稀Mg-Zn线材在较宽Zn含量范围内保持一致的微观组织和力学性能，且腐蚀介质选择对降解评估结果影响显著，该合金体系可作为未来可吸收骨固定器件开发的简便材料平台。

Abstract: Dilute Mg-Zn wires are of great interest for biodegradable small-bone fixation, as magnesium degradation can support bone-related processes, while low zinc additions may provide biological benefits without compromising biocompatibility. In this work, the influence of Zn content below the room-temperature solubility limit was assessed in Mg-Zn wires intended for resorbable implant applications. Mg-0.4Zn, Mg-0.6Zn, Mg-0.8Zn, and Mg-1.5Zn alloys were processed by single-step direct hot extrusion into thin wires and characterized by correlative microstructural analysis, tensile testing, bending experiments, and in vitro degradation. All compositions achieved a recrystallized fine equiaxed grain size of 5.0-5.9 um and exhibited ultimate tensile strengths of 246-256 MPa with elongations of 23-28 %. In these thin wires, Zn content had only a limited effect on grain size, tensile properties, and bending behavior, although lower-Zn alloys showed a pronounced sharp yield point. Bending was governed mainly by extrusion texture and preserved reversible plasticity through twinning and detwinning. Simulated body fluid caused rapid localized degradation and loss of mechanical integrity within 7 days, while the biologically more relevant DMEM-based medium better reflected the expected in vivo response. Together, these findings support dilute Mg-Zn wires as a simple material platform for the development of future resorbable bone fixation devices.

</details>


### [104] [Tailoring Mechanical Properties of Germanium Anodes via Metal Incorporation for Improved Cycle Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00304)
*Koki Nozawa,Noriyuki Saitoh,Noriko Yoshizawa,Takashi Suemasu,Kaoru Toko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过微量金属元素掺杂（尤其是Yb）来软化锗（Ge）负极材料、抑制锂化损伤，从而将循环寿命延长约三倍的材料本征策略。该研究建立了一个以力学柔顺性（mechanical compliance）而非体积变化抑制为核心的高容量合金负极设计新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高容量锂离子电池负极（如Ge）的长期稳定性（long-term stability）仍是关键难题。现有策略多聚焦于抑制体积变化，但效果有限，亟需新的设计思路。

Method: 系统研究了多种微量金属元素掺杂对Ge负极的影响，利用结构分析（structural analysis）与电化学分析（electrochemical analysis）表征循环稳定性与容量，并通过纳米压痕测量（nanoindentation）定量评估掺杂原子尺寸与薄膜硬度（film hardness）的关系。

Result: 原子尺寸较大的掺杂元素（尤其是Yb）可显著提升Ge负极的循环稳定性，且不牺牲初始容量；适当Yb掺杂使负极寿命延长约三倍。纳米压痕测量显示，掺杂原子尺寸与薄膜硬度呈强负相关。Yb掺杂在高倍率下会降低倍率性能（rate capability）。

Conclusion: 循环寿命的改善源于Ge负极的机械软化（mechanical softening），从而抑制锂化诱导的裂纹和分层。该结果将设计策略从“抑制体积变化”转向“提升力学柔顺性”，为通过原子尺度力学控制（atomic-scale mechanical control）稳定高容量合金负极提供了新框架。

Abstract: Achieving long-term stability in high-capacity lithium-ion battery anodes remains a critical challenge. In this study, we present a materials-intrinsic strategy for extending the cycle life of Ge, a promising next-generation anode material, through trace doping with metal elements. We systematically investigated the effects of small additions of various metals and found that elements with large atomic size, particularly Yb, markedly improved the cycling stability without sacrificing the initial capacity, while appropriate Yb doping enhanced the anode lifetime by approximately a factor of three. Structural and electrochemical analyses revealed that this improvement originates from mechanical softening of the Ge anode, which suppresses lithiation-induced damage such as cracking and delamination. Nanoindentation measurements further showed a strong negative correlation between dopant atomic size and film hardness, establishing anode softening as a new design principle for damage-tolerant electrodes. Although Yb doping reduced the rate capability at high C-rates, the present results demonstrate a clear shift in design strategy from volume-change suppression to mechanical compliance. These findings provide a useful framework for stabilizing high-capacity alloy anodes through atomic-scale mechanical control.

</details>


### [105] [Beyond Structure: Revolutionising Materials Discovery via AI-Driven Synthesis Protocol-Property Relationships](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00313)
*Guillaume Lambard*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出当前人工智能驱动材料发现的结构中心范式（structure-centric paradigm）面临可合成性鸿沟（synthesizability gap）这一关键瓶颈，主张转向以合成为优先（synthesis-first）的新范式，将可执行的合成协议（synthesis protocols）而非仅原子构型作为主要设计变量，并基于三支柱路线图推动可重复、数据优先的材料发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前以结构为中心（structure-centric）的AI材料发现方法已产出大量候选结构，但无法跨越可合成性鸿沟（synthesizability gap），即理论预测的结构难以在实际实验中被合成出来。作者认为，这一瓶颈的根本原因在于合成过程未被纳入设计变量，因此需要范式转换。

Method: 提出一个三支柱（three pillars）路线图：(i) 将合成流程表示为机器可读协议（machine-readable protocols）；(ii) 部署生成式和逆向设计模型（generative and inverse-design models），提出可执行的反应路径和配方；(iii) 整合闭环优化（closed-loop optimisation），根据实验现实和可持续性约束不断优化协议。该体系基于从协议P到结构X再到性质y的因果骨架（causal backbone） P→X→y。

Result: 本文是一篇观点性（perspective）论文，未提供新的实验结果，而是系统性地阐述了方法论构建模块（methodological building blocks）、标准需求（standards needs）及自驱动实验室（self-driving laboratory, SDL）集成策略，以加速可重复、数据优先（data-first）的材料发现。

Conclusion: 要弥合可合成性鸿沟，必须从结构中心范式转向合成为优先范式，将合成协议作为核心设计变量。通过机器可读协议、生成式设计与闭环优化三支柱，并结合自驱动实验室（SDL）的集成策略，有望实现更高效、可重复且可持续的材料发现流程。

Abstract: The current structure-centric paradigm in artificial intelligence (AI)-driven materials discovery, despite delivering thousands of candidate structures, is stalling at a critical barrier: the synthesizability gap. We argue that closing this gap demands a pivot to a synthesis-first paradigm in which executable synthesis protocols, not just atomic configurations, are treated as primary design variables. We outline a roadmap built on three pillars: (i) representing synthesis procedures as machine-readable protocols, (ii) deploying generative and inverse-design models to propose actionable reaction pathways and recipes, and (iii) integrating closed-loop optimisation to refine protocols against experimental realities and sustainability constraints. Framed in terms of the causal backbone P->X->y from protocol P to structure X and properties y, this perspective sets out methodological building blocks, standards needs and self-driving laboratory (SDL) integration strategies to accelerate reproducible, data-first materials discovery.

</details>


### [106] [Kinetically Arrested Twin-Domain State in Formamidinium Lead Iodide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00427)
*Xia Liang,Milos Dubajic,Zezhu Zeng,Yang Lu,Johan Klarbring,Samuel D. Stranks,Aron Walsh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文结合大规模分子动力学与基于密度泛函理论精度的机器学习力场，揭示了杂化卤化物钙钛矿FAPbI₃中从有序到动力学冻结的复杂结构相变，并指出有机阳离子的取向动力学通过热历史选择宏观结构与电子性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杂化卤化物钙钛矿（hybrid lead halide perovskites）中平均晶体学对称性、局域结构无序与A位取向动力学之间存在微妙的相互作用，导致反常的振动与电子行为，但其跨介观尺度的结构动力学机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）结合基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）精度的机器学习力场（machine learning force field），对FAPbI₃进行跨介观尺度的结构动力学模拟。

Result: 识别出FAPbI₃的高温α相（动态局域有序+关联倾斜纳米畴）、有序γ相（长程$ a^{+}a^{+}a^{+} $倾斜相干），以及低温~100 K以下的历史依赖γ'态（局域类γ纳米区域被尖锐孪晶界分隔）；该低温无序态并非独立体相多晶型，而是由浅倾斜能垒与缓慢FA重取向共同选择的动力学阻滞亚稳态孪晶畴网络。

Conclusion: 该结构图景统一解释了FAPbI₃低温行为的长期争议，表明有机阳离子通过其重取向动力学主动选择宏观结构与电子响应，使热历史（thermal history）与组分并列为决定结构及光电性质的关键因素。

Abstract: Hybrid lead halide perovskites exhibit a delicate interplay between average crystallographic symmetry, local structural disorder and A-site orientational dynamics, giving rise to unusual vibrational and electronic behaviour. Here, we combine large-scale molecular dynamics with a density-functional-theory-accurate machine learning force field to resolve the structural dynamics of perovskites across mesoscopic length scales. In formamidinium lead iodide FAPbI$_{3}$, we identify a high-temperature $α$ phase with dynamic local order and correlated tilt nanodomains, an ordered $γ$ phase with long-range $a^{+}a^{+}a^{+}$ tilt coherence, and, below $\sim$100~K, a history-dependent $γ'$ state consisting of locally $γ$-like nanoscale regions separated by sharp twin-like boundaries. This low-temperature disordered state is not a distinct bulk polymorph, but a kinetically arrested metastable twin-domain network selected by the interplay between shallow tilt energetics and slowing FA reorientation. This picture provides a consistent explanation for the low-temperature diffuse scattering features observed experimentally, and accounts for the broadened low-energy vibrational response found in the simulations. Furthermore, this unique structural landscape imprints a spatially varying electronic disorder that directly impacts macroscopic optoelectronic properties, evidenced by an anomalous increase in the Urbach energy at low temperatures. Our results reconcile the debated low-temperature behaviour of FAPbI$_{3}$ in terms of competition between ordered and arrested structural states, and show more broadly that in hybrid perovskites the organic cation can actively select the macroscopic structural and electronic response through its reorientation kinetics, placing thermal history on equal footing with composition as a determinant of structural and optoelectronic properties.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用溅射法结合快速热退火（rapid thermal annealing, RTA）在Si(111)衬底上原位形成厚度约0.5 nm的亚纳米级硅化物模板，后续通过金属有机化学气相沉积（metalorganic chemical vapor deposition, MOCVD）进行GaN薄膜的再生长。

Conclusion: 该策略在可扩展、低成本制备与器件级垂直性能之间成功搭建了桥梁，为实现高性能垂直GaN器件提供了新路径。

Abstract: While vertical GaN-on-silicon architectures promise a transformative leap in cost-effective power electronics and high-resolution micro-LEDs, their deployment remains bottlenecked by the high electrical resistance of conventional epitaxial buffer layers. Here, a universal and straightforward sputtering-based strategy is presented to realize high quality GaN epitaxial films on Si(111) substrates characterized by exceptionally low vertical resistance, ohmic behavior, and robust thermal stability. This technique centers on the in-situ formation of a sub nanometer (0.5 nm) silicide-based template via rapid thermal annealing method demonstrating unprecedented versatility across 25 different metallic species. Scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) reveals that a unique amorphous like interlayer (AL-IL) effectively accommodates lattice mismatch and relaxes epitaxial strain. These AL-IL templates further serve as high performance platforms for metalorganic chemical vapor deposition (MOCVD) overgrowth, successfully bridging the gap between scalable, low-cost fabrication and device-grade vertical performance.

### [109] [An Unsupervised Machine Learning-based Framework for Wafer Scale Variability Analysis and Performance Prediction of Ferroelectric Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 Thin Film Capacitors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00544)
*Anika Anu,Sayani Majumdar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对铁电Hf0.5Zr0.5O2电容器（ferroelectric HZO capacitors）因结晶动力学敏感性导致的器件间（device-to-device, D2D）性能非均匀性问题，提出了一种基于无监督机器学习（unsupervised machine learning）的框架，利用主成分分析（Principal Component Analysis, PCA）和K-Means聚类分析芯片内D2D性能变化，实现了对“未见”芯片性能的高效预测，平均绝对百分比误差（Mean Absolute Percentage Error, MAPE）在5-10%之间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体芯片高良率制造面临工艺引起的性能可变性（performance variability）这一重大障碍，而随着人工智能（Artificial Intelligence, AI）工作负载激增，对非易失性及计算存储器的需求呈指数级增长。铁电Hf0.5Zr0.5O2虽因CMOS后端工艺（back-end-of-line, BEOL）兼容性、可扩展性和高性能成为嵌入式非易失性存储器的有力候选，但其敏感的结晶动力学（crystallization kinetics）导致显著的器件间非均匀性（D2D non-uniformity），进而引发晶圆尺度上的性能不可预测性。

Method: 提出了一种无监督机器学习框架，利用主成分分析（PCA）和K-Means聚类分析HZO电容器中D2D性能变化；基于来自多个芯片的数据，构建了超越传统描述性统计的预测性“虚拟计量（Virtual Metrology）”方法，依据剩余极化（remanent polarization, Pr）和矫顽电压（coercive voltage, Vc）等关键参数划分性能类别。

Result: 该方法能准确预测未经测试芯片的器件性能，平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE）在5-10%的较低范围内；分析进一步扩展至比较整个晶圆上不同芯片之间的均匀性。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为实现加速良率提升（yield improvement）和减少计量开销（metrology overhead）提供了一条稳健的路径。

Abstract: Fabrication process-induced performance variability remains a formidable barrier in the high-volume manufacturing of semiconductor chips. With skyrocketing Artificial Intelligence (AI) workload, demand for non-volatile and computational memories is growing exponentially. As embedded non-volatile memory, ferroelectric Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 emerged as a strong candidate due to their CMOS back-end-of-line (BEOL) compatibility, scalability and high performance. However, their sensitive crystallization kinetics leads to significant device-to-device (D2D) non-uniformity leading to unpredictability of performance over wafer scale. In this work, we demonstrate unsupervised machine learning can analyze intra-die D2D variations and predict performance of "unseen" dies efficiently. We present a framework utilizing Principal Component Analysis (PCA) and K-Means clustering to analyze D2D performance variations in HZO capacitors and building on data from multiple dies, we move beyond traditional descriptive statistics to a predictive "Virtual Metrology" approach that separates performance categories, defined by key parameters like remanent polarization (Pr) and coercive voltage (Vc). The analysis further extends to comparing uniformity across different dies across the wafer showing the proposed methodology can accurately predict device performance on untested dies with a low Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE) in the range of 5-10%, suggesting a robust path for accelerated yield improvement and reduced metrology overhead.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 合成了cis-[Cd(Tz)$_2$(py)$_2$]配合物；采用红外（IR）和拉曼（Raman）光谱分析配位诱导的结构与电子扰动；利用Hirshfeld表面分析晶体堆积中的分子间相互作用；通过固态紫外-可见（UV-Vis）光谱测定吸收和光学带隙；使用光致发光（PL）光谱和色度坐标（CIE）评估发光特性。

Conclusion: 配合物cis-[Cd(Tz)$_2$(py)$_2$]的发光主要源于配体中心的π→π*和n→π*跃迁，Cd(II)的d$^{10}$电子构型抑制了金属中心和电荷转移过程，使其成为红光光电器件（red-emitting optoelectronic applications）的候选材料。

Abstract: Organic--inorganic complexes are promising materials for light-emitting applications. Here, we report a new organometallic complex, cis-[Cd(Tz)$_2$(py)$_2$], featuring a distorted octahedral Cd(II) coordination environment. IR and Raman spectroscopy reveal pronounced coordination-induced changes, particularly in the Raman response of the triazene moiety, indicating electronic and structural perturbation upon Cd(II) complexation. Hirshfeld surface analysis shows that the crystal packing is mainly governed by H$\cdots$H, O$\cdots$H/H$\cdots$O, and C$\cdots$H/H$\cdots$C contacts, whereas $π$--$π$ stacking interactions contribute modestly. Solid-state UV--Vis spectroscopy reveals broad absorption from $\sim$700 to 200 nm and a direct optical band gap of 1.83 eV, indicating semiconductor-like behavior. Photoluminescence measurements show a broad emission band at 500--850 nm with enhanced red contribution upon coordination. The emission is mainly assigned to ligand-centered transitions ($π\rightarrow π^*$ and $n \rightarrow π^*$), consistent with the $d^{10}$ configuration of Cd(II), which suppresses metal-centered and charge-transfer processes. The CIE chromaticity coordinates confirm warm emission, highlighting the potential of cis-[Cd(Tz)$_2$(py)$_2$] for red-emitting optoelectronic applications.

### [111] [Coordination Engineering of Dual-Atom Catalysts for Overall Water Splitting: Mechanistic Insights from Constant-Potential First-Principles and Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00609)
*Jiahang Li,Suhang Li,Chong Yan,Jiajun Yu,Qinzhuang Liu,Ruo-Ya Wang,Dongwei Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过调控石墨烯负载双原子催化剂（DACs）的配位环境（C/N配位）和双金属组合（Fe、Co、Ni、Cu），构建了228种结构库，结合恒电荷与恒电势密度泛函理论以及质子耦合电子转移（PCET）动力学分析，筛选出24种高活性析氧反应（OER）候选催化剂（以CoNi、CoCu和Co₂为主），其中22种同时表现出高析氢反应（HER）活性；机器学习揭示了配位依赖的结构-性能关系，表明配位工程（coordination engineering）可同时优化OER中间体吸附与HER氢结合强度，为设计高效双功能双原子电催化剂提供了有效策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 析氢反应（HER）和析氧反应（OER）双功能电催化剂的理性设计是实现高效、低成本全解水（overall water splitting）的关键，而配位工程（coordination engineering）在原子级分散过渡金属催化剂中对其催化性能起决定性作用，但如何系统设计兼具双功能活性的配位结构尚待探索。

Method: 以石墨烯负载的双原子催化剂（DACs）（TM1TM2-C6-xNx）为模型体系，通过调控C/N配位与双金属组合（Fe、Co、Ni、Cu）构建228种结构库；采用三步筛选策略，结合恒电荷与恒电势密度泛函理论（constant-charge and constant-potential DFT）以及质子耦合电子转移（PCET）动力学分析进行高通量计算筛选；并利用机器学习（machine learning）分析结构-性能关系。

Result: 筛选出24种高活性OER候选催化剂（TM1TM2=CoNi、CoCu、Co₂），其过电位与IrO₂相当，且PCET能垒低于0.40 eV；其中22种同时具备高HER活性。机器学习揭示了清晰的配位依赖型结构-性能关系（coordination-dependent structure-performance relationships）。

Conclusion: 双功能催化活性源于配位工程对OER中间体吸附和HER氢结合强度的同步优化；该工作确立了配位工程作为设计高性能双功能双原子全解水电催化剂的有效策略。

Abstract: The rational design of bifunctional electrocatalysts for the hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) and oxygen evolution reaction (OER) is essential for achieving efficient and cost-effective overall water splitting. Atomically dispersed transition-metal catalysts, including single-atom catalysts and dual-atom catalysts (DACs), have emerged as a prominent class of heterogeneous catalysts, in which coordination engineering plays a decisive role in tuning catalytic performance. Herein, we explore coordination-engineered bifunctional overall water splitting electrocatalysts using graphene-supported DACs (TM1TM2-C6-xNx) as model systems. By tuning C/N coordination and dual-metal combinations (Fe, Co, Ni, and Cu), a library of 228 structures was constructed. A three-step screening strategy, combining constant-charge and constant-potential density functional theory with kinetic analysis of proton-coupled electron transfer (PCET), identifies 24 highly active candidates (TM1TM2 = CoNi, CoCu and Co2) with mixed C/N coordination for OER. These catalysts exhibit overpotentials comparable to that of IrO2 and low PCET barriers (lower than 0.40 eV), among which 22 also show high HER activity. Machine learning reveals clear coordination-dependent structure-performance relationships. Such bifunctionality arises from coordination engineering that enables the simultaneous optimization of OER intermediate adsorption and the hydrogen binding strength for HER. This work establishes coordination engineering as an effective strategy for designing high-performance bifunctional dual-atom electrocatalysts for overall water splitting.

Result: 摘要未提供具体的实验或数值结果，但指出实现该愿景需要整个社区持续的共同承诺，且潜在回报与挑战的规模相匹配。

Conclusion: 该策略旨在从根本上改变当前自主科学的优化范式，通过前期约束设计使新材料从诞生之初就具备产业化资质，从而跨越“死亡之谷”。实现这一目标依赖学界与工业界的长期协同投入。

Abstract: Autonomous science is transforming how we discover materials and chemical systems for advanced energy technologies. However, many initially promising systems never reach deployment. This "valley of death" stems from optimization that prioritizes laboratory metrics over industrial viability. We propose a new strategy: "born-qualified" autonomous development, which embeds manufacturability, cost, and durability constraints from the outset. This approach is enabled by four pillars, including the development of multi-objective metrics, causal models, a modular infrastructure, and embedding manufacturing in the discovery loop. Realizing this vision will require sustained, community-wide commitment, but the potential return on that investment is commensurate with the scale of the challenge.

### [113] [TrueEBSD in MTEX: automatic image matching for correlative microscopy applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00703)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将 TrueEBSD 重新实现为 MTEX 工具箱的插件（add-on），用于图像对齐和空间畸变校正（spatial distortion correction），从而将 EBSD 取向图谱与来自其他成像模式的数据相结合。

Result: 在两个示例案例研究中，通过将 EBSD 图谱与 SEM 图像数据结合，成功实现了 WC-Co 复合材料中 Co 相分数和 WC 邻接度（contiguity）的测量，以及铜多晶中晶界对空洞形成的相对敏感性评估。

Conclusion: TrueEBSD 作为 MTEX 插件，通过空间对齐实现 EBSD 图谱的图像数据增强，使得原本无法从单独 EBSD 图谱或图像分析中获得的定量晶体学测量成为可能。

Abstract: TrueEBSD is an open-source MATLAB program for image alignment and spatial distortion correction of images and electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) maps. We have re-implemented TrueEBSD as an add-on to MTEX, an established toolbox for EBSD data analysis. Spatial alignment enables correlative analysis methods, such as augmenting EBSD orientation maps with data from other imaging modes. The augmented EBSD maps can then be analysed further using MTEX. We demonstrate TrueEBSD on two example case studies: one for measuring Co phase fraction and WC contiguity in a WC-Co composite, and another for determining the relative susceptibility of grain boundaries to void formation in a copper polycrystal. In both examples, the EBSD map was augmented with scanning electron microscopy (SEM) image data. This enabled quantitative crystallographic measurements which would not be possible from analysing the EBSD maps and images separately.

### [114] [Oxygen Vacancies at Dislocation Core Modulate Plasticity in Strontium Titanate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00801)
*Min-Chul Kang,Chunxu Yan,Alexander Frisch,Xufei Fang,Liming Xiong,Lin Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合球差校正扫描透射电子显微镜、电子能量损失谱与原子级分子动力学模拟，以SrTiO3为模型材料，首次直接观察到氧化物中位错核心化学在运动过程中的演化，发现氧空位密度随滑移距离变化，并提出氧空位演化与离子晶体塑性内在耦合的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化物中位错核心化学（dislocation core chemistry）对力学行为和功能性至关重要，但位错运动过程中核心化学的演化尚未被直接观测到，这限制了对其塑性机制的理解。

Method: 以SrTiO3为模型材料，将球差校正扫描透射电子显微镜（aberration-corrected scanning transmission electron microscopy, STEM）与电子能量损失谱（electron energy-loss spectroscopy, EELS）相结合，并辅以原子级分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，关联<110>{1-10}位错核心结构、氧空位密度、电荷态与迁移率。

Result: 机械诱导的位错环呈现解离核心（dissociated cores），其氧空位密度取决于滑移距离：短位错环的刃位错核心出现Ti还原和缺氧，而长位错环的刃型和螺型分量均接近化学计量比。MD模拟表明，扭结辅助的刃位错滑移会在后方留下缺氧痕迹，从而调节刃位错核心内的氧含量。

Conclusion: 位错核心的氧空位演化与离子晶体中的塑性（plasticity）内在耦合，提示了一种在塑性变形氧化物中依赖于氧空位的位错迁移率机制。

Abstract: Dislocation core chemistry in oxides critically influences mechanical behavior and functionality; yet the evolution of core chemistry during the dislocation motion in them has not been directly observed. Here, using SrTiO3 as a model material, we combine aberration-corrected scanning transmission electron microscopy and electron energy-loss spectroscopy with atomic-level molecular dynamics (MD) simulations to correlate the <110>{1-10} dislocation core structure, oxygen vacancy density, charge state, and mobility with each other. We find that the mechanically induced dislocation loops exhibit dissociated cores, whose oxygen vacancy density depends on the gliding distance: short loops are Ti-reduced and oxygen-deficient at the edge dislocation core, whereas longer loops remain close to stoichiometry in both the edge and screw components. MD simulations reveal that kink-assisted edge dislocation glide in SrTiO3 leaves oxygen-deficient trails behind, modulating the oxygen content inside the edge core. These results demonstrate that oxygen-vacancy evolution at the dislocation core intrinsically couples with plasticity in ionic crystals, suggesting a mechanism for oxygen vacancy-dependent dislocation mobility in plastically deformed oxides.

</details>


### [115] [Determination of Density Functional Tight Binding Models for Cerium Allotropes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00802)
*Nir Goldman,Artem Samtsevych,Chiara Panosetti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了针对铈（cerium）的密度泛函紧束缚（Density Functional Tight Binding, DFTB）模型，能够准确预测不同同素异形体的电子能带结构和能量排序。通过全局优化电子约束势（confining potentials），最小化了Kohn-Sham能量的预测误差，并帮助确定了多体排斥能（many-body repulsive energy）。结果表明DFTB能利用极少的密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）数据准确再现复杂的f电子相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发能够准确预测铈（cerium）不同同素异形体的电子能带结构（electronic band structure）和能量排序的密度泛函紧束缚（DFTB）模型。

Method: 通过全局优化（global optimization）电子约束势（confining potentials）来最小化预测的Kohn-Sham能量误差，同时辅助确定多体排斥能（many-body repulsive energy）。

Result: 所开发的DFTB模型能够准确预测铈同素异形体的电子能带结构和能量排序，并成功利用极少的DFT数据复现复杂的f电子相互作用（f-electron interactions）。

Conclusion: DFTB模型具备准确再现复杂f电子相互作用的能力，且可依托最小量的密度泛函理论（DFT）数据实现，为高效计算含f电子的多相材料提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We have developed Density Functional Tight Binding (DFTB) models for cerium that accurately predict both the electronic band structure and energetic ordering of different allotropes. We show that global optimization of the electronic confining potentials minimize the errors in the predicted Kohn-Sham energies while facilitating determination of a many-body repulsive energy. Our results illustrate the ability of DFTB to accurately reproduce complex f-electron interactions for multiple phases while leveraging minimal Density Functional Theory data.
