### [116] [Revealing the origin of XMCD in an altermagnet via three-dimensional control of spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00815)
*Daire Mallon,Zixuan Wu,Jheng-Cyuan Lin,Ruiwen Xie,Bo Zhao,Charles Godfrey,Qing He,Lucia Iglesias,Pierluigi Gargiani,Manuel Valvidares,Peter Bencok,Francesco Maccherozzi,Larissa S. I. Veiga,Paul Steadman,Manuel Bibes,Hongbin Zhang,Paolo G. Radaelli,Hariom Jani*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以g波交变磁体α-Fe₂O₃为例，证明X射线磁圆二色性（XMCD）信号实际上由自旋方向诱导的对称性破缺主导，而非直接反映交变磁性（altermagnetism），并基于局部法拉第张量重建了纳米尺度拓扑自旋织构的矢量图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）是一类新兴的共线反铁磁体，具有非常规的自旋极化电子能带，有望在不依赖自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）的情况下实现新功能。然而，传统用于验证自旋极化的实验信号（如XMCD）本身需要SOC且不自旋空间旋转不变，这引发了对其能否作为交变磁性直接证据的质疑。本文旨在厘清这一关键问题。

Method: 利用g波交变磁体α-Fe₂O₃进行实验研究，分析XMCD信号与自旋方向诱导的对称性破缺之间的关系；引入局域法拉第张量（Faraday tensor）来描述未补偿的自旋-轨道各向异性（spin-orbital anisotropy），并据此重建纳米尺度织构的矢量图。

Result: XMCD信号由自旋方向诱导的对称性破缺精确决定，而非直接源于交变磁性的自旋劈裂；该信号高度各向异性，且与弱磁倾斜（magnetic canting）解耦。基于局域法拉第张量的方法成功应用于α-Fe₂O₃薄膜，重建了包括畴壁（domain wall）和拓扑孤子（topological soliton）在内的完整纳米织构矢量图。

Conclusion: 传统认为的XMCD等自旋极化实验信号并非交变磁性的直接证据，而是由自旋方向诱导的对称性破缺所主导。所提出的基于局域法拉第张量的解析框架可推广至其他交变磁体，并可用于表征纳米尺度拓扑自旋织构，对未来的自旋电子学（spintronics）和磁振子学（magnonics）器件具有重要价值。

Abstract: Altermagnets are an emerging class of collinear antiferromagnets that exhibit unconventional spin-polarised electronic bands, potentially unlocking new functionalities that do not rely on spin-orbit coupling (SOC). Experimental signatures traditionally associated with spin polarisation, like X-ray magnetic circular dichroism (XMCD), are thus being used as a validation of altermagnetism. However, unlike altermagnetic spin-splitting, these responses require SOC and are not invariant under spin-space rotations. This brings into question the extent to which they can be considered direct signatures of altermagnetism. Here, we exploit the g-wave altermagnet $α$-Fe$_{2}$O$_{3}$ to demonstrate that XMCD is governed precisely by the spin-direction-induced symmetry breaking that altermagnetic spin groups are designed to ignore. Strikingly, the XMCD is highly anisotropic and is decoupled from the weak magnetic canting. We show that this anomalous XMCD can be described by on-site Faraday tensors capturing the locally uncompensated spin-orbital anisotropies - a scenario that can be applied to other altermagnets. Leveraging this, we reconstruct complete vectorial maps of nanoscale textures in $α$-Fe$_{2}$O$_{3}$ thin films, including domain walls and topological solitons, which are promising for building future spintronics and magnonics devices.

</details>


<div id='physics.optics'></div>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [117] [Plasmon Induced Delocalized Second-Harmonic Generation Towards Buried-Interface Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00575)
*Alan R. Bowman,Sergejs Boroviks,Omer Can Karaman,Laura M. Herz,Olivier J. F. Martin,Giulia Tagliabue*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过实验在单晶金表面与微结构中直接观察到由表面等离极化激元（surface plasmon polariton, SPP）介导的非局域二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG），信号可从激发点传播至35 µm远，且首次在微米尺度上揭示了两束反向传播SPP相互作用产生二次谐波的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次谐波显微术（second-harmonic generation microscopy）虽能探测界面局域晶体对称性和电场，但存在信号弱、多层体系中各材料信号相互竞争难以解析的问题，亟需一种能够实现宽域多层样品探测的更有效方法。

Method: 采用工业级脉冲激光激发金单晶表面及微结构，利用CMOS相机（无增益、1秒曝光）采集信号；通过分析信号偏振依赖性、远距离传播特性及与反向传播SPP的关联，揭示了非局域二次谐波产生的物理机制。

Result: 实现了距激发点最远35 µm处的二次谐波探测，在无基频光直接照射的原子级平整区域仍能获得信号；发现该信号源于两束反向传播的SPP相互作用，首次在微米尺度上观测到该过程；信号具有与局域二次谐波相同的偏振依赖性，并以准直光束垂直样品表面出射；利用局部电场增强效应，可在低功率条件下快速成像。

Conclusion: 所提出的SPP介导的非局域二次谐波产生机制，实现了仅用单束激发光即对大面积多层样品进行探测，为能源、催化及单颗粒表面传感等领域提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Second-harmonic generation microscopy is a powerful technique capable of probing local crystal symmetries and electric fields at interfaces. However, it often suffers from weak signal strength and is difficult to understand in multilayer systems where many materials can give competing signal contributions. In this work we present direct observation of delocalized, surface plasmon polariton-mediated second-harmonic generation on gold monocrystalline surfaces and structures. We generate second-harmonic light up to 35 um from the excitation spot and, excitingly, we obtain signal from atomically flat surfaces without a fundamental excitation beam present in the same region. We reveal that this process arises from the interaction of two counter-propagating surface plasmon polaritons, which we believe to be the first observation of this process at the microscale. This signal has the same polarisation dependence as localised second-harmonic generation and is emitted in a collimated beam travelling perpendicular to the sample surface. In part due to local electric field enhancements, we were able to observe these signals on a CMOS camera with 1 s exposure and no gain using an industrial-grade pulsed laser. Our results enable wide area multilayer samples to be probed using a single excitation beam, with applications including in energy, catalysis and single particle surface sensing.

</details>


### [118] [Suppressing Plasmonic Heating in Aqueous Environments with Hexagonal Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00587)
*Martina Russo,Roland van der Vegt,Bohai Liu,Sam Beijers,Sara Salera,Guillaume Baffou,Klaas-Jan Tielrooij,Peter Zijlstra*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过有限元模拟和交叉光栅波前显微术（CGM），系统研究了六方氮化硼（hBN）薄片作为散热层对金纳米球等离激元加热的冷却效果，发现温度可降低高达60%，并揭示了厚度依赖的热耗散机制与两种主散热路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 等离激元纳米结构（plasmonic nanostructures）的光学加热效应会降低热敏感应用（如生物传感、纳米光子学、微电子学）的性能，而传统冷却策略在纳米尺度因热输运受限和界面热阻过高而失效，因此亟需引入先进热管理材料。

Method: 采用有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）量化hBN薄片厚度、面内热导率（in-plane thermal conductivity）和界面热导（interfacial thermal conductance）对冷却效率的影响，同时利用交叉光栅波前显微术（cross-grating wavefront microscopy, CGM）进行纳米测温（nanothermometry），实验测量光加热金纳米颗粒周围的温度分布。

Result: hBN可将温度升高幅度较仅用玻璃基底降低高达60%；薄片中热耗散受hBN热容（heat capacity）限制，厚片中则受界面热导限制；存在两种主散热路径：从纳米颗粒直接到hBN，以及从颗粒经由水再到hBN。

Conclusion: 该模拟-实验联合框架为等离激元系统及其他领域提供了通用热管理改进策略，并为将二维材料（2D materials）集成到生物传感器和集成电路等热敏感平台建立了设计指南。

Abstract: Optical heating of plasmonic nanostructures is a critical challenge in nanoscale systems. Although plasmonic effects enable enhanced optical functionalities, the associated temperature rise can degrade performance in heat-sensitive applications such as biosensing, nanophotonics, and microelectronics. Conventional cooling strategies fail at these scales due to limited heat transport and high interfacial thermal resistance, motivating the integration of advanced materials for thermal management. Here, we investigate hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) thin flakes as heat spreaders to mitigate plasmonic heating of gold nanospheres immobilized on hBN deposited on glass and surrounded by water. Using finite-element simulations, we quantify the influence of hBN thickness, in-plane thermal conductivity, and interfacial thermal conductance on cooling efficiency. Complementary experiments employ cross-grating wavefront microscopy (CGM) for nanothermometry to map the temperature around optically heated gold nanoparticles and quantify the cooling effect of hBN. We extend the application of CGM for rapid, non-invasive, and all-optical characterization of non-absorbing 2D materials. Our results reveal a strong thickness dependence, where heat dissipation in thin flakes is limited by the heat capacity of hBN and in thick flakes by interfacial thermal conductance. Including hBN, we obtain a reduction in temperature rise by up to 60% compared to glass. In addition, the presence of two main heat dissipation pathways emerges: a direct one from the nanoparticle to the hBN and an indirect one from the particle via water to the hBN. This combined simulation-experiment framework offers a versatile approach to improve thermal management in plasmonic systems and beyond, establishing design guidelines for integrating 2D materials into thermally sensitive platforms such as biosensors and integrated circuits.

</details>

# physics.data-an [[Back]](#toc)

### [119] [FitED: A User-Centric, Extensible Software Environment for Robust Peak-Profile and General Functional Data Fitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00172)
*Mustafa Mahmoud Aboulsaad*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文介绍 FitED，一个基于 Python 的桌面应用程序，用于一维科学数据的交互式与自动化非线性拟合（nonlinear fitting），集成多种峰型轮廓、自定义函数、背景建模及可视化工具，旨在提高拟合的可复现性与可访问性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从谱学、衍射、光致发光、色谱、显微术及时间分辨测量等实验数据中可靠提取参数，是定量分析的核心需求。现有工具在可及性与参数级控制之间常存在权衡，因此需要一款兼具图形化工作流与数值后端灵活性的非线性拟合软件。

Method: FitED 采用 Python 开发，提供桌面图形用户界面；后端支持高斯（Gaussian）、洛伦兹（Lorentzian）、伪 Voigt（Pseudo-Voigt）及精确面积归一化 Voigt 轮廓，以及用户自定义解析函数（如指数衰减、拉伸指数、饱和曲线、谱学响应函数）。集成文本文件导入、感兴趣区域选择、背景建模、参数边界约束、加权策略、自动预拟合搜索、迭代峰精细化、残差可视化、会话持久化及结构化导出功能。

Result: 软件实现了对常规峰型与任意用户定义函数的拟合支持，并集成了完整的交互式与自动化分析流程，包括预拟合搜索、迭代精化、残差检查及元数据导出。

Conclusion: FitED 兼具数学透明性与实用易用性，旨在使非线性拟合更可复现、更易访问，同时保留经验丰富的研究人员所需的参数级控制能力。

Abstract: Reliable parameter extraction from experimental data is central to quantitative analysis in spectroscopy, diffraction, photoluminescence, chromatography, microscopy, and time-resolved measurements. We present FitED, a Python-based desktop application for interactive and automated nonlinear fitting of one-dimensional scientific data. FitED combines an accessible graphical workflow with a numerical backend capable of fitting both conventional peak profiles and arbitrary user-defined analytical functions. The software supports Gaussian, Lorentzian, Pseudo-Voigt, and exact area-normalized Voigt profiles, together with custom functions such as exponential decays, stretched exponentials, saturation curves, and spectroscopy-specific response functions. It integrates robust text-file import, region-of-interest selection, background modeling, parameter bounds, weighting strategies, automated pre-fit search, iterative peak refinement, residual visualization, session persistence, and structured export of fitted curves, components, reports, and metadata. By combining mathematical transparency with practical usability, FitED aims to make nonlinear fitting more reproducible and accessible while preserving the parameter-level control required by experienced experimental researchers.

</details>
